March 06, 2026

OpenFrontier: General Navigation with Visual-Language Grounded Frontiers

Abstract (English): Open-world navigation requires robots to make decisions in complex everyday environments while adapting to flexible task requirements. Conventional navigation approaches often rely on dense 3D reconstruction and hand-crafted goal metrics, which limits their generalization across tasks and environments. Recent advances in vision--language navigation (VLN) and vision--language--action (VLA) models enable end-to-end policies conditioned on natural language, but typically require interactive training, large-scale data collection, or task-specific fine-tuning with a mobile agent. We formulate navigation as a sparse subgoal identification and reaching problem and observe that providing visual anchoring targets for high-level semantic priors enables highly efficient goal-conditioned navigation. Based on this insight, we select navigation frontiers as semantic anchors and propose OpenFrontier, a training-free navigation framework that seamlessly integrates diverse vision--language prior models. OpenFrontier enables efficient navigation with a lightweight system design, without dense 3D mapping, policy training, or model fine-tuning. We evaluate OpenFrontier across multiple navigation benchmarks and demonstrate strong zero-shot performance, as well as effective real-world deployment on a mobile robot.

摘要（中文）: 开放世界导航要求机器人在复杂的日常环境中做出决策，同时适应灵活的任务需求。传统的导航方法通常依赖于密集的3D重建和手工设计的目标指标，这限制了它们在不同任务和环境中的泛化能力。视觉-语言导航（VLN）和视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型的最新进展使得能够实现以自然语言为条件的端到端策略，但通常需要交互式训练、大规模数据收集，或者使用移动代理进行特定于任务的微调。我们把导航描述为稀疏子目标识别和到达问题，并观察到为高级语义先验提供视觉锚定目标能够实现高效的目标条件导航。基于这一洞察，我们选择导航前沿作为语义锚，并提出OpenFrontier，一个无需训练的导航框架，能够无缝集成各种视觉-语言先验模型。 OpenFrontier能够以轻量级的系统设计实现高效导航，无需密集的3D地图、策略训练或模型微调。我们在多个导航基准上评估了OpenFrontier，并展示了强大的零样本性能，以及在移动机器人上的有效真实世界部署。

TLDR: OpenFrontier is a training-free navigation framework that uses visual-language grounded frontiers as semantic anchors for efficient, zero-shot navigation, enabling deployment on real-world mobile robots without dense 3D mapping or policy training.

简要说明: OpenFrontier是一个无需训练的导航框架，它使用视觉-语言接地的边界作为语义锚点，实现高效的零样本导航，无需密集的3D地图构建或策略训练即可部署在现实世界的移动机器人上。

Authors: Esteban Padilla, Boyang Sun, Marc Pollefeys, Hermann Blum

Critic in the Loop: A Tri-System VLA Framework for Robust Long-Horizon Manipulation

Abstract (English): Balancing high-level semantic reasoning with low-level reactive control remains a core challenge in visual robotic manipulation. While Vision-Language Models (VLMs) excel at cognitive planning, their inference latency precludes real-time execution. Conversely, fast Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models often lack the semantic depth required for complex, long-horizon tasks. To bridge this gap, we introduce Critic in the Loop, an adaptive hierarchical framework driven by dynamic VLM-Expert scheduling. At its core is a bionic Tri-System architecture comprising a VLM brain for global reasoning, a VLA cerebellum for reactive execution, and a lightweight visual Critic. By continuously monitoring the workspace, the Critic dynamically routes control authority. It sustains rapid closed-loop execution via the VLA for routine subtasks, and adaptively triggers the VLM for replanning upon detecting execution anomalies such as task stagnation or failures. Furthermore, our architecture seamlessly integrates human-inspired rules to intuitively break infinite retry loops. This visually-grounded scheduling minimizes expensive VLM queries, while substantially enhancing system robustness and autonomy in out-of-distribution (OOD) scenarios. Comprehensive experiments on challenging, long-horizon manipulation benchmarks reveal that our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance.

摘要（中文）: 在视觉机器人操作中，如何平衡高层语义推理与底层反应式控制仍然是一个核心挑战。尽管视觉-语言模型（VLM）擅长认知规划，但其推理延迟阻碍了实时执行。相反，快速的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型通常缺乏复杂、长时序任务所需的语义深度。为了弥合这一差距，我们引入了循环内的评论家，一个由动态VLM-专家调度驱动的自适应分层框架。其核心是一个仿生三系统架构，包含一个用于全局推理的VLM大脑，一个用于反应式执行的VLA小脑，以及一个轻量级的视觉评论家。通过持续监控工作空间，评论家动态地路由控制权限。对于常规子任务，它通过VLA维持快速闭环执行，并在检测到任务停滞或失败等执行异常时，自适应地触发VLM进行重新规划。此外，我们的架构无缝地集成了受人类启发式规则，以直观地打破无限重试循环。这种视觉驱动的调度最大限度地减少了昂贵的VLM查询，同时显著提高了系统在分布外（OOD）场景中的鲁棒性和自主性。在具有挑战性的长时序操作基准测试上的综合实验表明，我们的方法实现了最先进的性能。

TLDR: This paper presents a "Critic in the Loop" framework using a VLM, VLA, and a visual critic to improve long-horizon robotic manipulation by adaptively switching between high-level planning and low-level reactive control, achieving SOTA results.

简要说明: 这篇论文提出了一个“循环中的批评者”框架，使用VLM、VLA和一个视觉评论家，通过自适应地切换高级规划和低级反应控制来改进长距离机器人操作，并实现了SOTA结果。

Authors: Pengfei Yi, Yingjie Ma, Wenjiang Xu, Yanan Hao, Shuai Gan, Wanting Li, Shanlin Zhong

RoboMME: Benchmarking and Understanding Memory for Robotic Generalist Policies

Abstract (English): Memory is critical for long-horizon and history-dependent robotic manipulation. Such tasks often involve counting repeated actions or manipulating objects that become temporarily occluded. Recent vision-language-action (VLA) models have begun to incorporate memory mechanisms; however, their evaluations remain confined to narrow, non-standardized settings. This limits their systematic understanding, comparison, and progress measurement. To address these challenges, we introduce RoboMME: a large-scale standardized benchmark for evaluating and advancing VLA models in long-horizon, history-dependent scenarios. Our benchmark comprises 16 manipulation tasks constructed under a carefully designed taxonomy that evaluates temporal, spatial, object, and procedural memory. We further develop a suite of 14 memory-augmented VLA variants built on the π0.5 backbone to systematically explore different memory representations across multiple integration strategies. Experimental results show that the effectiveness of memory representations is highly task-dependent, with each design offering distinct advantages and limitations across different tasks. Videos and code can be found at our website https://robomme.github.io.

摘要（中文）: 记忆对于长时程和历史依赖型机器人操作至关重要。这类任务通常涉及重复动作的计数或对临时遮挡物体的操作。近期的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型已经开始结合记忆机制；然而，它们的评估仍然局限于狭窄的、非标准化的环境中。这限制了它们的系统性理解、比较和进度衡量。为了应对这些挑战，我们引入RoboMME：一个大规模标准化基准，用于评估和推进VLA模型在长时程、历史依赖型情景中的性能。我们的基准包含16个操作任务，这些任务是在一个精心设计的分类法下构建的，该分类法评估了时间、空间、物体以及程序性记忆。我们进一步开发了一套基于π0.5主干的14种记忆增强型VLA变体，以系统地探索跨多种集成策略的不同记忆表征。实验结果表明，记忆表征的有效性高度依赖于任务，每种设计在不同任务中都表现出独特的优势和局限性。视频和代码可在我们的网站https://robomme.github.io找到。

TLDR: The paper introduces RoboMME, a standardized benchmark for evaluating memory in vision-language-action models for long-horizon robotic manipulation, and explores the effectiveness of different memory representations across various tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 RoboMME，一个用于评估视觉-语言-动作模型在长程机器人操作中记忆能力的标准化基准，并探讨了不同记忆表征在各种任务中的有效性。

Authors: Yinpei Dai, Hongze Fu, Jayjun Lee, Yuejiang Liu, Haoran Zhang, Jianing Yang, Chelsea Finn, Nima Fazeli, Joyce Chai

RoboCasa365: A Large-Scale Simulation Framework for Training and Benchmarking Generalist Robots

Abstract (English): Recent advances in robot learning have accelerated progress toward generalist robots that can perform everyday tasks in human environments. Yet it remains difficult to gauge how close we are to this vision. The field lacks a reproducible, large-scale benchmark for systematic evaluation. To fill this gap, we present RoboCasa365, a comprehensive simulation benchmark for household mobile manipulation. Built on the RoboCasa platform, RoboCasa365 introduces 365 everyday tasks across 2,500 diverse kitchen environments, with over 600 hours of human demonstration data and over 1600 hours of synthetically generated demonstration data -- making it one of the most diverse and large-scale resources for studying generalist policies. RoboCasa365 is designed to support systematic evaluations for different problem settings, including multi-task learning, robot foundation model training, and lifelong learning. We conduct extensive experiments on this benchmark with state-of-the-art methods and analyze the impacts of task diversity, dataset scale, and environment variation on generalization. Our results provide new insights into what factors most strongly affect the performance of generalist robots and inform strategies for future progress in the field.

摘要（中文）: 机器人学习的最新进展加速了通用机器人方向的发展，这种机器人能够在人类环境中执行日常任务。然而，衡量我们离这个愿景有多近仍然很困难。该领域缺乏一个可复现的大规模基准，用于系统性评估。为了填补这一空白，我们提出了RoboCasa365，这是一个用于家庭移动操作的综合模拟基准。RoboCasa365建立在RoboCasa平台之上，引入了2,500个不同厨房环境下的365个日常任务，包含超过600小时的人类演示数据和超过1600小时的合成生成演示数据——使其成为研究通用策略的最多样化和大规模的资源之一。RoboCasa365旨在支持对不同问题设置的系统性评估，包括多任务学习、机器人基础模型训练和终身学习。我们使用最先进的方法，在这个基准上进行了广泛的实验，并分析了任务多样性、数据集规模和环境变化对泛化的影响。我们的结果为哪些因素对通用机器人的性能影响最大提供了新的见解，并为该领域未来的发展战略提供了信息。

TLDR: The paper introduces RoboCasa365, a large-scale simulation benchmark for training and evaluating generalist robots in realistic household environments, featuring diverse tasks, environments, and demonstration data.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了RoboCasa365，一个大规模模拟基准，用于在真实的家庭环境中训练和评估通用机器人，具有多样化的任务、环境和演示数据。

Authors: Soroush Nasiriany, Sepehr Nasiriany, Abhiram Maddukuri, Yuke Zhu

WebChain: A Large-Scale Human-Annotated Dataset of Real-World Web Interaction Traces

Abstract (English): We introduce WebChain, the largest open-source dataset of human-annotated trajectories on real-world websites, designed to accelerate reproducible research in web agents. It contains 31,725 trajectories and 318k steps, featuring a core Triple Alignment of visual, structural, and action data to provide rich, multi-modal supervision. The data is collected via a scalable pipeline that ensures coverage of complex, high-value tasks often missed by synthetic methods. Leveraging this dataset, we propose a Dual Mid-Training recipe that decouples spatial grounding from planning, achieving state-of-the-art performance on our proposed WebChainBench and other public GUI benchmarks. Our work provides the data and insights necessary to build and rigorously evaluate the next generation of scalable web agents.

摘要（中文）: 我们推出了WebChain，这是最大的开源人类标注的真实网站轨迹数据集，旨在加速Web代理中可复现的研究。它包含31,725条轨迹和31.8万个步骤，具有视觉、结构和行动数据的核心三重对齐，以提供丰富的多模态监督。该数据是通过可扩展的流水线收集的，确保了对合成方法经常遗漏的复杂、高价值任务的覆盖。利用该数据集，我们提出了一种双重中间训练策略，将空间定位与规划分离，从而在我们的WebChainBench以及其他公共GUI基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。我们的工作提供了构建和严格评估下一代可扩展Web代理所需的数据和见解。

TLDR: The paper introduces WebChain, a large-scale, human-annotated web interaction dataset with visual, structural, and action data, and proposes a dual mid-training recipe achieving SOTA performance on web agent benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了WebChain，一个大规模的人工标注网络交互数据集，包含视觉、结构和动作数据，并提出了一种双重中间训练方法，在网络代理基准测试中实现了SOTA性能。

Authors: Sicheng Fan, Rui Wan, Yifei Leng, Gaoning Liang, Li Ling, Yanyi Shang, Dehan Kong

EvoTool: Self-Evolving Tool-Use Policy Optimization in LLM Agents via Blame-Aware Mutation and Diversity-Aware Selection

Abstract (English): LLM-based agents depend on effective tool-use policies to solve complex tasks, yet optimizing these policies remains challenging due to delayed supervision and the difficulty of credit assignment in long-horizon trajectories. Existing optimization approaches tend to be either monolithic, which are prone to entangling behaviors, or single-aspect, which ignore cross-module error propagation. To address these limitations, we propose EvoTool, a self-evolving framework that optimizes a modular tool-use policy via a gradient-free evolutionary paradigm. EvoTool decomposes agent's tool-use policy into four modules, including Planner, Selector, Caller, and Synthesizer, and iteratively improves them in a self-improving loop through three novel mechanisms. Trajectory-Grounded Blame Attribution uses diagnostic traces to localize failures to a specific module. Feedback-Guided Targeted Mutation then edits only that module via natural-language critique. Diversity-Aware Population Selection preserves complementary candidates to ensure solution diversity. Across four benchmarks, EvoTool outperforms strong baselines by over 5 points on both GPT-4.1 and Qwen3-8B, while achieving superior efficiency and transferability. The code will be released once paper is accepted.

摘要（中文）: 基于LLM的智能体依赖于有效的工具使用策略来解决复杂任务，然而，由于监督延迟和长程轨迹中信用分配的困难，优化这些策略仍然具有挑战性。现有的优化方法往往是单片的，容易纠缠行为，或者是单方面的，忽略了跨模块的误差传播。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了EvoTool，一个自演化框架，通过无梯度演化范式优化模块化的工具使用策略。EvoTool将智能体的工具使用策略分解为四个模块，包括规划器（Planner）、选择器（Selector）、调用器（Caller）和合成器（Synthesizer），并通过三种新颖机制在自改进循环中迭代改进它们。轨迹溯源故障归因使用诊断追踪将故障定位到特定模块。然后，反馈引导的目标突变仅通过自然语言评判来编辑该模块。多样性感知种群选择保留互补候选方案，以确保解决方案的多样性。在四个基准测试中，EvoTool在GPT-4.1和Qwen3-8B上都优于强大的基线超过5个点，同时实现了卓越的效率和可迁移性。代码将在论文被接收后发布。

TLDR: EvoTool is a self-evolving framework that optimizes modular tool-use policies in LLM agents using blame attribution, targeted mutation, and diversity-aware selection, outperforming strong baselines in several benchmarks.

简要说明: EvoTool是一个自进化框架，它通过归因、针对性突变和多样性选择来优化LLM代理中模块化的工具使用策略，并在多个基准测试中优于现有方法。

Authors: Shuo Yang, Soyeon Caren Han, Xueqi Ma, Yan Li, Mohammad Reza Ghasemi Madani, Eduard Hovy

Latent Particle World Models: Self-supervised Object-centric Stochastic Dynamics Modeling

Abstract (English): We introduce Latent Particle World Model (LPWM), a self-supervised object-centric world model scaled to real-world multi-object datasets and applicable in decision-making. LPWM autonomously discovers keypoints, bounding boxes, and object masks directly from video data, enabling it to learn rich scene decompositions without supervision. Our architecture is trained end-to-end purely from videos and supports flexible conditioning on actions, language, and image goals. LPWM models stochastic particle dynamics via a novel latent action module and achieves state-of-the-art results on diverse real-world and synthetic datasets. Beyond stochastic video modeling, LPWM is readily applicable to decision-making, including goal-conditioned imitation learning, as we demonstrate in the paper. Code, data, pre-trained models and video rollouts are available: https://taldatech.github.io/lpwm-web

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了潜在粒子世界模型（LPWM），一种自监督的、以对象为中心的世界模型，可扩展到真实世界的多对象数据集并适用于决策。 LPWM能够直接从视频数据中自主发现关键点、边界框和对象掩码，从而无需监督即可学习丰富的场景分解。 我们的架构完全从视频中进行端到端训练，并支持基于动作、语言和图像目标的灵活条件控制。 LPWM通过一种新颖的潜在动作模块对随机粒子动力学进行建模，并在各种真实世界和合成数据集上取得了最先进的结果。 除了随机视频建模之外，LPWM还可轻松应用于决策，包括目标条件模仿学习，正如我们在本文中所展示的那样。代码、数据、预训练模型和视频回滚可在此处获得：https://taldatech.github.io/lpwm-web

TLDR: The paper introduces Latent Particle World Model (LPWM), a self-supervised object-centric world model that learns scene decompositions and stochastic particle dynamics from video data, achieving state-of-the-art results and enabling goal-conditioned imitation learning.

简要说明: 本文介绍了潜粒子世界模型（LPWM），这是一种自我监督的以对象为中心的世界模型，可以从视频数据中学习场景分解和随机粒子动力学，实现了最先进的结果，并实现了目标条件模仿学习。

Authors: Tal Daniel, Carl Qi, Dan Haramati, Amir Zadeh, Chuan Li, Aviv Tamar, Deepak Pathak, David Held

PhysiFlow: Physics-Aware Humanoid Whole-Body VLA via Multi-Brain Latent Flow Matching and Robust Tracking

Abstract (English): In the domain of humanoid robot control, the fusion of Vision-Language-Action (VLA) with whole-body control is essential for semantically guided execution of real-world tasks. However, existing methods encounter challenges in terms of low VLA inference efficiency or an absence of effective semantic guidance for whole-body control, resulting in instability in dynamic limb-coordinated tasks. To bridge this gap, we present a semantic-motion intent guided, physics-aware multi-brain VLA framework for humanoid whole-body control. A series of experiments was conducted to evaluate the performance of the proposed framework. The experimental results demonstrated that the framework enabled reliable vision-language-guided full-body coordination for humanoid robots.

摘要（中文）: 在人形机器人控制领域，视觉-语言-动作(VLA)与全身控制的融合对于语义引导的现实世界任务执行至关重要。然而，现有方法在VLA推理效率低下或缺乏对全身控制的有效语义引导方面面临挑战，导致动态肢体协调任务的不稳定性。为了弥补这一差距，我们提出了一种语义-运动意图引导的、具备物理感知的多脑VLA框架，用于人形机器人全身控制。 一系列实验被用来评估所提框架的性能。实验结果表明，该框架能够实现可靠的视觉-语言引导的人形机器人全身协调。

TLDR: The paper introduces a physics-aware multi-brain VLA framework called PhysiFlow for humanoid robot whole-body control, addressing limitations in efficiency and semantic guidance of existing VLA methods for dynamic tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个名为PhysiFlow的物理感知多脑VLA框架，用于人形机器人全身控制，解决了现有VLA方法在动态任务中的效率和语义指导方面的局限性。

Authors: Weikai Qin, Sichen Wu, Ci Chen, Mengfan Liu, Linxi Feng, Xinru Cui, Haoqi Han, Hesheng Wang

UltraDexGrasp: Learning Universal Dexterous Grasping for Bimanual Robots with Synthetic Data

Abstract (English): Grasping is a fundamental capability for robots to interact with the physical world. Humans, equipped with two hands, autonomously select appropriate grasp strategies based on the shape, size, and weight of objects, enabling robust grasping and subsequent manipulation. In contrast, current robotic grasping remains limited, particularly in multi-strategy settings. Although substantial efforts have targeted parallel-gripper and single-hand grasping, dexterous grasping for bimanual robots remains underexplored, with data being a primary bottleneck. Achieving physically plausible and geometrically conforming grasps that can withstand external wrenches poses significant challenges. To address these issues, we introduce UltraDexGrasp, a framework for universal dexterous grasping with bimanual robots. The proposed data-generation pipeline integrates optimization-based grasp synthesis with planning-based demonstration generation, yielding high-quality and diverse trajectories across multiple grasp strategies. With this framework, we curate UltraDexGrasp-20M, a large-scale, multi-strategy grasp dataset comprising 20 million frames across 1,000 objects. Based on UltraDexGrasp-20M, we further develop a simple yet effective grasp policy that takes point clouds as input, aggregates scene features via unidirectional attention, and predicts control commands. Trained exclusively on synthetic data, the policy achieves robust zero-shot sim-to-real transfer and consistently succeeds on novel objects with varied shapes, sizes, and weights, attaining an average success rate of 81.2% in real-world universal dexterous grasping. To facilitate future research on grasping with bimanual robots, we open-source the data generation pipeline at https://github.com/InternRobotics/UltraDexGrasp.

摘要（中文）: 抓取是机器人与物理世界交互的一项基础能力。人类凭借双手，能够根据物体的形状、大小和重量自主选择合适的抓取策略，从而实现稳健的抓取和后续操作。相比之下，当前的机器人抓取仍然受到限制，尤其是在多策略的场景下。尽管大量的研究工作集中于平行夹爪和单手抓取，但针对双臂机器人的灵巧抓取仍然未被充分探索，数据是主要的瓶颈。实现物理上合理且几何上符合的、能够承受外部扳手的抓取姿态带来了巨大的挑战。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了UltraDexGrasp，一个用于双臂机器人通用灵巧抓取的框架。所提出的数据生成流程集成了基于优化的抓取合成和基于规划的示教生成，从而产生了高质量且多样化的、跨多种抓取策略的轨迹。基于此框架，我们整理了 UltraDexGrasp-20M，一个大规模、多策略的抓取数据集，包含 1000 个物体的 2000 万帧数据。基于 UltraDexGrasp-20M，我们进一步开发了一种简单而有效的抓取策略，该策略以点云作为输入，通过单向注意力聚合场景特征，并预测控制指令。该策略完全在合成数据上训练，实现了鲁棒的零样本 Sim-to-Real 迁移，并在各种形状、大小和重量的新物体上持续成功，在真实世界通用灵巧抓取中达到了 81.2% 的平均成功率。为了促进未来对双臂机器人抓取的研究，我们开源了数据生成流程，地址为 https://github.com/InternRobotics/UltraDexGrasp。

TLDR: The paper introduces UltraDexGrasp, a framework and large-scale synthetic dataset for learning universal dexterous grasping with bimanual robots, demonstrating robust zero-shot sim-to-real transfer with a simple grasp policy.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了UltraDexGrasp，一个用于学习双臂机器人通用灵巧抓取的框架和大规模合成数据集，并通过简单的抓取策略展示了强大的零样本模拟到真实的迁移能力。

Authors: Sizhe Yang, Yiman Xie, Zhixuan Liang, Yang Tian, Jia Zeng, Dahua Lin, Jiangmiao Pang

Latent Policy Steering through One-Step Flow Policies

Abstract (English): Offline reinforcement learning (RL) allows robots to learn from offline datasets without risky exploration. Yet, offline RL's performance often hinges on a brittle trade-off between (1) return maximization, which can push policies outside the dataset support, and (2) behavioral constraints, which typically require sensitive hyperparameter tuning. Latent steering offers a structural way to stay within the dataset support during RL, but existing offline adaptations commonly approximate action values using latent-space critics learned via indirect distillation, which can lose information and hinder convergence. We propose Latent Policy Steering (LPS), which enables high-fidelity latent policy improvement by backpropagating original-action-space Q-gradients through a differentiable one-step MeanFlow policy to update a latent-action-space actor. By eliminating proxy latent critics, LPS allows an original-action-space critic to guide end-to-end latent-space optimization, while the one-step MeanFlow policy serves as a behavior-constrained generative prior. This decoupling yields a robust method that works out-of-the-box with minimal tuning. Across OGBench and real-world robotic tasks, LPS achieves state-of-the-art performance and consistently outperforms behavioral cloning and strong latent steering baselines.

摘要（中文）: 离线强化学习 (RL) 允许机器人从离线数据集中学习，而无需进行有风险的探索。然而，离线 RL 的性能通常取决于 (1) 回报最大化与 (2) 行为约束之间脆弱的权衡，前者可能会将策略推到数据集支持之外，而后者通常需要灵敏的超参数调整。潜在空间操纵提供了一种在 RL 期间保持在数据集支持范围内的结构化方法，但现有的离线适配通常使用通过间接蒸馏学习的潜在空间评论家来近似行动价值，这可能会丢失信息并阻碍收敛。我们提出了潜在策略操纵 (LPS)，它通过将原始动作空间的 Q-梯度反向传播到可微分的单步 MeanFlow 策略，来更新潜在动作空间中的策略，从而实现高保真的潜在策略提升。通过消除代理潜在空间评论家，LPS 允许原始动作空间的评论家指导端到端的潜在空间优化，而单步 MeanFlow 策略则充当行为约束的生成先验。这种解耦产生了一种鲁棒的方法，可以开箱即用，且只需最少的调整。在 OGBench 和真实世界的机器人任务中，LPS 实现了最先进的性能，并始终优于行为克隆和强大的潜在空间操纵基线。

TLDR: The paper introduces Latent Policy Steering (LPS), a novel offline RL method that leverages a differentiable one-step MeanFlow policy for high-fidelity latent policy improvement, achieving state-of-the-art performance across multiple benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种新的离线强化学习方法，称为潜在策略引导（LPS），它利用可微的单步 MeanFlow 策略来实现高保真潜在策略的改进，并在多个基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。

Authors: Hokyun Im, Andrey Kolobov, Jianlong Fu, Youngwoon Lee

Iterative On-Policy Refinement of Hierarchical Diffusion Policies for Language-Conditioned Manipulation

Abstract (English): Hierarchical policies for language-conditioned manipulation decompose tasks into subgoals, where a high-level planner guides a low-level controller. However, these hierarchical agents often fail because the planner generates subgoals without considering the actual limitations of the controller. Existing solutions attempt to bridge this gap via intermediate modules or shared representations, but they remain limited by their reliance on fixed offline datasets. We propose HD-ExpIt, a framework for iterative fine-tuning of hierarchical diffusion policies via environment feedback. HD-ExpIt organizes training into a self-reinforcing cycle: it utilizes diffusion-based planning to autonomously discover successful behaviors, which are then distilled back into the hierarchical policy. This loop enables both components to improve while implicitly grounding the planner in the controller's actual capabilities without requiring explicit proxy models. Empirically, HD-ExpIt significantly improves hierarchical policies trained solely on offline data, achieving state-of-the-art performance on the long-horizon CALVIN benchmark among methods trained from scratch.

摘要（中文）: 语言条件操纵的分层策略将任务分解为子目标，其中高层规划器指导低层控制器。然而，这些分层智能体常常失败，因为规划器在生成子目标时没有考虑控制器的实际限制。现有的解决方案试图通过中间模块或共享表示来弥合这一差距，但它们仍然受到其对固定离线数据集的依赖的限制。我们提出HD-ExpIt，一个通过环境反馈迭代精调分层扩散策略的框架。HD-ExpIt将训练组织成一个自我增强的循环：它利用基于扩散的规划自主发现成功的行为，然后将其提炼回分层策略中。这个循环使得两个组件都能得到改进，同时隐式地将规划器建立在控制器的实际能力上，而无需显式的代理模型。在实验上，HD-ExpIt显著改进了完全在离线数据上训练的分层策略，在从头开始训练的方法中，在长时程CALVIN基准测试上实现了最先进的性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces HD-ExpIt, a framework for iteratively refining hierarchical diffusion policies via environment feedback for language-conditioned manipulation, achieving state-of-the-art performance on the CALVIN benchmark from scratch.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了HD-ExpIt，一个通过环境反馈迭代改进分层扩散策略的框架，用于语言条件下的操作任务，并在CALVIN基准测试中从头开始训练时实现了最先进的性能。

Authors: Clemence Grislain, Olivier Sigaud, Mohamed Chetouani

Digital Twin Driven Textile Classification and Foreign Object Recognition in Automated Sorting Systems

Abstract (English): The increasing demand for sustainable textile recycling requires robust automation solutions capable of handling deformable garments and detecting foreign objects in cluttered environments. This work presents a digital twin driven robotic sorting system that integrates grasp prediction, multi modal perception, and semantic reasoning for real world textile classification. A dual arm robotic cell equipped with RGBD sensing, capacitive tactile feedback, and collision-aware motion planning autonomously separates garments from an unsorted basket, transfers them to an inspection zone, and classifies them using state of the art Visual Language Models (VLMs). We benchmark nine VLM s from five model families on a dataset of 223 inspection scenarios comprising shirts, socks, trousers, underwear, foreign objects (including garments outside of the aforementioned classes), and empty scenes. The evaluation assesses per class accuracy, hallucination behavior, and computational performance under practical hardware constraints. Results show that the Qwen model family achieves the highest overall accuracy (up to 87.9 %), with strong foreign object detection performance, while lighter models such as Gemma3 offer competitive speed accuracy trade offs for edge deployment. A digital twin combined with MoveIt enables collision aware path planning and integrates segmented 3D point clouds of inspected garments into the virtual environment for improved manipulation reliability. The presented system demonstrates the feasibility of combining semantic VLM reasoning with conventional grasp detection and digital twin technology for scalable, autonomous textile sorting in realistic industrial settings.

摘要（中文）: 对可持续纺织品回收日益增长的需求促使人们寻求能够处理可变形衣物并检测杂乱环境中异物的强大自动化解决方案。本研究提出了一种数字孪生驱动的机器人分拣系统，该系统集成了抓取预测、多模态感知和语义推理，用于现实世界的纺织品分类。一个配备RGBD传感、电容式触觉反馈和防碰撞运动规划的双臂机器人单元，能够自主地从一个未分类的篮子中分离衣物，并将它们转移到检查区域，然后使用最先进的视觉语言模型（VLMs）对它们进行分类。我们在一个包含衬衫、袜子、裤子、内衣、异物（包括上述类别之外的衣物）和空场景的223个检查场景的数据集上，对来自五个模型系列的九个VLMs进行了基准测试。评估内容包括各类别的准确率、幻觉行为以及在实际硬件约束下的计算性能。结果表明，Qwen模型系列实现了最高的总体准确率（高达 87.9%），并具有强大的异物检测性能，而像Gemma3这样的更轻量级模型则为边缘部署提供了具有竞争力的速度-准确率权衡。数字孪生结合MoveIt实现了防碰撞路径规划，并将被检查衣物的分割3D点云集成到虚拟环境中，以提高操纵的可靠性。所提出的系统证明了将语义VLMs推理与传统抓取检测和数字孪生技术相结合，用于在现实工业环境中实现可扩展的自主纺织品分拣的可行性。

TLDR: This paper presents a digital twin-driven robotic system for automated textile sorting, using VLMs for classification and foreign object detection, demonstrating promising results with the Qwen model family. The system also uses MoveIt for collision-aware path planning and updates the digital twin with segmented garment point clouds.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种数字孪生驱动的机器人系统，用于自动纺织品分类，使用视觉语言模型（VLM）进行分类和异物检测，并展示了Qwen模型家族的良好性能。该系统还使用MoveIt进行避碰路径规划，并使用分割后的服装点云更新数字孪生。

Authors: Serkan Ergun, Tobias Mitterer, Hubert Zangl

Lifelong Language-Conditioned Robotic Manipulation Learning

Abstract (English): Traditional language-conditioned manipulation agent sequential adaptation to new manipulation skills leads to catastrophic forgetting of old skills, limiting dynamic scene practical deployment. In this paper, we propose SkillsCrafter, a novel robotic manipulation framework designed to continually learn multiple skills while reducing catastrophic forgetting of old skills. Specifically, we propose a Manipulation Skills Adaptation to retain the old skills knowledge while inheriting the shared knowledge between new and old skills to facilitate learning of new skills. Meanwhile, we perform the singular value decomposition on the diverse skill instructions to obtain common skill semantic subspace projection matrices, thereby recording the essential semantic space of skills. To achieve forget-less and generalization manipulation, we propose a Skills Specialization Aggregation to compute inter-skills similarity in skill semantic subspaces, achieving aggregation of the previously learned skill knowledge for any new or unknown skill. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness and superiority of our proposed SkillsCrafter.

摘要（中文）: 传统语言条件下的操控智能体在顺序适应新操控技能时，会导致旧技能的灾难性遗忘，从而限制了动态场景的实际部署。在本文中，我们提出了 SkillsCrafter，一种新型的机器人操控框架，旨在持续学习多种技能，同时减少旧技能的灾难性遗忘。具体来说，我们提出了一种操控技能适应方法，以保留旧技能知识，同时继承新旧技能之间的共享知识，从而促进新技能的学习。同时，我们对多样的技能指令进行奇异值分解，以获得通用的技能语义子空间投影矩阵，从而记录技能的基本语义空间。为了实现无遗忘和泛化的操控，我们提出了一种技能专业化聚合方法，以计算技能语义子空间中的技能间相似度，从而实现对任何新的或未知的技能的先前学习的技能知识的聚合。大量的实验证明了我们提出的 SkillsCrafter 的有效性和优越性。

TLDR: The paper introduces SkillsCrafter, a new robotic manipulation framework using language-conditioned learning to mitigate catastrophic forgetting in sequential skill adaptation, leveraging semantic subspace projection and skill similarity aggregation.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为SkillsCrafter的新的机器人操纵框架，该框架使用语言条件学习来减轻顺序技能适应中的灾难性遗忘，利用语义子空间投影和技能相似性聚合。

Authors: Xudong Wang, Zebin Han, Zhiyu Liu, Gan Li, Jiahua Dong, Baichen Liu, Lianqing Liu, Zhi Han

Act, Think or Abstain: Complexity-Aware Adaptive Inference for Vision-Language-Action Models

Abstract (English): Current research on Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models predominantly focuses on enhancing generalization through established reasoning techniques. While effective, these improvements invariably increase computational complexity and inference latency. Furthermore, these mechanisms are typically applied indiscriminately, resulting in the inefficient allocation of resources for trivial tasks while simultaneously failing to provide the uncertainty estimation necessary to prevent catastrophic failure on out-of-distribution tasks. Inspired by human cognition, we propose an adaptive framework that dynamically routes VLA execution based on the complexity of the perceived state. Our approach transforms the VLA's vision-language backbone into an active detection tool by projecting latent embeddings into an ensemble of parametric and non-parametric estimators. This allows the system to execute known tasks immediately (Act), reason about ambiguous scenarios (Think), and preemptively halt execution when encountering significant physical or semantic anomalies (Abstain). In our empirical analysis, we observe a phenomenon where visual embeddings alone are superior for inferring task complexity due to the semantic invariance of language. Evaluated on the LIBERO and LIBERO-PRO benchmarks as well as on a real robot, our vision-only configuration achieves 80% F1-Score using as little as 5% of training data, establishing itself as a reliable and efficient task complexity detector.

摘要（中文）: 当前视觉-语言-动作 (VLA) 模型的研究主要集中在使用成熟的推理技术来增强泛化能力。尽管这些方法有效，但它们总是会增加计算复杂性和推理延迟。此外，这些机制通常被无差别地应用，导致对简单任务的资源分配效率低下，同时又未能提供必要的不确定性估计，从而无法防止在分布外任务上发生灾难性故障。受人类认知启发，我们提出了一种自适应框架，该框架根据感知状态的复杂性动态路由 VLA 的执行过程。我们的方法将 VLA 的视觉-语言主干转变为一种主动检测工具，通过将潜在嵌入投影到参数和非参数估计器的集成中来实现。这使得系统能够立即执行已知任务（Act），推理模糊场景（Think），以及在遇到显著的物理或语义异常时提前停止执行（Abstain）。在我们的实证分析中，我们观察到一种现象，即仅使用视觉嵌入在推断任务复杂性方面更胜一筹，因为语言具有语义不变性。在 LIBERO 和 LIBERO-PRO 基准以及真实机器人上的评估表明，我们仅使用视觉的配置能够使用少至 5% 的训练数据达到 80% 的 F1 分数，从而确立了其作为可靠且高效的任务复杂性检测器的地位。

TLDR: This paper proposes an adaptive inference framework for VLA models that dynamically routes execution based on task complexity, using a vision-only configuration for efficient task complexity detection, showing promising results on robot navigation benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种VLA模型的自适应推理框架，该框架根据任务的复杂性动态地路由执行，使用纯视觉配置进行高效的任务复杂性检测，并在机器人导航基准测试中显示出有希望的结果。

Authors: Riccardo Andrea Izzo, Gianluca Bardaro, Matteo Matteucci

SeedPolicy: Horizon Scaling via Self-Evolving Diffusion Policy for Robot Manipulation

Abstract (English): Imitation Learning (IL) enables robots to acquire manipulation skills from expert demonstrations. Diffusion Policy (DP) models multi-modal expert behaviors but suffers performance degradation as observation horizons increase, limiting long-horizon manipulation. We propose Self-Evolving Gated Attention (SEGA), a temporal module that maintains a time-evolving latent state via gated attention, enabling efficient recurrent updates that compress long-horizon observations into a fixed-size representation while filtering irrelevant temporal information. Integrating SEGA into DP yields Self-Evolving Diffusion Policy (SeedPolicy), which resolves the temporal modeling bottleneck and enables scalable horizon extension with moderate overhead. On the RoboTwin 2.0 benchmark with 50 manipulation tasks, SeedPolicy outperforms DP and other IL baselines. Averaged across both CNN and Transformer backbones, SeedPolicy achieves 36.8% relative improvement in clean settings and 169% relative improvement in randomized challenging settings over the DP. Compared to vision-language-action models such as RDT with 1.2B parameters, SeedPolicy achieves competitive performance with one to two orders of magnitude fewer parameters, demonstrating strong efficiency and scalability. These results establish SeedPolicy as a state-of-the-art imitation learning method for long-horizon robotic manipulation. Code is available at: https://github.com/Youqiang-Gui/SeedPolicy.

摘要（中文）: 模仿学习 (IL) 使机器人能够从专家演示中获得操作技能。扩散策略 (DP) 能够对多模态专家行为进行建模，但随着观察时间范围的增加，其性能会下降，从而限制了长程操作。我们提出了一种自演化门控注意力 (SEGA)，这是一种时间模块，通过门控注意力维护一个随时间演化的潜在状态，从而实现高效的循环更新，将长程观察压缩成固定大小的表示，同时过滤掉不相关的时间信息。将 SEGA 集成到 DP 中，产生自演化扩散策略 (SeedPolicy)，从而解决了时间建模瓶颈，并能够以适中的开销扩展时间范围。在包含 50 个操作任务的 RoboTwin 2.0 基准上，SeedPolicy 优于 DP 和其他 IL 基线。在使用 CNN 和 Transformer 作为主干网络的平均情况下，SeedPolicy 在干净设置下实现了 36.8% 的相对改进，在随机化的挑战性设置下实现了 169% 的相对改进，优于 DP。与具有 12 亿参数的视觉-语言-动作模型（例如 RDT）相比，SeedPolicy 在参数数量减少一到两个数量级的情况下实现了具有竞争力的性能，证明了其强大的效率和可扩展性。这些结果证明了 SeedPolicy 作为长程机器人操作最先进的模仿学习方法。代码可在以下网址获取：https://github.com/Youqiang-Gui/SeedPolicy。

TLDR: The paper introduces SeedPolicy, a Diffusion Policy variant that uses a Self-Evolving Gated Attention mechanism to improve performance in long-horizon robotic manipulation tasks. SeedPolicy achieves state-of-the-art results on the RoboTwin 2.0 benchmark while using significantly fewer parameters than vision-language-action models.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为SeedPolicy的扩散策略变体，该变体使用自演化门控注意力机制来提高长程机器人操作任务的性能。SeedPolicy在RoboTwin 2.0基准测试中取得了最先进的结果，同时使用的参数明显少于视觉-语言-动作模型。

Authors: Youqiang Gui, Yuxuan Zhou, Shen Cheng, Xinyang Yuan, Haoqiang Fan, Peng Cheng, Shuaicheng Liu

Decoupling Task and Behavior: A Two-Stage Reward Curriculum in Reinforcement Learning for Robotics

Abstract (English): Deep Reinforcement Learning is a promising tool for robotic control, yet practical application is often hindered by the difficulty of designing effective reward functions. Real-world tasks typically require optimizing multiple objectives simultaneously, necessitating precise tuning of their weights to learn a policy with the desired characteristics. To address this, we propose a two-stage reward curriculum where we decouple task-specific objectives from behavioral terms. In our method, we first train the agent on a simplified task-only reward function to ensure effective exploration before introducing the full reward that includes auxiliary behavior-related terms such as energy efficiency. Further, we analyze various transition strategies and demonstrate that reusing samples between phases is critical for training stability. We validate our approach on the DeepMind Control Suite, ManiSkill3, and a mobile robot environment, modified to include auxiliary behavioral objectives. Our method proves to be simple yet effective, substantially outperforming baselines trained directly on the full reward while exhibiting higher robustness to specific reward weightings.

摘要（中文）: 深度强化学习是机器人控制领域一种很有前景的工具，然而，实际应用往往受到难以设计有效的奖励函数的阻碍。现实世界的任务通常需要同时优化多个目标，因此需要精确调整它们的权重，才能学习到具有所需特征的策略。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种两阶段奖励课程，在该课程中，我们将特定任务目标与行为项解耦。在我们的方法中，我们首先在简化的仅任务奖励函数上训练智能体，以确保有效的探索，然后再引入包含辅助行为相关项（如能源效率）的完整奖励。此外，我们分析了各种转移策略，并证明在阶段之间重用样本对于训练稳定性至关重要。我们在 DeepMind Control Suite、ManiSkill3 和一个移动机器人环境（修改后包含辅助行为目标）上验证了我们的方法。我们的方法证明了其简单而有效，显著优于直接在完整奖励上训练的基线方法，同时对特定奖励权重的鲁棒性更高。

TLDR: This paper introduces a two-stage reward curriculum for robotic reinforcement learning that decouples task-specific objectives from behavioral terms, leading to improved performance and robustness.

Authors: Kilian Freitag, Knut Åkesson, Morteza Haghir Chehreghani

SPIRIT: Perceptive Shared Autonomy for Robust Robotic Manipulation under Deep Learning Uncertainty

Abstract (English): Deep learning (DL) has enabled impressive advances in robotic perception, yet its limited robustness and lack of interpretability hinder reliable deployment in safety critical applications. We propose a concept termed perceptive shared autonomy, in which uncertainty estimates from DL based perception are used to regulate the level of autonomy. Specifically, when the robot's perception is confident, semi-autonomous manipulation is enabled to improve performance; when uncertainty increases, control transitions to haptic teleoperation for maintaining robustness. In this way, high-performing but uninterpretable DL methods can be integrated safely into robotic systems. A key technical enabler is an uncertainty aware DL based point cloud registration approach based on the so called Neural Tangent Kernels (NTK). We evaluate perceptive shared autonomy on challenging aerial manipulation tasks through a user study of 15 participants and realization of mock-up industrial scenarios, demonstrating reliable robotic manipulation despite failures in DL based perception. The resulting system, named SPIRIT, improves both manipulation performance and system reliability. SPIRIT was selected as a finalist of a major industrial innovation award.

摘要（中文）: 深度学习(DL)已在机器人感知领域取得了显著进展，但其有限的鲁棒性和缺乏可解释性阻碍了其在安全关键型应用中的可靠部署。我们提出了一种名为感知共享自主的概念，其中来自基于DL的感知的置信度估计被用于调节自主水平。具体来说，当机器人的感知具有高度置信度时，启用半自主操作以提高性能；当置信度降低时，控制过渡到触觉遥操作以保持鲁棒性。通过这种方式，高性能但不可解释的DL方法可以安全地集成到机器人系统中。一个关键的技术推动因素是基于所谓的神经正切核(NTK)的、基于DL的、具有置信度意识的点云配准方法。我们通过一项包含15名参与者的用户研究以及模拟的工业场景，在具有挑战性的空中操作任务中评估了感知共享自主，验证了即使基于DL的感知出现故障，也能实现可靠的机器人操作。由此产生的系统，名为SPIRIT，提高了操作性能和系统可靠性。SPIRIT入围了一项重要的工业创新奖的决赛。

TLDR: The paper introduces SPIRIT, a perceptive shared autonomy system that leverages uncertainty estimates from deep learning-based perception to switch between semi-autonomous manipulation and haptic teleoperation, enhancing robustness in robotic manipulation, especially in aerial scenarios.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了SPIRIT，一种感知共享自主系统，它利用深度学习感知的不确定性估计，在半自主操作和触觉遥操作之间切换，从而增强了机器人操作的鲁棒性，特别是在空中场景中。

Authors: Jongseok Lee, Ribin Balachandran, Harsimran Singh, Jianxiang Feng, Hrishik Mishra, Marco De Stefano, Rudolph Triebel, Alin Albu-Schaeffer, Konstantin Kondak

GaussTwin: Unified Simulation and Correction with Gaussian Splatting for Robotic Digital Twins

Abstract (English): Digital twins promise to enhance robotic manipulation by maintaining a consistent link between real-world perception and simulation. However, most existing systems struggle with the lack of a unified model, complex dynamic interactions, and the real-to-sim gap, which limits downstream applications such as model predictive control. Thus, we propose GaussTwin, a real-time digital twin that combines position-based dynamics with discrete Cosserat rod formulations for physically grounded simulation, and Gaussian splatting for efficient rendering and visual correction. By anchoring Gaussians to physical primitives and enforcing coherent SE(3) updates driven by photometric error and segmentation masks, GaussTwin achieves stable prediction-correction while preserving physical fidelity. Through experiments in both simulation and on a Franka Research 3 platform, we show that GaussTwin consistently improves tracking accuracy and robustness compared to shape-matching and rigid-only baselines, while also enabling downstream tasks such as push-based planning. These results highlight GaussTwin as a step toward unified, physically meaningful digital twins that can support closed-loop robotic interaction and learning.

摘要（中文）: 数字孪生有望通过维持真实世界感知和仿真之间的一致性联系来增强机器人操作。然而，现有的大多数系统都面临着缺乏统一模型、复杂的动态交互以及真实到仿真（real-to-sim）的鸿沟等问题，这些问题限制了诸如模型预测控制之类的下游应用。因此，我们提出了GaussTwin，一种实时数字孪生，它结合了基于位置的动力学和离散Cosserat杆公式用于物理上的仿真，并结合高斯溅射用于高效渲染和视觉校正。通过将高斯分布锚定到物理原语，并强制执行由光度误差和分割掩码驱动的连贯SE(3)更新，GaussTwin实现了稳定的预测-校正，同时保持了物理保真度。通过在仿真和Franka Research 3平台上进行的实验，我们表明，与形状匹配和仅刚体基线相比，GaussTwin始终如一地提高了跟踪精度和鲁棒性，同时还支持了诸如基于推送的规划等下游任务。这些结果表明，GaussTwin是朝着统一的、具有物理意义的数字孪生迈出的一步，它可以支持闭环机器人交互和学习。

TLDR: GaussTwin introduces a real-time digital twin system for robotic manipulation using Gaussian splatting and physically grounded simulation to improve tracking accuracy and enable downstream tasks like push-based planning.

简要说明: GaussTwin 提出了一个用于机器人操作的实时数字孪生系统，该系统使用高斯溅射和基于物理的仿真，从而提高跟踪精度并实现诸如基于推动的规划等下游任务。

Authors: Yichen Cai, Paul Jansonnie, Cristiana de Farias, Oleg Arenz, Jan Peters

Direct Contact-Tolerant Motion Planning With Vision Language Models

Abstract (English): Navigation in cluttered environments often requires robots to tolerate contact with movable or deformable objects to maintain efficiency. Existing contact-tolerant motion planning (CTMP) methods rely on indirect spatial representations (e.g., prebuilt map, obstacle set), resulting in inaccuracies and a lack of adaptiveness to environmental uncertainties. To address this issue, we propose a direct contact-tolerant (DCT) planner, which integrates vision-language models (VLMs) into direct point perception and navigation, including two key components. The first one is VLM point cloud partitioner (VPP), which performs contact-tolerance reasoning in image space using VLM, caches inference masks, propagates them across frames using odometry, and projects them onto the current scan to generate a contact-aware point cloud. The second innovation is VPP guided navigation (VGN), which formulates CTMP as a perception-to-control optimization problem under direct contact-aware point cloud constraints, which is further solved by a specialized deep neural network (DNN). We implement DCT in Isaac Sim and a real car-like robot, demonstrating that DCT achieves robust and efficient navigation in cluttered environments with movable obstacles, outperforming representative baselines across diverse metrics. The code is available at: https://github.com/ChrisLeeUM/DCT.

摘要（中文）: 在杂乱环境中导航通常需要机器人能够容忍与可移动或可变形物体的接触，以保持效率。现有的容许接触运动规划(CTMP)方法依赖于间接的空间表示（例如，预先构建的地图、障碍物集合），导致不准确和缺乏对环境不确定性的适应性。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种直接容许接触(DCT)规划器，它将视觉-语言模型(VLM)集成到直接点云感知和导航中，包括两个关键组件。第一个是VLM点云分割器(VPP)，它使用VLM在图像空间中执行容许接触推理，缓存推理掩码，使用里程计在帧之间传播它们，并将它们投影到当前扫描上，以生成一个具有接触感知的点云。第二个创新是VPP引导的导航(VGN)，它将CTMP形式化为一个在直接接触感知点云约束下的感知到控制的优化问题，并通过一个专门的深度神经网络(DNN)进一步求解。我们在Isaac Sim和一个真实的类车机器人上实现了DCT，结果表明，DCT在充满可移动障碍物的杂乱环境中实现了稳健和高效的导航，在各种指标上优于代表性的基线方法。代码可在以下网址获得：https://github.com/ChrisLeeUM/DCT。

TLDR: This paper introduces a direct contact-tolerant motion planning (DCT) method that uses Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to navigate cluttered environments by reasoning about contact-tolerance from image space and optimizing navigation based on contact-aware point clouds.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种直接接触容错运动规划（DCT）方法，该方法利用视觉语言模型（VLM）通过推理图像空间中的接触容错来导航拥挤环境，并基于接触感知点云优化导航。

Authors: He Li, Jian Sun, Chengyang Li, Guoliang Li, Qiyu Ruan, Shuai Wang, Chengzhong Xu

VPWEM: Non-Markovian Visuomotor Policy with Working and Episodic Memory

Abstract (English): Imitation learning from human demonstrations has achieved significant success in robotic control, yet most visuomotor policies still condition on single-step observations or short-context histories, making them struggle with non-Markovian tasks that require long-term memory. Simply enlarging the context window incurs substantial computational and memory costs and encourages overfitting to spurious correlations, leading to catastrophic failures under distribution shift and violating real-time constraints in robotic systems. By contrast, humans can compress important past experiences into long-term memories and exploit them to solve tasks throughout their lifetime. In this paper, we propose VPWEM, a non-Markovian visuomotor policy equipped with working and episodic memories. VPWEM retains a sliding window of recent observation tokens as short-term working memory, and introduces a Transformer-based contextual memory compressor that recursively converts out-of-window observations into a fixed number of episodic memory tokens. The compressor uses self-attention over a cache of past summary tokens and cross-attention over a cache of historical observations, and is trained jointly with the policy. We instantiate VPWEM on diffusion policies to exploit both short-term and episode-wide information for action generation with nearly constant memory and computation per step. Experiments demonstrate that VPWEM outperforms state-of-the-art baselines including diffusion policies and vision-language-action (VLA) models by more than 20% on the memory-intensive manipulation tasks in MIKASA and achieves an average 5% improvement on the mobile manipulation benchmark MoMaRT. Code is available at https://github.com/HarryLui98/code_vpwem.

摘要（中文）: 从人类演示中进行模仿学习已在机器人控制领域取得了显著成功，然而，大多数视觉运动策略仍然依赖于单步观测或短上下文历史，这使得它们难以应对需要长期记忆的非马尔可夫任务。简单地扩大上下文窗口会导致大量的计算和内存成本，并容易过度拟合虚假相关性，从而在分布偏移下导致灾难性失败，并且违背机器人系统中的实时约束。相比之下，人类可以将重要的过往经验压缩成长时记忆，并利用这些记忆来解决其一生中的任务。在本文中，我们提出了一种配备工作记忆和情景记忆的非马尔可夫视觉运动策略VPWEM。VPWEM保留了一个滑动窗口，用于存储最近的观测令牌作为短期工作记忆，并引入了一个基于Transformer的上下文记忆压缩器，该压缩器递归地将窗口外的观测转换为固定数量的情景记忆令牌。该压缩器使用对过去摘要令牌缓存的自注意力，以及对历史观测缓存的交叉注意力，并与策略联合训练。我们实例化了基于扩散策略的VPWEM，以利用短期和情景级别的全部信息来生成动作，同时保持近乎恒定的每步内存和计算量。实验表明，VPWEM在MIKASA中对内存密集型操作任务的表现优于包括扩散策略和视觉-语言-动作(VLA)模型在内的最先进基线20%以上，并在移动操作基准测试MoMaRT上平均提高了5%。代码可在https://github.com/HarryLui98/code_vpwem 获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces VPWEM, a non-Markovian visuomotor policy with working and episodic memory for imitation learning, showing significant improvement on long-horizon manipulation tasks compared to state-of-the-art baselines.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了VPWEM，一种具有工作记忆和情景记忆的非马尔可夫视觉运动策略，用于模仿学习，与最先进的基线相比，在长时程操作任务上表现出显著改进。

Authors: Yuheng Lei, Zhixuan Liang, Hongyuan Zhang, Ping Luo

Causally Robust Reward Learning from Reason-Augmented Preference Feedback

Abstract (English): Preference-based reward learning is widely used for shaping agent behavior to match a user's preference, yet its sparse binary feedback makes it especially vulnerable to causal confusion. The learned reward often latches onto spurious features that merely co-occur with preferred trajectories during training, collapsing when those correlations disappear or reverse at test time. We introduce ReCouPLe, a lightweight framework that uses natural language rationales to provide the missing causal signal. Each rationale is treated as a guiding projection axis in an embedding space, training the model to score trajectories based on features aligned with that axis while de-emphasizing context that is unrelated to the stated reason. Because the same rationales (e.g., "avoids collisions", "completes the task faster") can appear across multiple tasks, ReCouPLe naturally reuses the same causal direction whenever tasks share semantics, and transfers preference knowledge to novel tasks without extra data or language-model fine-tuning. Our learned reward model can ground preferences on the articulated reason, aligning better with user intent and generalizing beyond spurious features. ReCouPLe outperforms baselines by up to 1.5x in reward accuracy under distribution shifts, and 2x in downstream policy performance in novel tasks. We have released our code at https://github.com/mj-hwang/ReCouPLe

摘要（中文）: 基于偏好的奖励学习被广泛用于塑造智能体的行为以匹配用户的偏好，但其稀疏的二元反馈使其特别容易受到因果混淆的影响。学习到的奖励往往会锁定在虚假特征上，这些特征仅仅在训练期间与偏好轨迹共同出现，当这些相关性在测试时消失或反转时，奖励就会失效。我们引入了ReCouPLe，一个轻量级框架，利用自然语言理由来提供缺失的因果信号。每个理由都被视为嵌入空间中的一个引导投影轴，训练模型根据与该轴对齐的特征来对轨迹进行评分，同时淡化与所述理由无关的上下文。由于相同的理由（例如，“避免碰撞”，“更快地完成任务”）可以出现在多个任务中，因此ReCouPLe会在任务共享语义时自然地重用相同的因果方向，并将偏好知识转移到新的任务，而无需额外的数据或语言模型的微调。我们学习到的奖励模型可以将偏好建立在明确表达的理由之上，更好地与用户意图对齐，并推广到虚假特征之外。在分布偏移下，ReCouPLe在奖励准确性方面比基线方法高出1.5倍，在新任务中的下游策略性能方面高出2倍。我们已在https://github.com/mj-hwang/ReCouPLe发布了我们的代码。

TLDR: The paper introduces ReCouPLe, a framework for causally robust reward learning using natural language rationales to guide preference learning and improve generalization in reinforcement learning tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ReCouPLe，一个利用自然语言推理增强因果鲁棒性奖励学习的框架，通过自然语言推理指导偏好学习，并提升强化学习任务中的泛化能力。

Authors: Minjune Hwang, Yigit Korkmaz, Daniel Seita, Erdem Bıyık

Hyperbolic Multiview Pretraining for Robotic Manipulation

Abstract (English): 3D-aware visual pretraining has proven effective in improving the performance of downstream robotic manipulation tasks. However, existing methods are constrained to Euclidean embedding spaces, whose flat geometry limits their ability to model structural relations among embeddings. As a result, they struggle to learn structured embeddings that are essential for robust spatial perception in robotic applications. To this end, we propose HyperMVP, a self-supervised framework for \underline{Hyper}bolic \underline{M}ulti\underline{V}iew \underline{P}retraining. Hyperbolic space offers geometric properties well suited for capturing structural relations. Methodologically, we extend the masked autoencoder paradigm and design a GeoLink encoder to learn multiview hyperbolic representations. The pretrained encoder is then finetuned with visuomotor policies on manipulation tasks. In addition, we introduce 3D-MOV, a large-scale dataset comprising multiple types of 3D point clouds to support pretraining. We evaluate HyperMVP on COLOSSEUM, RLBench, and real-world scenarios, where it consistently outperforms strong baselines across diverse tasks and perturbation settings. Our results highlight the potential of 3D-aware pretraining in a non-Euclidean space for learning robust and generalizable robotic manipulation policies.

摘要（中文）: 3D 感知视觉预训练已被证明能够有效提升下游机器人操作任务的性能。然而，现有方法受限于欧几里得嵌入空间，其扁平几何结构限制了建模嵌入之间结构关系的能力。因此，它们难以学习结构化嵌入，而结构化嵌入对于机器人应用中稳健的空间感知至关重要。为此，我们提出 HyperMVP，一种用于双曲多视图预训练的自监督框架。双曲空间提供了非常适合捕捉结构关系的几何属性。在方法论上，我们扩展了掩码自编码器范式，并设计了一个 GeoLink 编码器来学习多视图双曲表示。然后，使用视觉运动策略在操作任务上对预训练编码器进行微调。此外，我们引入了 3D-MOV，一个包含多种 3D 点云类型的大规模数据集，以支持预训练。我们在 COLOSSEUM、RLBench 和真实世界场景中评估了 HyperMVP，在各种任务和扰动设置下，它始终优于强大的基线方法。我们的结果突出了在非欧几里得空间进行 3D 感知预训练，以学习稳健且可泛化的机器人操作策略的潜力。

TLDR: This paper introduces HyperMVP, a self-supervised framework for pretraining robotic manipulation policies in hyperbolic space, leveraging a new dataset (3D-MOV) and demonstrating improved performance on various benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了HyperMVP，一个在双曲空间中预训练机器人操作策略的自监督框架，利用了一个新的数据集（3D-MOV），并在多个基准测试中表现出改进的性能。

Authors: Jin Yang, Ping Wei, Yixin Chen

On the Strengths and Weaknesses of Data for Open-set Embodied Assistance

Abstract (English): Embodied foundation models are increasingly performant in real-world domains such as robotics or autonomous driving. These models are often deployed in interactive or assistive settings, where it is important that these assistive models generalize to new users and new tasks. Diverse interactive data generation offers a promising avenue for providing data-efficient generalization capabilities for interactive embodied foundation models. In this paper, we investigate the generalization capabilities of a multimodal foundation model fine-tuned on diverse interactive assistance data in a synthetic domain. We explore generalization along two axes: a) assistance with unseen categories of user behavior and b) providing guidance in new configurations not encountered during training. We study a broad capability called \textbf{Open-Set Corrective Assistance}, in which the model needs to inspect lengthy user behavior and provide assistance through either corrective actions or language-based feedback. This task remains unsolved in prior work, which typically assumes closed corrective categories or relies on external planners, making it a challenging testbed for evaluating the limits of assistive data. To support this task, we generate synthetic assistive datasets in Overcooked and fine-tune a LLaMA-based model to evaluate generalization to novel tasks and user behaviors. Our approach provides key insights into the nature of assistive datasets required to enable open-set assistive intelligence. In particular, we show that performant models benefit from datasets that cover different aspects of assistance, including multimodal grounding, defect inference, and exposure to diverse scenarios.

摘要（中文）: 具身基础模型在机器人或自动驾驶等现实世界领域中的性能日益提升。这些模型通常部署在交互式或辅助性环境中，因此辅助模型能泛化到新的用户和新的任务至关重要。多样化的交互数据生成为交互式具身基础模型提供数据高效的泛化能力提供了一个有前景的途径。在本文中，我们研究了一个在合成领域中基于多样化交互辅助数据微调的多模态基础模型的泛化能力。我们沿着两个维度探索泛化：a) 对未见类别的用户行为的辅助，以及 b) 在训练期间未遇到的新配置中提供指导。我们研究了一种称为\textbf{开放集纠正性辅助}的广泛能力，其中模型需要检查冗长的用户行为，并通过纠正性动作或基于语言的反馈来提供辅助。这项任务在先前的工作中仍未解决，这些工作通常假设封闭的纠正类别或依赖于外部规划器，因此它成为了评估辅助数据限制的一个具有挑战性的试验平台。为了支持这项任务，我们在 Overcooked 中生成合成辅助数据集，并微调一个基于 LLaMA 的模型，以评估其对新任务和用户行为的泛化能力。我们的方法为实现开放集辅助智能所需的辅助数据集的性质提供了关键见解。特别是，我们表明性能优越的模型受益于涵盖辅助不同方面的数据集，包括多模态基础、缺陷推断和暴露于各种场景。

TLDR: This paper explores using diverse, interactive data to improve the generalization capabilities of multimodal foundation models for open-set corrective assistance in embodied environments, specifically in a synthetic Overcooked environment using a LLaMA-based model.

简要说明: 本文研究了使用多样化、交互式数据来提高多模态基础模型在具身环境中进行开放式纠正辅助的泛化能力，具体来说是在一个合成的 Overcooked 环境中使用基于 LLaMA 的模型。

Authors: Pradyumna Tambwekar, Andrew Silva, Deepak Gopinath, Jonathan DeCastro, Xiongyi Cui, Guy Rosman

Diffusion Policy through Conditional Proximal Policy Optimization

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning (RL) has been extensively employed in a wide range of decision-making problems, such as games and robotics. Recently, diffusion policies have shown strong potential in modeling multi-modal behaviors, enabling more diverse and flexible action generation compared to the conventional Gaussian policy. Despite various attempts to combine RL with diffusion, a key challenge is the difficulty of computing action log-likelihood under the diffusion model. This greatly hinders the direct application of diffusion policies in on-policy reinforcement learning. Most existing methods calculate or approximate the log-likelihood through the entire denoising process in the diffusion model, which can be memory- and computationally inefficient. To overcome this challenge, we propose a novel and efficient method to train a diffusion policy in an on-policy setting that requires only evaluating a simple Gaussian probability. This is achieved by aligning the policy iteration with the diffusion process, which is a distinct paradigm compared to previous work. Moreover, our formulation can naturally handle entropy regularization, which is often difficult to incorporate into diffusion policies. Experiments demonstrate that the proposed method produces multimodal policy behaviors and achieves superior performance on a variety of benchmark tasks in both IsaacLab and MuJoCo Playground.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习（RL）已被广泛应用于各种决策问题中，如游戏和机器人学。最近，扩散策略在建模多模态行为方面展现出强大的潜力，与传统的 Gaussian 策略相比，能够实现更多样化和灵活的动作生成。尽管已经尝试将强化学习与扩散相结合，但一个关键挑战在于难以计算扩散模型下的动作对数似然。这极大地阻碍了扩散策略在同策略强化学习中的直接应用。现有的大多数方法通过扩散模型中的整个去噪过程来计算或近似对数似然，这可能会导致内存和计算效率低下。为了克服这一挑战，我们提出了一种新颖且高效的方法，在同策略设置下训练扩散策略，而只需要评估一个简单的 Gaussian 概率。这通过将策略迭代与扩散过程对齐来实现，这是一种与先前工作截然不同的范式。此外，我们的公式可以自然地处理熵正则化，这通常难以融入到扩散策略中。实验表明，所提出的方法可以产生多模态的策略行为，并在 IsaacLab 和 MuJoCo Playground 中的各种基准任务上实现卓越的性能。

TLDR: This paper presents a novel on-policy reinforcement learning method using diffusion policies, addressing the computational inefficiency of log-likelihood calculation through a new alignment strategy requiring only Gaussian probability evaluation. The method handles entropy regularization naturally and demonstrates superior performance on benchmark tasks.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种新的基于扩散策略的on-policy强化学习方法，通过一种新的对齐策略解决了计算对数似然时的计算效率问题，该策略仅需评估高斯概率。该方法可以自然地处理熵正则化，并在基准任务上表现出卓越的性能。

Authors: Ben Liu, Shunpeng Yang, Hua Chen

LLM-Guided Decentralized Exploration with Self-Organizing Robot Teams

Abstract (English): When individual robots have limited sensing capabilities or insufficient fault tolerance, it becomes necessary for multiple robots to form teams during exploration, thereby increasing the collective observation range and reliability. Traditionally, swarm formation has often been managed by a central controller; however, from the perspectives of robustness and flexibility, it is preferable for the swarm to operate autonomously even in the absence of centralized control. In addition, the determination of exploration targets for each team is crucial for efficient exploration in such multi-team exploration scenarios. This study therefore proposes an exploration method that combines (1) an algorithm for self-organization, enabling the autonomous and dynamic formation of multiple teams, and (2) an algorithm that allows each team to autonomously determine its next exploration target (destination). In particular, for (2), this study explores a novel strategy based on large language models (LLMs), while classical frontier-based methods and deep reinforcement learning approaches have been widely studied. The effectiveness of the proposed method was validated through simulations involving tens to hundreds of robots.

摘要（中文）: 当单个机器人感知能力有限或容错性不足时，有必要由多个机器人组队进行探索，从而扩大整体观测范围并提高可靠性。传统上，群体队形通常由中央控制器管理；然而，从鲁棒性和灵活性的角度来看，群体最好在没有集中控制的情况下也能自主运行。此外，在这样的多团队探索场景中，确定每个团队的探索目标对于高效探索至关重要。因此，本研究提出了一种结合以下两种算法的探索方法：（1）一种实现自主和动态组建多个团队的自组织算法，以及（2）一种允许每个团队自主确定其下一个探索目标（目的地）的算法。特别地，对于（2），本研究探索了一种基于大型语言模型（LLM）的新策略，而经典的基于边界的方法和深度强化学习方法已被广泛研究。通过涉及数十到数百个机器人的仿真验证了所提出方法的有效性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a decentralized multi-robot exploration method guided by LLMs for target selection, enabling autonomous team formation and efficient exploration without centralized control.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种由LLM引导的去中心化多机器人探索方法，该方法通过LLM进行目标选择，能够实现自主组队和高效探索，无需中央控制。

Authors: Hiroaki Kawashima, Shun Ikejima, Takeshi Takai, Mikita Miyaguchi, Yasuharu Kunii

Design, Mapping, and Contact Anticipation with 3D-printed Whole-Body Tactile and Proximity Sensors

Abstract (English): Robots operating in dynamic and shared environments benefit from anticipating contact before it occurs. We present GenTact-Prox, a fully 3D-printed artificial skin that integrates tactile and proximity sensing for contact detection and anticipation. The artificial skin platform is modular in design, procedurally generated to fit any robot morphology, and can cover the whole body of a robot. The skin achieved detection ranges of up to 18 cm during evaluation. To characterize how robots perceive nearby space through this skin, we introduce a data-driven framework for mapping the Perisensory Space -- the body-centric volume of space around the robot where sensors provide actionable information for contact anticipation. We demonstrate this approach on a Franka Research 3 robot equipped with five GenTact-Prox units, enabling online object-aware operation and contact prediction.

摘要（中文）: 在动态和共享环境中运行的机器人受益于提前预测接触的发生。我们提出GenTact-Prox，一种完全3D打印的人工皮肤，集成了触觉和接近觉传感，用于接触检测和预测。该人工皮肤平台采用模块化设计，可程序化生成以适应任何机器人形态，并可覆盖机器人的整个身体。在评估过程中，该皮肤实现了高达18厘米的检测范围。为了表征机器人如何通过该皮肤感知周围空间，我们引入了一个数据驱动框架，用于映射周身感知空间（Perisensory Space）-- 以机器人为中心的体积空间，其中传感器提供可操作的信息以进行接触预测。我们在一台配备五个GenTact-Prox单元的Franka Research 3机器人上演示了这种方法，实现了在线、对象感知的操作和接触预测。

TLDR: This paper introduces GenTact-Prox, a 3D-printed artificial skin with tactile and proximity sensing for whole-body robot coverage, enabling contact anticipation and object-aware operation.

Authors: Carson Kohlbrenner, Anna Soukhovei, Caleb Escobedo, Nataliya Nechyporenko, Alessandro Roncone

LEGS-POMDP: Language and Gesture-Guided Object Search in Partially Observable Environments

Abstract (English): To assist humans in open-world environments, robots must interpret ambiguous instructions to locate desired objects. Foundation model-based approaches excel at multimodal grounding, but they lack a principled mechanism for modeling uncertainty in long-horizon tasks. In contrast, Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes (POMDPs) provide a systematic framework for planning under uncertainty but are often limited in supported modalities and rely on restrictive environment assumptions. We introduce LanguagE and Gesture-Guided Object Search in Partially Observable Environments (LEGS-POMDP), a modular POMDP system that integrates language, gesture, and visual observations for open-world object search. Unlike prior work, LEGS-POMDP explicitly models two sources of partial observability: uncertainty over the target object's identity and its spatial location. In simulation, multimodal fusion significantly outperforms unimodal baselines, achieving an average success rate of 89\% across challenging environments and object categories. Finally, we demonstrate the full system on a quadruped mobile manipulator, where real-world experiments qualitatively validate robust multimodal perception and uncertainty reduction under ambiguous instructions.

摘要（中文）: 为了辅助人类在开放世界环境中工作，机器人必须能够解读含糊的指令以定位期望的目标物体。基于通用模型的方案在多模态信息关联方面表现出色，但缺乏在长时程任务中对不确定性进行建模的有效机制。相比之下，部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDPs）为不确定性下的规划提供了一个系统的框架，但其支持的模态类型通常有限，且依赖于严格的环境假设。我们引入了基于语言和手势引导的部分可观测环境下的物体搜索（LEGS-POMDP），这是一个模块化的POMDP系统，集成了语言、手势和视觉观测，用于开放世界中的物体搜索。与以往工作不同，LEGS-POMDP显式地对两种部分可观测性的来源进行建模：目标物体身份的不确定性和其空间位置的不确定性。在仿真环境中，多模态融合显著优于单模态基线，在具有挑战性的环境和物体类别中，平均成功率达到89%。最后，我们在一个四足移动机械臂上演示了完整的系统，真实世界的实验定性验证了在含糊指令下稳健的多模态感知和不确定性降低。

TLDR: The paper introduces LEGS-POMDP, a POMDP-based system that integrates language, gesture, and visual observations for object search in partially observable environments, demonstrating its effectiveness in simulation and on a quadruped robot.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了LEGS-POMDP，一个基于POMDP的系统，集成了语言、手势和视觉观察，用于在部分可观察的环境中进行物体搜索，并在模拟和四足机器人上证明了其有效性。

Authors: Ivy Xiao He, Stefanie Tellex, Jason Xinyu Liu

Risk-Aware Reinforcement Learning for Mobile Manipulation

Abstract (English): For robots to successfully transition from lab settings to everyday environments, they must begin to reason about the risks associated with their actions and make informed, risk-aware decisions. This is particularly true for robots performing mobile manipulation tasks, which involve both interacting with and navigating within dynamic, unstructured spaces. However, existing whole-body controllers for mobile manipulators typically lack explicit mechanisms for risk-sensitive decision-making under uncertainty. To our knowledge, we are the first to (i) learn risk-aware visuomotor policies for mobile manipulation conditioned on egocentric depth observations with runtime-adjustable risk sensitivity, and (ii) show risk-aware behaviours can be transferred through Imitation Learning (IL) to a visuomotor policy conditioned on egocentric depth observations. Our method achieves this by first training a privileged teacher policy using Distributional Reinforcement Learning (DRL), with a risk-neutral distributional critic. Distortion risk-metrics are then applied to the critic's predicted return distribution to calculate risk-adjusted advantage estimates used in policy updates to achieve a range of risk-aware behaviours. We then distil teacher policies with IL to obtain risk-aware student policies conditioned on egocentric depth observations. We perform extensive evaluations demonstrating that our trained visuomotor policies exhibit risk-aware behaviour (specifically achieving better worst-case performance) while performing reactive whole-body motions in unmapped environments, leveraging live depth observations for perception.

摘要（中文）: 为了使机器人能够成功地从实验室环境过渡到日常环境，它们必须开始推理其行动相关的风险，并做出知情的、具有风险意识的决策。对于执行移动操作任务的机器人来说尤其如此，这些任务既涉及与动态、非结构化空间交互，又涉及在其中导航。然而，现有的移动操作器全身控制器通常缺乏在不确定性下进行风险敏感决策的显式机制。据我们所知，我们是第一个 (i) 学习基于以自我为中心的深度观测，并具有运行时可调的风险敏感性的移动操作风险感知视觉运动策略的，以及 (ii) 展示风险感知行为可以通过模仿学习 (IL) 迁移到基于以自我为中心的深度观测的视觉运动策略的。我们的方法首先使用具有风险中性的分布评论家的分布强化学习 (DRL) 训练一个特权教师策略。然后，将失真风险度量应用于评论家预测的回报分布，以计算风险调整优势估计，用于策略更新，从而实现一系列风险感知行为。接下来，我们通过模仿学习将教师策略提炼，以获得基于以自我为中心的深度观测的风险感知学生策略。我们进行了广泛的评估，证明我们训练的视觉运动策略展现出风险感知行为（特别是实现了更好的最坏情况性能），同时在未映射环境中执行反应式全身运动，利用实时深度观测进行感知。

TLDR: This paper introduces a risk-aware reinforcement learning method for mobile manipulation, using distributional RL and imitation learning to train visuomotor policies that perform well in unmapped environments, especially in worst-case scenarios.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种用于移动操作的风险感知强化学习方法，使用分布强化学习和模仿学习来训练视觉运动策略，该策略在未映射的环境中表现良好，尤其是在最坏情况下。

Authors: Michael Groom, James Wilson, Nick Hawes, Lars Kunze

From Local Corrections to Generalized Skills: Improving Neuro-Symbolic Policies with MEMO

Abstract (English): Recent works use a neuro-symbolic framework for general manipulation policies. The advantage of this framework is that -- by applying off-the-shelf vision and language models -- the robot can break complex tasks down into semantic subtasks. However, the fundamental bottleneck is that the robot needs skills to ground these subtasks into embodied motions. Skills can take many forms (e.g., trajectory snippets, motion primitives, coded functions), but regardless of their form skills act as a constraint. The high-level policy can only ground its language reasoning through the available skills; if the robot cannot generate the right skill for the current task, its policy will fail. We propose to address this limitation -- and dynamically expand the robot's skills -- by leveraging user feedback. When a robot fails, humans can intuitively explain what went wrong (e.g., ``no, go higher''). While a simple approach is to recall this exact text the next time the robot faces a similar situation, we hypothesize that by collecting, clustering, and re-phrasing natural language corrections across multiple users and tasks, we can synthesize more general text guidance and coded skill templates. Applying this hypothesis we develop Memory Enhanced Manipulation (MEMO). MEMO builds and maintains a retrieval-augmented skillbook gathered from human feedback and task successes. At run time, MEMO retrieves relevant text and code from this skillbook, enabling the robot's policy to generate new skills while reasoning over multi-task human feedback. Our experiments demonstrate that using MEMO to aggregate local feedback into general skill templates enables generalization to novel tasks where existing baselines fall short. See supplemental material here: https://collab.me.vt.edu/memo

摘要（中文）: 近期工作采用神经符号框架来实现通用操作策略。该框架的优势在于——通过应用现成的视觉和语言模型——机器人可以将复杂任务分解为语义子任务。然而，根本瓶颈在于机器人需要技能来将这些子任务转化为具身运动。技能可以采取多种形式（例如，轨迹片段、运动原语、编码函数），但无论其形式如何，技能都作为一种约束。高层策略只能通过现有技能来实现其语言推理；如果机器人无法为当前任务生成正确的技能，其策略将失败。我们提出通过利用用户反馈来解决此限制——并动态扩展机器人的技能。当机器人失败时，人类可以直观地解释出错的原因（例如，“不，再高一点”）。虽然一种简单的方法是在下次机器人遇到类似情况时回忆起这段确切的文本，但我们假设，通过收集、聚类和改写多个用户和任务的自然语言更正，我们可以合成更通用的文本指导和编码技能模板。应用这一假设，我们开发了记忆增强操作(MEMO)。MEMO构建并维护一个从人类反馈和任务成功中收集的检索增强技能书。在运行时，MEMO从该技能书中检索相关的文本和代码，使得机器人的策略能够在推理多任务人类反馈的同时生成新的技能。我们的实验表明，使用MEMO将局部反馈聚合到通用技能模板中能够推广到现有基线方法无法胜任的新任务。 请参见辅助材料：https://collab.me.vt.edu/memo

TLDR: The paper introduces MEMO, a neuro-symbolic framework that leverages human feedback to dynamically expand robot skills by collecting, clustering, and re-phrasing natural language corrections to synthesize generalized skill templates, enabling better generalization to novel manipulation tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了MEMO，一种神经符号框架，通过收集、聚类和改述自然语言修正，利用人类反馈动态扩展机器人技能，合成通用技能模板，从而更好地泛化到新的操作任务。

Authors: Benjamin A. Christie, Yinlong Dai, Mohammad Bararjanianbahnamiri, Simon Stepputtis, Dylan P. Losey

ManipulationNet: An Infrastructure for Benchmarking Real-World Robot Manipulation with Physical Skill Challenges and Embodied Multimodal Reasoning

Abstract (English): Dexterous manipulation enables robots to purposefully alter the physical world, transforming them from passive observers into active agents in unstructured environments. This capability is the cornerstone of physical artificial intelligence. Despite decades of advances in hardware, perception, control, and learning, progress toward general manipulation systems remains fragmented due to the absence of widely adopted standard benchmarks. The central challenge lies in reconciling the variability of the real world with the reproducibility and authenticity required for rigorous scientific evaluation. To address this, we introduce ManipulationNet, a global infrastructure that hosts real-world benchmark tasks for robotic manipulation. ManipulationNet delivers reproducible task setups through standardized hardware kits, and enables distributed performance evaluation via a unified software client that delivers real-time task instructions and collects benchmarking results. As a persistent and scalable infrastructure, ManipulationNet organizes benchmark tasks into two complementary tracks: 1) the Physical Skills Track, which evaluates low-level physical interaction skills, and 2) the Embodied Reasoning Track, which tests high-level reasoning and multimodal grounding abilities. This design fosters the systematic growth of an interconnected network of real-world abilities and skills, paving the path toward general robotic manipulation. By enabling comparable manipulation research in the real world at scale, this infrastructure establishes a sustainable foundation for measuring long-term scientific progress and identifying capabilities ready for real-world deployment.

摘要（中文）: 灵巧操作使机器人能够有目的地改变物理世界，将其从被动观察者转变为非结构化环境中的主动代理，而这正是物理人工智能的基石。尽管在硬件、感知、控制和学习方面取得了数十年的进步，但由于缺乏广泛采用的标准基准，通用操作系统的进展仍然分散。核心挑战在于如何将现实世界的变异性与严格科学评估所需的重现性和真实性相协调。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了ManipulationNet，一个托管机器人操作的真实世界基准任务的全球基础设施。ManipulationNet通过标准化的硬件套件提供可重复的任务设置，并通过统一的软件客户端实现分布式性能评估，该客户端提供实时的任务指令并收集基准测试结果。作为一个持久且可扩展的基础设施，ManipulationNet将基准任务组织成两个互补的轨道：1) 物理技能轨道，评估低级别的物理交互技能；2) 具身推理轨道，测试高级别的推理和多模态语境能力。这种设计促进了一个相互关联的真实世界能力和技能网络的系统性增长，为通用机器人操作铺平了道路。通过实现大规模的真实世界可比操作研究，该基础设施为衡量长期科学进展并识别适合真实世界部署的能力奠定了可持续的基础。

Adelson, Tamim Asfour, Podshara Chanrungmaneekul, Sachin Chitta, Yash Chitambar, Ziyang Chen, Ken Goldberg, Danica Kragic, Hui Li, Xiang Li, Yunzhu Li, Aaron Prather, Nancy Pollard, Maximo A. Tendon Force Modeling for Sim2Real Transfer of Reinforcement Learning Policies for Tendon-Driven Robots

Abstract (English): Robots which make use of soft or compliant inter- actions often leverage tendon-driven actuation which enables actuators to be placed more flexibly, and compliance to be maintained. However, controlling complex tendon systems is challenging. Simulation paired with reinforcement learning (RL) could be enable more complex behaviors to be generated. Such methods rely on torque and force-based simulation roll- outs which are limited by the sim-to-real gap, stemming from the actuator and system dynamics, resulting in poor transfer of RL policies onto real robots. To address this, we propose a method to model the tendon forces produced by typical servo motors, focusing specifically on the transfer of RL policies for a tendon driven finger. Our approach extends existing data- driven techniques by leveraging contextual history and a novel data collection test-bench. This test-bench allows us to capture tendon forces undergo contact-rich interactions typical of real- world manipulation. We then utilize our force estimation model in a GPU-accelerated tendon force-driven rigid body simulation to train RL-based controllers. Our transformer-based model is capable of predicting tendon forces within 3% of the maximum motor force and is robot-agnostic. By integrating our learned model into simulation, we reduce the sim-to-real gap for test trajectories by 41%. RL-based controller trained with our model achieves a 50% improvement in fingertip pose tracking tasks on real tendon-driven robotic fingers. This approach is generalizable to different actuators and robot systems, and can enable RL policies to be used widely across tendon systems, advancing capabilities of dexterous manipulators and soft robots.

摘要（中文）: 利用柔性或顺应交互的机器人通常采用腱驱动方式，这使得驱动器可以更灵活地放置并保持顺应性。然而，控制复杂的腱系统具有挑战性。与强化学习（RL）相结合的仿真可以生成更复杂的行为。这类方法依赖于基于扭矩和力的仿真推演，但受限于仿真到真实（sim-to-real）的差距，该差距源于驱动器和系统动力学，导致RL策略在真实机器人上的迁移效果不佳。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种方法来模拟典型伺服电机产生的腱力，特别关注腱驱动手指的RL策略迁移。我们的方法通过利用上下文历史信息和一种新颖的数据采集测试平台来扩展现有的数据驱动技术。该测试平台使我们能够捕获经历富含接触的交互的腱力，这在真实世界的操纵中很常见。然后，我们利用力估计模型在GPU加速的腱力驱动刚体仿真中训练基于RL的控制器。我们的基于Transformer的模型能够预测最大电机力3%范围内的腱力，并且与机器人无关。通过将我们学习的模型集成到仿真中，我们将测试轨迹的仿真到真实差距减少了41%。使用我们的模型训练的基于RL的控制器在真实腱驱动机器人手指上，于指尖姿态跟踪任务中实现了50%的改进。这种方法可以推广到不同的驱动器和机器人系统，并能够使RL策略广泛应用于腱系统，从而提高灵巧机械臂和软体机器人的能力。

TLDR: This paper presents a method to model tendon forces for improved sim-to-real transfer of RL policies in tendon-driven robots, achieving significant performance gains in real-world tasks. It leverages a transformer-based model for force prediction and a data-driven method in simulation.

Authors: Valentin Yuryev, Josie Hughes

STRUCTUREDAGENT: Planning with AND/OR Trees for Long-Horizon Web Tasks

Abstract (English): Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have enabled agentic systems for sequential decision-making. Such agents must perceive their environment, reason across multiple time steps, and take actions that optimize long-term objectives. However, existing web agents struggle on complex, long-horizon tasks due to limited in-context memory for tracking history, weak planning abilities, and greedy behaviors that lead to premature termination. To address these challenges, we propose STRUCTUREDAGENT, a hierarchical planning framework with two core components: (1) an online hierarchical planner that uses dynamic AND/OR trees for efficient search and (2) a structured memory module that tracks and maintains candidate solutions to improve constraint satisfaction in information-seeking tasks. The framework also produces interpretable hierarchical plans, enabling easier debugging and facilitating human intervention when needed. Our results on WebVoyager, WebArena, and custom shopping benchmarks show that STRUCTUREDAGENT improves performance on long-horizon web-browsing tasks compared to standard LLM-based agents.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLMs）的最新进展推动了用于序列决策的主体系统的发展。此类主体必须感知其环境，在多个时间步长上进行推理，并采取行动以优化长期目标。然而，现有的Web主体在复杂、长时程任务中表现不佳，原因在于其有限的上下文记忆用于追踪历史、较弱的规划能力以及导致过早终止的贪婪行为。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了STRUCTUREDAGENT，一个分层规划框架，包含两个核心组件：（1）一个在线分层规划器，利用动态与/或树进行高效搜索，以及（2）一个结构化记忆模块，用于跟踪和维护候选解决方案，从而提高信息搜索任务中的约束满足度。该框架还生成可解释的分层计划，简化调试并促进必要时的人工干预。我们在WebVoyager、WebArena和自定义购物基准测试上的结果表明，与标准的基于LLM的主体相比，STRUCTUREDAGENT提高了长时程Web浏览任务的性能。

TLDR: STRUCTUREDAGENT is a hierarchical planning framework using AND/OR trees and structured memory to improve LLM-based web agents on long-horizon tasks, demonstrating better performance on web-browsing benchmarks.

简要说明: STRUCTUREDAGENT是一个分层规划框架，使用AND/OR树和结构化内存来改进基于LLM的Web代理在长时程任务上的表现，并在Web浏览基准测试中显示出更好的性能。

Authors: ELita Lobo, Xu Chen, Jingjing Meng, Nan Xi, Yang Jiao, Chirag Agarwal, Yair Zick, Yan Gao

KARL: Knowledge Agents via Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): We present a system for training enterprise search agents via reinforcement learning that achieves state-of-the-art performance across a diverse suite of hard-to-verify agentic search tasks. Our work makes four core contributions. First, we introduce KARLBench, a multi-capability evaluation suite spanning six distinct search regimes, including constraint-driven entity search, cross-document report synthesis, tabular numerical reasoning, exhaustive entity retrieval, procedural reasoning over technical documentation, and fact aggregation over internal enterprise notes. Second, we show that models trained across heterogeneous search behaviors generalize substantially better than those optimized for any single benchmark. Third, we develop an agentic synthesis pipeline that employs long-horizon reasoning and tool use to generate diverse, grounded, and high-quality training data, with iterative bootstrapping from increasingly capable models. Fourth, we propose a new post-training paradigm based on iterative large-batch off-policy RL that is sample efficient, robust to train-inference engine discrepancies, and naturally extends to multi-task training with out-of-distribution generalization. Compared to Claude 4.6 and GPT 5.2, KARL is Pareto-optimal on KARLBench across cost-quality and latency-quality trade-offs, including tasks that were out-of-distribution during training. With sufficient test-time compute, it surpasses the strongest closed models. These results show that tailored synthetic data in combination with multi-task reinforcement learning enables cost-efficient and high-performing knowledge agents for grounded reasoning.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了一种通过强化学习训练企业搜索代理的系统，该系统在一套多样化的、难以验证的代理搜索任务中实现了最先进的性能。我们的工作主要有四个方面的贡献。首先，我们引入了KARLBench，一个多功能评估套件，涵盖六个不同的搜索模式，包括约束驱动的实体搜索、跨文档报告合成、表格数值推理、穷举式实体检索、技术文档上的程序推理以及对内部企业注释的事实聚合。其次，我们表明，在异构搜索行为上训练的模型比针对任何单一基准优化过的模型具有更好的泛化能力。第三，我们开发了一个代理合成流水线，该流水线采用长程推理和工具使用来生成多样化、有依据且高质量的训练数据，并通过能力越来越强的模型进行迭代引导。第四，我们提出了一种新的后训练范例，该范例基于迭代的大批量离策略强化学习，该方法具有样本效率高、对训练-推理引擎差异的鲁棒性好，并且自然地扩展到具有分布外泛化的多任务训练。与Claude 4.6和GPT 5.2相比，KARL在KARLBench上实现了帕累托最优，在成本-质量和延迟-质量的权衡中表现出色，包括训练期间属于分布外的任务。在有足够的测试时计算资源的情况下，它可以超越最强大的封闭模型。这些结果表明，定制的合成数据与多任务强化学习相结合，可以为基于知识的推理提供经济高效且高性能的知识代理。

TLDR: The paper introduces KARL, a reinforcement learning system for training enterprise search agents, achieving state-of-the-art performance on a new benchmark (KARLBench) and demonstrating strong generalization capabilities through tailored synthetic data and multi-task RL.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 KARL，一个用于训练企业搜索代理的强化学习系统，在新的基准测试 (KARLBench) 上实现了最先进的性能，并通过定制的合成数据和多任务 RL 展示了强大的泛化能力。

Authors: Jonathan D. Chang, Andrew Drozdov, Shubham Toshniwal, Owen Oertell, Alexander Trott, Jacob Portes, Abhay Gupta, Pallavi Koppol, Ashutosh Baheti, Sean Kulinski, Ivan Zhou, Irene Dea, Krista Opsahl-Ong, Simon Favreau-Lessard, Sean Owen, Jose Javier Gonzalez Ortiz, Arnav Singhvi, Xabi Andrade, Cindy Wang, Kartik Sreenivasan, Sam Havens, Jialu Liu, Peyton DeNiro, Wen Sun, Michael Bendersky, Jonathan Frankle

WebFactory: Automated Compression of Foundational Language Intelligence into Grounded Web Agents

Abstract (English): Current paradigms for training GUI agents are fundamentally limited by a reliance on either unsafe, non-reproducible live web interactions or costly, scarce human-crafted data and environments. We argue this focus on data volume overlooks a more critical factor: the efficiency of compressing a large language model's (LLM) latent knowledge into actionable agent behavior. We introduce WebFactory, a novel, fully automated closed-loop reinforcement learning pipeline for GUI agents, systematically compressing LLM-encoded internet intelligence into efficient, grounded actions. Our pipeline features a process of scalable environment synthesis, knowledge-aware task generation, LLM-powered trajectory collection, decomposed reward RL training, and systematic agent evaluation. Remarkably, our agent demonstrates exceptional data efficiency and generalization. Trained on synthetic data from only 10 websites within WebFactory, it achieves performance comparable to GUI agents trained on the same amount of human-annotated data from a much larger set of environments. This superior performance is consistent across our internal offline and online transfer benchmarks, where our agent also significantly outperforms the base foundation model. We further provide critical insights into the "embodiment potential" of different LLM foundations, offering a new axis for model evaluation. This work presents a scalable and cost-effective paradigm for transforming passive internet knowledge into active, grounded intelligence, marking a critical step towards general-purpose interactive agents.

摘要（中文）: 目前GUI代理的训练范式从根本上受到依赖不安全、不可复现的实时网络交互或代价高昂、稀缺的人工数据和环境的限制。我们认为，这种对数据量的关注忽略了一个更关键的因素：将大型语言模型（LLM）的潜在知识压缩为可操作的代理行为的效率。我们引入了WebFactory，一种新颖的、完全自动化的闭环强化学习流水线，用于GUI代理，该流水线系统地将LLM编码的互联网智能压缩为高效、基于上下文的行为。我们的流水线包含可扩展的环境合成、知识感知的任务生成、LLM驱动的轨迹收集、分解式奖励的强化学习训练以及系统性的代理评估流程。值得注意的是，我们的代理展现出了卓越的数据效率和泛化能力。仅使用WebFactory中来自10个网站的合成数据进行训练，即可达到与使用来自更大集合环境的相同数量的人工标注数据训练的GUI代理相当的性能。这种卓越的性能在我们内部的离线和在线迁移基准测试中是一致的，在这些测试中，我们的代理也显著优于基础模型。我们进一步提供了关于不同LLM基础模型的“具身潜力”的关键见解，为模型评估提供了一个新的维度。这项工作提出了一种可扩展且经济高效的范式，将被动互联网知识转化为主动、基于上下文的智能，标志着朝着通用交互式代理迈出了关键一步。

TLDR: The paper introduces WebFactory, an automated reinforcement learning pipeline that efficiently compresses LLM knowledge into grounded web agent actions, achieving comparable performance to human-annotated data with significantly less training data and highlighting a new axis for LLM evaluation: embodiment potential.
