Authors: Sicheng Fan, Qingyun Shi, Shengze Xu, Shengbo Cai, Tieyong Zeng, Li Ling, Yanyi Shang, Dehan Kong

3D-RFT: Reinforcement Fine-Tuning for Video-based 3D Scene Understanding

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards ( RLVR ) has emerged as a transformative paradigm for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models ( LLMs), yet its potential in 3D scene understanding remains under-explored. Existing approaches largely rely on Supervised Fine-Tuning ( SFT), where the token-level cross-entropy loss acts as an indirect proxy for optimization, leading to a misalignment between training objectives and task performances. To bridge this gap, we present Reinforcement Fine-Tuning for Video-based 3D Scene Understanding (3D-RFT ), the first framework to extend RLVR to video-based 3D perception and reasoning. 3D-RFT shifts the paradigm by directly optimizing the model towards evaluation metrics. 3D-RFT first activates 3D-aware Multi-modal Large Language Models ( MLLM s) via SFT, followed by reinforcement fine-tuning using Group Relative Policy Optimization ( GRPO) with strictly verifiable reward functions. We design task-specific reward functions directly from metrics like 3D IoU and F1-Score to provide more effective signals to guide model training. Extensive experiments demonstrate that 3D-RFT-4B achieves state-of-the-art performance on various video-based 3D scene understanding tasks. Notably, 3D-RFT-4B significantly outperforms larger models (e.g., VG LLM-8B) on 3D video detection, 3D visual grounding, and spatial reasoning benchmarks. We further reveal good properties of 3D-RFT such as robust efficacy, and valuable insights into training strategies and data impact. We hope 3D-RFT can serve as a robust and promising paradigm for future development of 3D scene understanding.

摘要（中文）: 具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已经成为一种变革性的范例，旨在增强大型语言模型（LLM）的推理能力，但其在3D场景理解中的潜力仍未得到充分探索。现有方法主要依赖于监督微调（SFT），其中token级别的交叉熵损失充当优化的间接代理，导致训练目标与任务性能之间的不匹配。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了基于视频的3D场景理解的强化微调（3D-RFT），这是第一个将RLVR扩展到基于视频的3D感知和推理的框架。3D-RFT通过直接针对评估指标优化模型来转变范例。3D-RFT首先通过SFT激活3D感知的多模态大型语言模型（MLLM），然后使用具有严格可验证奖励函数的组相对策略优化（GRPO）进行强化微调。我们从诸如3D IoU和F1-Score等指标中直接设计任务特定的奖励函数，以提供更有效的信号来指导模型训练。大量实验表明，3D-RFT-4B在各种基于视频的3D场景理解任务上实现了最先进的性能。值得注意的是，3D-RFT-4B在3D视频检测、3D视觉定位和空间推理基准测试中显著优于更大的模型（例如，VG LLM-8B）。我们进一步揭示了3D-RFT的良好特性，例如强大的功效，以及对训练策略和数据影响的宝贵见解。我们希望3D-RFT能够成为未来3D场景理解发展的一个稳健且有前景的范例。

TLDR: The paper introduces 3D-RFT, a novel framework that extends Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) to video-based 3D scene understanding, achieving state-of-the-art performance by directly optimizing for evaluation metrics using reinforcement fine-tuning.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 3D-RFT，一种新颖的框架，将具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）扩展到基于视频的 3D 场景理解，通过使用强化微调直接针对评估指标进行优化，实现了最先进的性能。

Authors: Xiongkun Linghu, Jiangyong Huang, Baoxiong Jia, Siyuan Huang

TimeWarp: Evaluating Web Agents by Revisiting the Past

Abstract (English): The improvement of web agents on current benchmarks raises the question: Do today's agents perform just as well when the web changes? We introduce TimeWarp, a benchmark that emulates the evolving web using containerized environments that vary in UI, design, and layout. TimeWarp consists of three web environments, each with six UI versions spanning different eras of the internet, paired with a set of complex, realistic tasks requiring different forms of web navigation. Our experiments reveal web agents' vulnerability to changes and the limitations of behavior cloning (BC) on single-version trajectories. To address this, we propose TimeTraj, a simple yet effective algorithm that uses plan distillation to collect trajectories across multiple versions. By training agents on teacher rollouts using our BC-variant, we achieve substantial performance gains: $20.4\%\rightarrow37.7\%$ for Qwen-3 4B and $0\%\rightarrow27.0\%$ for Llama-3.1 8B models. We hope our work helps researchers study generalization across web designs and unlock a new paradigm for collecting plans rather than trajectories, thereby improving the robustness of web agents.

摘要（中文）: 目前网页代理在基准测试上的性能提升引发了一个问题：当网页发生变化时，现在的代理表现是否依旧出色？我们引入了 TimeWarp，一个使用容器化环境模拟不断演进的网页的基准测试，这些环境在用户界面、设计和布局上各不相同。TimeWarp 包含三个网页环境，每个环境有六个用户界面版本，跨越互联网的不同时代，并配有一系列需要不同形式网页导航的复杂、真实的任务。我们的实验揭示了网页代理对变化的脆弱性，以及在单版本轨迹上行为克隆（BC）的局限性。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了 TimeTraj，一种简单而有效的算法，它使用计划蒸馏来收集跨多个版本的轨迹。通过使用我们的 BC 变体在教师展开上训练代理，我们取得了显著的性能提升：Qwen-3 4B 模型从 $20.4\%$ 提升到 $37.7\%$，Llama-3.1 8B 模型从 $0\%$ 提升到 $27.0\%$。我们希望我们的工作能够帮助研究人员研究跨网页设计的泛化能力，并开启一种新的范式，即收集计划而非轨迹，从而提高网页代理的鲁棒性。

TLDR: The paper introduces TimeWarp, a benchmark to evaluate web agents' robustness to UI changes over time, and proposes TimeTraj, an algorithm to improve generalization by training on trajectories collected across multiple web versions, demonstrably improving performance on specific models.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 TimeWarp，一个用于评估 Web 代理对随时间变化的 UI 变化的鲁棒性的基准测试，并提出了 TimeTraj 算法，通过训练在多个 Web 版本中收集的轨迹来提高泛化能力，从而显著提高了特定模型的性能。

Authors: Md Farhan Ishmam, Kenneth Marino

BandPO: Bridging Trust Regions and Ratio Clipping via Probability-Aware Bounds for LLM Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Proximal constraints are fundamental to the stability of the Large Language Model reinforcement learning. While the canonical clipping mechanism in PPO serves as an efficient surrogate for trust regions, we identify a critical bottleneck: fixed bounds strictly constrain the upward update margin of low-probability actions, disproportionately suppressing high-advantage tail strategies and inducing rapid entropy collapse. To address this, we introduce Band-constrained Policy Optimization (BandPO). BandPO replaces canonical clipping with Band, a unified theoretical operator that projects trust regions defined by f-divergences into dynamic, probability-aware clipping intervals. Theoretical analysis confirms that Band effectively resolves this exploration bottleneck. We formulate this mapping as a convex optimization problem, guaranteeing a globally optimal numerical solution while deriving closed-form solutions for specific divergences. Extensive experiments across diverse models and datasets demonstrate that BandPO consistently outperforms canonical clipping and Clip-Higher, while robustly mitigating entropy collapse.

摘要（中文）: 近端约束对于大型语言模型强化学习的稳定性至关重要。虽然PPO中经典的裁剪机制可以作为信任区域的有效替代，但我们发现了一个关键瓶颈：固定的边界严格地约束了低概率动作的向上更新幅度，不成比例地抑制了高优势尾部策略，并导致快速的熵崩溃。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了带约束策略优化（BandPO）。BandPO用带（Band）替换了经典裁剪，带是一种统一的理论算子，可以将由f-散度定义的信任区域投影到动态的、概率感知的裁剪区间中。理论分析证实，带有效地解决了这个探索瓶颈。我们将此映射公式化为一个凸优化问题，保证了全局最优的数值解，同时推导出了特定散度的闭式解。在各种模型和数据集上的大量实验表明，BandPO始终优于经典裁剪和Clip-Higher，同时稳健地缓解了熵崩溃。

TLDR: BandPO introduces a probability-aware clipping mechanism to address the entropy collapse issue in PPO for LLM reinforcement learning, outperforming canonical clipping methods.

简要说明: BandPO提出了一种概率感知剪切机制，旨在解决LLM强化学习中PPO的熵崩溃问题，并且性能优于标准的剪切方法。

Authors: Yuan Li, Bo Wang, Yufei Gao, Yuqian Yao, Xinyuan Wang, Zhangyue Yin, Xipeng Qiu

K-Gen: A Multimodal Language-Conditioned Approach for Interpretable Keypoint-Guided Trajectory Generation

Abstract (English): Generating realistic and diverse trajectories is a critical challenge in autonomous driving simulation. While Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise, existing methods often rely on structured data like vectorized maps, which fail to capture the rich, unstructured visual context of a scene. To address this, we propose K-Gen, an interpretable keypoint-guided multimodal framework that leverages Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) to unify rasterized BEV map inputs with textual scene descriptions. Instead of directly predicting full trajectories, K-Gen generates interpretable keypoints along with reasoning that reflects agent intentions, which are subsequently refined into accurate trajectories by a refinement module. To further enhance keypoint generation, we apply T-DAPO, a trajectory-aware reinforcement fine-tuning algorithm. Experiments on WOMD and nuPlan demonstrate that K-Gen outperforms existing baselines, highlighting the effectiveness of combining multimodal reasoning with keypoint-guided trajectory generation.

摘要（中文）: 在自动驾驶仿真中，生成逼真且多样的轨迹是一个关键挑战。虽然大型语言模型（LLMs）展现出潜力，但现有方法通常依赖于向量化地图等结构化数据，无法捕捉场景中丰富的、非结构化的视觉上下文。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了K-Gen，一个可解释的关键点引导的多模态框架，利用多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）将栅格化的BEV地图输入与文本场景描述相结合。K-Gen并非直接预测完整轨迹，而是生成可解释的关键点及其反映智能体意图的推理过程，随后通过一个精细化模块将这些关键点细化为精确的轨迹。为了进一步提升关键点的生成质量，我们应用了一种轨迹感知强化微调算法T-DAPO。在WOMD和nuPlan上的实验表明，K-Gen优于现有基线，突显了将多模态推理与关键点引导的轨迹生成相结合的有效性。

TLDR: K-Gen is a multimodal LLM framework that generates interpretable keypoints and reasoning for trajectory generation, outperforming existing methods on autonomous driving datasets.

Authors: Mingxuan Mu, Guo Yang, Lei Chen, Ping Wu, Jianxun Cui

Breaking Contextual Inertia: Reinforcement Learning with Single-Turn Anchors for Stable Multi-Turn Interaction

Abstract (English): While LLMs demonstrate strong reasoning capabilities when provided with full information in a single turn, they exhibit substantial vulnerability in multi-turn interactions. Specifically, when information is revealed incrementally or requires updates, models frequently fail to integrate new constraints, leading to a collapse in performance compared to their single-turn baselines. We term the root cause as \emph{Contextual Inertia}: a phenomenon where models rigidly adhere to previous reasoning traces. Even when users explicitly provide corrections or new data in later turns, the model ignores them, preferring to maintain consistency with its previous (incorrect) reasoning path. To address this, we introduce \textbf{R}einforcement \textbf{L}earning with \textbf{S}ingle-\textbf{T}urn \textbf{A}nchors (\textbf{RLSTA}), a generalizable training approach designed to stabilize multi-turn interaction across diverse scenarios and domains. RLSTA leverages the model's superior single-turn capabilities as stable internal anchors to provide reward signals. By aligning multi-turn responses with these anchors, RLSTA empowers models to break contextual inertia and self-calibrate their reasoning based on the latest information. Experiments show that RLSTA significantly outperforms standard fine-tuning and abstention-based methods. Notably, our method exhibits strong cross-domain generalization (e.g., math to code) and proves effective even without external verifiers, highlighting its potential for general-domain applications.

摘要（中文）: 虽然大型语言模型在单轮交互中提供完整信息时表现出强大的推理能力，但它们在多轮交互中表现出显著的脆弱性。具体而言，当信息以增量方式揭示或需要更新时，模型经常无法整合新的约束条件，导致性能相比单轮基线崩塌。我们将根本原因称为\emph{上下文惰性}：一种模型僵化地坚持先前推理轨迹的现象。即使在之后的轮次中用户明确提供更正或新数据，模型也会忽略这些信息，转而保持与其先前（不正确的）推理路径的一致性。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了\textbf{基}于\textbf{单}轮\textbf{锚点}的\textbf{强}化\textbf{学}习（\textbf{RLSTA}），这是一种通用化的训练方法，旨在稳定跨不同场景和领域的多轮交互。RLSTA利用模型优秀的单轮能力作为稳定的内部锚点来提供奖励信号。通过将多轮响应与这些锚点对齐，RLSTA使模型能够消除上下文惰性，并基于最新信息进行自我校准推理。实验表明，RLSTA显著优于标准的微调和基于弃权的方法。值得注意的是，我们的方法表现出很强的跨领域泛化能力（例如，数学到代码），并且即使没有外部验证器也能证明其有效性，突显了其在通用领域应用中的潜力。

TLDR: This paper introduces Reinforcement Learning with Single-Turn Anchors (RLSTA) to address the problem of 'contextual inertia' in LLMs during multi-turn interactions, improving their ability to integrate new information and self-calibrate reasoning.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了使用单轮锚点的强化学习 (RLSTA) 方法，旨在解决LLM在多轮交互中存在的“上下文惯性”问题，提升模型整合新信息和自我校准推理的能力。

Authors: Xingwu Chen, Zhanqiu Zhang, Yiwen Guo, Difan Zou

Are Multimodal LLMs Ready for Surveillance? A Reality Check on Zero-Shot Anomaly Detection in the Wild

Abstract (English): Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have demonstrated impressive general competence in video understanding, yet their reliability for real-world Video Anomaly Detection (VAD) remains largely unexplored. Unlike conventional pipelines relying on reconstruction or pose-based cues, MLLMs enable a paradigm shift: treating anomaly detection as a language-guided reasoning task. In this work, we systematically evaluate state-of-the-art MLLMs on the ShanghaiTech and CHAD benchmarks by reformulating VAD as a binary classification task under weak temporal supervision. We investigate how prompt specificity and temporal window lengths (1s--3s) influence performance, focusing on the precision--recall trade-off. Our findings reveal a pronounced conservative bias in zero-shot settings; while models exhibit high confidence, they disproportionately favor the 'normal' class, resulting in high precision but a recall collapse that limits practical utility. We demonstrate that class-specific instructions can significantly shift this decision boundary, improving the peak F1-score on ShanghaiTech from 0.09 to 0.64, yet recall remains a critical bottleneck. These results highlight a significant performance gap for MLLMs in noisy environments and provide a foundation for future work in recall-oriented prompting and model calibration for open-world surveillance, which demands complex video understanding and reasoning.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型(MLLMs)在视频理解方面展现了令人印象深刻的通用能力，但它们在现实世界视频异常检测(VAD)中的可靠性在很大程度上仍未被探索。与依赖于重构或基于姿态的线索的传统流程不同，MLLMs实现了一种范式转变：将异常检测视为一种语言引导的推理任务。 在这项工作中，我们通过在弱时间监督下将VAD重新定义为二元分类任务，从而系统地评估了最先进的MLLMs在ShanghaiTech和CHAD基准上的表现。我们研究了提示词的具体性和时间窗口长度(1秒-3秒)如何影响性能，重点关注精确率-召回率的权衡。我们的发现揭示了零样本设置中存在显著的保守偏见；虽然模型表现出很高的置信度，但它们不成比例地倾向于“正常”类别，导致高精确率但召回率崩溃，从而限制了实际应用。我们证明了特定类别的指令可以显著改变这个决策边界，将ShanghaiTech上的峰值F1分数从0.09提高到0.64，但召回率仍然是一个关键瓶颈。这些结果突出了MLLMs在嘈杂环境中的显著性能差距，并为未来在面向召回的提示工程和模型校准方面的工作奠定了基础，以适应需要复杂视频理解和推理的开放世界监控。

TLDR: This paper evaluates the performance of zero-shot MLLMs for video anomaly detection, revealing a conservative bias towards 'normal' classification and highlighting the need for recall-oriented prompting strategies to improve practical utility in surveillance applications.

简要说明: 该论文评估了零样本多模态大型语言模型在视频异常检测中的性能，揭示了一种趋向于'正常'分类的保守偏差，并强调需要面向召回的提示策略，以提高其在监控应用中的实用性。

Authors: Shanle Yao, Armin Danesh Pazho, Narges Rashvand, Hamed Tabkhi

Probabilistic Dreaming for World Models

Abstract (English): "Dreaming" enables agents to learn from imagined experiences, enabling more robust and sample-efficient learning of world models. In this work, we consider innovations to the state-of-the-art Dreamer model using probabilistic methods that enable: (1) the parallel exploration of many latent states; and (2) maintaining distinct hypotheses for mutually exclusive futures while retaining the desirable gradient properties of continuous latents. Evaluating on the MPE SimpleTag domain, our method outperforms standard Dreamer with a 4.5% score improvement and 28% lower variance in episode returns. We also discuss limitations and directions for future work, including how optimal hyperparameters (e.g. particle count K) scale with environmental complexity, and methods to capture epistemic uncertainty in world models.

摘要（中文）: “梦境”使智能体能够从想象的经验中学习，从而更稳健、更具样本效率地学习世界模型。在这项工作中，我们考虑使用概率方法对最先进的Dreamer模型进行创新，以实现：（1）并行探索多个潜在状态；以及（2）在保持连续潜在变量理想梯度属性的同时，维持对互斥未来的不同假设。 在MPE SimpleTag 域上进行评估，我们的方法优于标准的 Dreamer，分数提高了 4.5%，且单幕回报的方差降低了 28%。 我们还讨论了局限性以及未来工作的方向，包括最佳超参数（例如，粒子数量 K）如何随环境复杂性而变化，以及在世界模型中捕获认知不确定性的方法。

TLDR: This paper introduces a probabilistic extension to the Dreamer world model, enabling parallel exploration of latent states and improved performance on the SimpleTag domain.

Authors: Gavin Wong

When Sensors Fail: Temporal Sequence Models for Robust PPO under Sensor Drift

Abstract (English): Real-world reinforcement learning systems must operate under distributional drift in their observation streams, yet most policy architectures implicitly assume fully observed and noise-free states. We study robustness of Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) under temporally persistent sensor failures that induce partial observability and representation shift. To respond to this drift, we augment PPO with temporal sequence models, including Transformers and State Space Models (SSMs), to enable policies to infer missing information from history and maintain performance. Under a stochastic sensor failure process, we prove a high-probability bound on infinite-horizon reward degradation that quantifies how robustness depends on policy smoothness and failure persistence. Empirically, on MuJoCo continuous-control benchmarks with severe sensor dropout, we show Transformer-based sequence policies substantially outperform MLP, RNN, and SSM baselines in robustness, maintaining high returns even when large fractions of sensors are unavailable. These results demonstrate that temporal sequence reasoning provides a principled and practical mechanism for reliable operation under observation drift caused by sensor unreliability.

摘要（中文）: 真实世界的强化学习系统必须在观测流中的分布漂移下运行，然而大多数策略架构隐式地假设完全观测且无噪声的状态。 我们研究了近端策略优化（PPO）在诱导部分可观测性和表征偏移的持续性传感器故障下的鲁棒性。为了应对这种漂移，我们利用时间序列模型（包括 Transformers 和状态空间模型 (SSM)）来增强 PPO，以使策略能够从历史中推断缺失信息并维持性能。 在随机传感器故障过程下，我们证明了无限视界回报退化的高概率界限，该界限量化了鲁棒性如何依赖于策略平滑度和故障持久性。通过实验，在具有严重传感器丢失的 MuJoCo 连续控制基准上，我们证明了基于 Transformer 的序列策略在鲁棒性方面大大优于 MLP、RNN 和 SSM 基线，即使在大部分传感器不可用时也能保持高回报。这些结果表明，时间序列推理为在由传感器不可靠性引起的观测漂移下实现可靠操作提供了一种有原则且实用的机制。

TLDR: The paper enhances PPO with temporal sequence models (Transformers, SSMs) to improve robustness against sensor failures, demonstrating superior performance on MuJoCo benchmarks with sensor dropout.

简要说明: 该论文通过将时间序列模型（Transformers，SSMs）加入 PPO，提高了其在传感器故障下的鲁棒性，并在 MuJoCo 基准测试中展示了卓越的性能，尤其是在传感器失灵的情况下。

Authors: Kevin Vogt-Lowell, Theodoros Tsiligkaridis, Rodney Lafuente-Mercado, Surabhi Ghatti, Shanghua Gao, Marinka Zitnik, Daniela Rus

Bootstrapping Exploration with Group-Level Natural Language Feedback in Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Large language models (LLMs) typically receive diverse natural language (NL) feedback through interaction with the environment. However, current reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms rely solely on scalar rewards, leaving the rich information in NL feedback underutilized and leading to inefficient exploration. In this work, we propose GOLF, an RL framework that explicitly exploits group-level language feedback to guide targeted exploration through actionable refinements. GOLF aggregates two complementary feedback sources: (i) external critiques that pinpoint errors or propose targeted fixes, and (ii) intra-group attempts that supply alternative partial ideas and diverse failure patterns. These group-level feedbacks are aggregated to produce high-quality refinements, which are adaptively injected into training as off-policy scaffolds to provide targeted guidance in sparse-reward regions. Meanwhile, GOLF jointly optimizes generation and refinement within a unified RL loop, creating a virtuous cycle that continuously improves both capabilities. Experiments on both verifiable and non-verifiable benchmarks show that GOLF achieves superior performance and exploration efficiency, achieving 2.2$\times$ improvements in sample efficiency compared to RL methods trained solely on scalar rewards. Code is available at https://github.com/LuckyyySTA/GOLF.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLM）通常通过与环境交互接收到多种多样的自然语言（NL）反馈。然而，当前的强化学习（RL）算法仅仅依赖于标量奖励，使得自然语言反馈中蕴含的丰富信息未被充分利用，导致探索效率低下。在这项工作中，我们提出了GOLF，一种强化学习框架，它显式地利用群体层面的语言反馈，通过可执行的改进来指导目标明确的探索。GOLF聚合了两种互补的反馈来源：（i）外部评论，它精准地指出错误或提出有针对性的修复建议，以及（ii）组内尝试，它提供替代性的局部想法和多样化的失败模式。这些群体层面的反馈被聚合以产生高质量的改进，这些改进被自适应地注入到训练中作为离策略支架，从而在稀疏奖励区域提供有针对性的指导。同时，GOLF在一个统一的强化学习循环中联合优化生成和改进，创造一个不断改进两种能力的良性循环。在可验证和不可验证的基准测试上的实验表明，GOLF实现了卓越的性能和探索效率，与仅通过标量奖励训练的强化学习方法相比，样本效率提高了2.2倍。代码可在https://github.com/LuckyyySTA/GOLF获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces GOLF, a reinforcement learning framework that leverages group-level natural language feedback to guide exploration and improve sample efficiency in sparse-reward environments by adaptively injecting off-policy scaffolds.

Authors: Lei Huang, Xiang Cheng, Chenxiao Zhao, Guobin Shen, Junjie Yang, Xiaocheng Feng, Yuxuan Gu, Xing Yu, Bing Qin

Self-Attribution Bias: When AI Monitors Go Easy on Themselves

Abstract (English): Agentic systems increasingly rely on language models to monitor their own behavior. For example, coding agents may self critique generated code for pull request approval or assess the safety of tool-use actions. We show that this design pattern can fail when the action is presented in a previous or in the same assistant turn instead of being presented by the user in a user turn. We define self-attribution bias as the tendency of a model to evaluate an action as more correct or less risky when the action is implicitly framed as its own, compared to when the same action is evaluated under off-policy attribution. Across four coding and tool-use datasets, we find that monitors fail to report high-risk or low-correctness actions more often when evaluation follows a previous assistant turn in which the action was generated, compared to when the same action is evaluated in a new context presented in a user turn. In contrast, explicitly stating that the action comes from the monitor does not by itself induce self-attribution bias. Because monitors are often evaluated on fixed examples rather than on their own generated actions, these evaluations can make monitors appear more reliable than they actually are in deployment, leading developers to unknowingly deploy inadequate monitors in agentic systems.

摘要（中文）: 代理系统越来越依赖于语言模型来监控自身的行为。例如，编码代理可能会自我批判其生成的代码，以便批准拉取请求，或者评估工具使用行为的安全性。我们发现，当动作在之前或相同的助手轮次中呈现，而不是由用户在用户轮次中呈现时，这种设计模式可能会失效。我们定义“自我归因偏差”为：当一个动作被隐含地视为模型自身的动作时，与在离策略归因下评估同一动作相比，模型倾向于将该动作评估为更正确或风险更低。在四个编码和工具使用数据集上，我们发现，与在用户轮次中呈现的新上下文中评估同一动作相比，当评估跟随生成该动作的上一个助手轮次之后时，监控器更频繁地未能报告高风险或低正确性的动作。相反，明确声明该动作来自监控器本身并不会诱发自我归因偏差。由于监控器通常在固定的示例上进行评估，而不是基于它们自己生成的动作，因此这些评估可能会使监控器在部署时显得比实际更可靠，导致开发者在不知情的情况下在代理系统中部署不充分的监控器。

TLDR: The paper identifies a 'self-attribution bias' in AI monitors, where they are less likely to flag errors in their own actions compared to those presented by users, leading to potentially unreliable agentic systems. The bias does not appear when explicitly stating the action comes from the monitor.

简要说明: 该论文指出AI监控器存在“自我归因偏见”，与用户提出的行为相比，它们不太可能标记自己行为中的错误，这可能导致代理系统不可靠。 当明确声明动作来自监控器时，不会出现这种偏差。

Authors: Dipika Khullar, Jack Hopkins, Rowan Wang, Fabien Roger

Dual-Modality Multi-Stage Adversarial Safety Training: Robustifying Multimodal Web Agents Against Cross-Modal Attacks

Abstract (English): Multimodal web agents that process both screenshots and accessibility trees are increasingly deployed to interact with web interfaces, yet their dual-stream architecture opens an underexplored attack surface: an adversary who injects content into the webpage DOM simultaneously corrupts both observation channels with a consistent deceptive narrative. Our vulnerability analysis on MiniWob++ reveals that attacks including a visual component far outperform text-only injections, exposing critical gaps in text-centric VLM safety training. Motivated by this finding, we propose Dual-Modality Multi-Stage Adversarial Safety Training (DMAST), a framework that formalizes the agent-attacker interaction as a two-player zero-sum Markov game and co-trains both players through a three-stage pipeline: (1) imitation learning from a strong teacher model, (2) oracle-guided supervised fine-tuning that uses a novel zero-acknowledgment strategy to instill task-focused reasoning under adversarial noise, and (3) adversarial reinforcement learning via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) self-play. On out-of-distribution tasks, DMAST substantially mitigates adversarial risks while simultaneously doubling task completion efficiency. Our approach significantly outperforms established training-based and prompt-based defenses, demonstrating genuine co-evolutionary progress and robust generalization to complex, unseen environments.

摘要（中文）: 处理屏幕截图和可访问性树的多模态网络代理正越来越多地被部署以与网页界面交互，但其双流架构开启了一个尚未充分探索的攻击面：攻击者通过将内容注入网页DOM，同时以一致的欺骗性叙事破坏两个观察通道。我们对MiniWob++的漏洞分析表明，包含视觉成分的攻击远胜于仅文本注入，暴露了以文本为中心的视觉语言模型（VLM）安全训练中的关键缺陷。受此发现的启发，我们提出了双模态多阶段对抗安全训练（DMAST），该框架将代理-攻击者交互形式化为一个双人零和马尔可夫博弈，并通过一个三阶段流程共同训练这两个玩家：（1）从强大的教师模型进行模仿学习；（2）使用一种新颖的零确认策略，在对抗噪声下灌输以任务为中心的推理的、具有指导意义的监督微调；（3）通过群体相对策略优化（GRPO）自博弈进行对抗强化学习。在分布外任务中，DMAST显著降低了对抗风险，同时使任务完成效率提高了一倍。我们的方法显著优于已建立的基于训练和基于提示的防御，展示了真正的协同进化进展以及对复杂、未见环境的强大泛化能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces Dual-Modality Multi-Stage Adversarial Safety Training (DMAST) to improve the robustness of multimodal web agents against cross-modal attacks by co-training an agent and attacker through a three-stage pipeline, achieving significant improvements in adversarial risk mitigation and task completion efficiency.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种双模态多阶段对抗安全训练 (DMAST) 方法，旨在通过三阶段流水线共同训练智能体和攻击者，从而提高多模态 Web 智能体对跨模态攻击的鲁棒性，并在降低对抗风险和提高任务完成效率方面取得了显著进展。

Authors: Haoyu Liu, Dingcheng Li, Lukas Rutishauser, Zeyu Zheng

SGR3 Model: Scene Graph Retrieval-Reasoning Model in 3D

Abstract (English): 3D scene graphs provide a structured representation of object entities and their relationships, enabling high-level interpretation and reasoning for robots while remaining intuitively understandable to humans. Existing approaches for 3D scene graph generation typically combine scene reconstruction with graph neural networks (GNNs). However, such pipelines require multi-modal data that may not always be available, and their reliance on heuristic graph construction can constrain the prediction of relationship triplets. In this work, we introduce a Scene Graph Retrieval-Reasoning Model in 3D (SGR3 Model), a training-free framework that leverages multi-modal large language models (MLLMs) with retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) for semantic scene graph generation. SGR3 Model bypasses the need for explicit 3D reconstruction. Instead, it enhances relational reasoning by incorporating semantically aligned scene graphs retrieved via a ColPali-style cross-modal framework. To improve retrieval robustness, we further introduce a weighted patch-level similarity selection mechanism that mitigates the negative impact of blurry or semantically uninformative regions. Experiments demonstrate that SGR3 Model achieves competitive performance compared to training-free baselines and on par with GNN-based expert models. Moreover, an ablation study on the retrieval module and knowledge base scale reveals that retrieved external information is explicitly integrated into the token generation process, rather than being implicitly internalized through abstraction.

摘要（中文）: 3D场景图提供了对象实体及其关系的结构化表示，从而使机器人可以进行高级别的解释和推理，同时保持对人类的直观可理解性。现有的3D场景图生成方法通常将场景重建与图神经网络(GNN)相结合。然而，这种流程需要多模态数据，而这些数据并不总是可用的，并且它们对启发式图构建的依赖可能会限制关系三元组的预测。在这项工作中，我们引入了一个3D场景图检索-推理模型(SGR3模型)，这是一个无需训练的框架，它利用带有检索增强生成(RAG)的多模态大型语言模型(MLLM)进行语义场景图生成。SGR3模型绕过了对显式3D重建的需求。相反，它通过结合经由ColPali式跨模态框架检索到的语义对齐的场景图来增强关系推理。为了提高检索的鲁棒性，我们进一步引入了一种加权的patch级别相似性选择机制，以减轻模糊或语义信息不足区域的负面影响。实验表明，与无需训练的基线相比，SGR3模型实现了有竞争力的性能，并且与基于GNN的专家模型相当。此外，对检索模块和知识库规模的消融研究表明，检索到的外部信息被显式地集成到token生成过程中，而不是通过抽象隐式地内化。

TLDR: The paper introduces SGR3, a training-free framework for 3D scene graph generation using MLLMs and retrieval-augmented generation, bypassing 3D reconstruction and achieving competitive performance.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了SGR3，一个使用多模态大语言模型和检索增强生成的三维场景图生成框架，无需三维重建并达到了有竞争力的性能。

Authors: Zirui Wang, Ruiping Liu, Yufan Chen, Junwei Zheng, Weijia Fan, Kunyu Peng, Di Wen, Jiale Wei, Jiaming Zhang, Rainer Stiefelhagen

TaxonRL: Reinforcement Learning with Intermediate Rewards for Interpretable Fine-Grained Visual Reasoning

Abstract (English): Traditional vision-language models struggle with contrastive fine-grained taxonomic reasoning, particularly when distinguishing between visually similar species within the same genus or family. We introduce TaxonRL, a reinforcement learning approach using Group Relative Policy Optimization with intermediate rewards that decomposes the reasoning process into hierarchical taxonomic predictions. Our method incentivizes models to explicitly reason about species-level, genus-level, and family-level features before making final classifications. This structured approach is designed not only to boost accuracy but also to yield a transparent, verifiable decision-making process. On the challenging Birds-to-Words dataset, TaxonRL achieves 91.7\% average accuracy, exceeding human performance (77.3\%) while generating interpretable reasoning traces. We demonstrate strong cross-domain generalization, showing substantial gains in primate and marine species verification. Our results establish that enforcing structured, hierarchical reasoning provides a powerful and transferable framework for fine-grained visual discrimination.

摘要（中文）: 传统视觉-语言模型在对比细粒度分类推理方面表现不佳，尤其是在区分同一属或科内视觉相似的物种时。我们提出 TaxonRL，一种使用带中间奖励的群相对策略优化的强化学习方法，将推理过程分解为分层分类预测。我们的方法激励模型在做出最终分类之前，显式地推理物种级别、属级别和科级别的特征。这种结构化方法旨在不仅提高准确性，而且产生透明、可验证的决策过程。在具有挑战性的 Birds-to-Words 数据集上，TaxonRL 实现了 91.7% 的平均准确率，超过了人类的表现（77.3%），同时生成了可解释的推理轨迹。我们展示了强大的跨域泛化能力，在灵长类动物和海洋物种验证方面取得了显著提升。我们的结果表明，强制执行结构化的分层推理为细粒度视觉辨别提供了一个强大且可迁移的框架。

TLDR: TaxonRL uses reinforcement learning with hierarchical taxonomic prediction and intermediate rewards to improve fine-grained visual reasoning, surpassing human accuracy on the Birds-to-Words dataset and demonstrating strong cross-domain generalization.

简要说明: TaxonRL利用强化学习和分层分类预测以及中间奖励来提升细粒度视觉推理能力，超越了在Birds-to-Words数据集上的人类准确率，并展示了强大的跨领域泛化能力。

Authors: Maximilian von Klinski, Maximilian Schall

FocusGraph: Graph-Structured Frame Selection for Embodied Long Video Question Answering

Abstract (English): The ability to understand long videos is vital for embodied intelligent agents, because their effectiveness depends on how well they can accumulate, organize, and leverage long-horizon perceptual memories. Recently, multimodal LLMs have been gaining popularity for solving the long video understanding task due to their general ability to understand natural language and to leverage world knowledge. However, as the number of frames provided to an MLLM increases, the quality of its responses tends to degrade, and inference time grows. Therefore, when using MLLMs for long video understanding, a crucial step is selecting key frames from the video to answer user queries. In this work, we develop FocusGraph, a framework for keyframe selection for question answering over long egocentric videos. It leverages a lightweight trainable Scene-Caption LLM Selector that selects query-relevant clips based on their graph-based captions, and a training-free method for selecting keyframes from these clips. Unlike existing methods, the proposed Scene-Caption LLM Selector does not rely on the original sequence of low-resolution frames; instead, it operates on a compact textual representation of the scene. We then design a training-free Patch-wise Sparse-Flow Retention (PSFR) method to select keyframes from the resulting sequence of clips, which are fed into an MLLM to produce the final answer. Together, these components enable FocusGraph to achieve state-of-the-art results on challenging egocentric long-video question answering benchmarks, including FindingDory and HourVideo, while significantly reducing inference time relative to baseline approaches.

摘要（中文）: 理解长视频对于具身智能体至关重要，因为它们的有效性取决于它们积累、组织和利用长时域感知记忆的能力。 近年来，多模态LLM (MLLM) 因其理解自然语言和利用世界知识的通用能力，在解决长视频理解任务方面越来越受欢迎。然而，随着提供给MLLM的帧数增加，其响应质量往往会下降，并且推理时间会增长。因此，在使用MLLM进行长视频理解时，一个关键步骤是从视频中选择关键帧来回答用户查询。 在这项工作中，我们开发了FocusGraph，这是一个用于长第一人称视角视频问答的关键帧选择框架。 它利用一个轻量级的可训练场景描述LLM选择器，该选择器基于其基于图的描述来选择与查询相关的片段，以及一种无训练方法来从这些片段中选择关键帧。 与现有方法不同，所提出的场景描述LLM选择器不依赖于原始的低分辨率帧序列，而是基于场景的紧凑文本表示进行操作。 然后，我们设计了一种无训练的逐块稀疏流保留 (PSFR) 方法，从生成的片段序列中选择关键帧，这些关键帧被馈送到MLLM以生成最终答案。 总而言之，这些组件使FocusGraph能够在具有挑战性的第一人称视角长视频问答基准测试（包括FindingDory和HourVideo）上实现最先进的结果，同时相对于基线方法显著减少推理时间。

TLDR: The paper introduces FocusGraph, a keyframe selection framework for long egocentric video question answering that uses a lightweight LLM selector and patch-wise sparse-flow retention to improve accuracy and reduce inference time when using Multimodal LLMs. It achieves state-of-the-art results on FindingDory and HourVideo datasets.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了FocusGraph，一个用于长时自中心视频问答的关键帧选择框架，它使用轻量级的LLM选择器和逐块稀疏流保持来提高在使用多模态LLM时的准确性并减少推理时间。该方法在FindingDory和HourVideo数据集上取得了最先进的结果。

Authors: Tatiana Zemskova, Solomon Andryushenko, Ilya Obrubov, Viktoriia Khoruzhaia, Ekaterina Eroshenko, Ekaterina Derevyanka, Dmitry Yudin

Reward-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): RL agents are typically trained under a single, fixed reward function, which makes them brittle to reward misspecification and limits their ability to adapt to changing task preferences. We introduce Reward-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (RCRL), a framework that trains a single agent to optimize a family of reward specifications while collecting experience under only one nominal objective. RCRL conditions the agent on reward parameterizations and learns multiple reward objectives from a shared replay data entirely off-policy, enabling a single policy to represent reward-specific behaviors. Across single-task, multi-task, and vision-based benchmarks, we show that RCRL not only improves performance under the nominal reward parameterization, but also enables efficient adaptation to new parameterizations. Our results demonstrate that RCRL provides a scalable mechanism for learning robust, steerable policies without sacrificing the simplicity of single-task training.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习智能体通常在单一、固定的奖励函数下进行训练，这使得它们对奖励指定错误非常敏感，并限制了其适应变化的任务偏好的能力。我们引入了奖励条件强化学习(RCRL)，该框架训练单个智能体来优化一系列奖励规范，同时仅在一个标称目标下收集经验。RCRL 以奖励参数化为条件，并从完全离线的共享回放数据中学习多个奖励目标，从而使单个策略能够代表特定于奖励的行为。在单任务、多任务和基于视觉的基准测试中，我们表明 RCRL 不仅提高了标称奖励参数化下的性能，而且能够高效地适应新的参数化。我们的结果表明，RCRL 提供了一种可扩展机制，用于学习鲁棒、可操纵的策略，而不会牺牲单任务训练的简易性。

TLDR: The paper introduces Reward-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (RCRL) which trains an RL agent to optimize a family of reward specifications from a shared replay buffer, enabling adaptation to new reward parameterizations and improving performance under the nominal reward.

简要说明: 本文介绍了奖励条件强化学习 (RCRL)，它训练一个强化学习智能体从共享的重放缓冲区中优化一系列奖励规范，从而能够适应新的奖励参数化并提高标称奖励下的性能。

Authors: Michal Nauman, Marek Cygan, Pieter Abbeel

Accelerating Sampling-Based Control via Learned Linear Koopman Dynamics

Abstract (English): This paper presents an efficient model predictive path integral (MPPI) control framework for systems with complex nonlinear dynamics. To improve the computational efficiency of classic MPPI while preserving control performance, we replace the nonlinear dynamics used for trajectory propagation with a learned linear deep Koopman operator (DKO) model, enabling faster rollout and more efficient trajectory sampling. The DKO dynamics are learned directly from interaction data, eliminating the need for analytical system models. The resulting controller, termed MPPI-DK, is evaluated in simulation on pendulum balancing and surface vehicle navigation tasks, and validated on hardware through reference-tracking experiments on a quadruped robot. Experimental results demonstrate that MPPI-DK achieves control performance close to MPPI with true dynamics while substantially reducing computational cost, enabling efficient real-time control on robotic platforms.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种高效的模型预测路径积分（MPPI）控制框架，用于具有复杂非线性动力学的系统。为了在保持控制性能的同时提高经典MPPI的计算效率，我们用一个学习到的线性深度Koopman算子（DKO）模型来替代用于轨迹传播的非线性动力学，从而实现更快的展开和更有效的轨迹采样。DKO动力学直接从交互数据中学习，无需解析系统模型。由此产生的控制器，命名为MPPI-DK，在钟摆平衡和水面车辆导航任务的仿真中进行了评估，并通过四足机器人的参考跟踪实验在硬件上进行了验证。实验结果表明，MPPI-DK在计算成本大幅降低的同时，实现了接近于使用真实动力学的MPPI的控制性能，从而能够在机器人平台上实现高效的实时控制。

TLDR: This paper presents a computationally efficient Model Predictive Path Integral (MPPI) control framework using a learned linear Deep Koopman Operator (DKO) model, validated on simulated and real robotic systems.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种计算高效的模型预测路径积分（MPPI）控制框架，该框架使用学习到的线性深度 Koopman 算子（DKO）模型，并在模拟和真实机器人系统上进行了验证。

Authors: Wenjian Hao, Yuxuan Fang, Zehui Lu, Shaoshuai Mou

Omni-Manip: Beyond-FOV Large-Workspace Humanoid Manipulation with Omnidirectional 3D Perception

Abstract (English): The deployment of humanoid robots for dexterous manipulation in unstructured environments remains challenging due to perceptual limitations that constrain the effective workspace. In scenarios where physical constraints prevent the robot from repositioning itself, maintaining omnidirectional awareness becomes far more critical than color or semantic information. While recent advances in visuomotor policy learning have improved manipulation capabilities, conventional RGB-D solutions suffer from narrow fields of view (FOV) and self-occlusion, requiring frequent base movements that introduce motion uncertainty and safety risks. Existing approaches to expanding perception, including active vision systems and third-view cameras, introduce mechanical complexity, calibration dependencies, and latency that hinder reliable real-time performance. In this work, We propose Omni-Manip, an end-to-end LiDAR-driven 3D visuomotor policy that enables robust manipulation in large workspaces. Our method processes panoramic point clouds through a Time-Aware Attention Pooling mechanism, efficiently encoding sparse 3D data while capturing temporal dependencies. This 360° perception allows the robot to interact with objects across wide areas without frequent repositioning. To support policy learning, we develop a whole-body teleoperation system for efficient data collection on full-body coordination. Extensive experiments in simulation and real-world environments show that Omni-Manip achieves robust performance in large-workspace and cluttered scenarios, outperforming baselines that rely on egocentric depth cameras.

摘要（中文）: 在非结构化环境中部署具有灵巧操作能力的人形机器人仍然面临挑战，这主要是由于感知限制约束了有效的工作空间。当物理约束阻止机器人重新定位自身时，保持全向感知变得比颜色或语义信息更为关键。尽管视觉运动策略学习的最新进展提高了操作能力，但传统的RGB-D解决方案受到狭窄视野(FOV)和自遮挡的限制，需要频繁的基础移动，这引入了运动不确定性和安全风险。现有的扩展感知方法，包括主动视觉系统和第三视角相机，引入了机械复杂性、标定依赖性和延迟，阻碍了可靠的实时性能。在这项工作中，我们提出了Omni-Manip，一种端到端的激光雷达驱动的3D视觉运动策略，能够在大型工作空间中实现鲁棒的操作。我们的方法通过一种时序感知注意力池化机制处理全景点云，高效地编码稀疏的3D数据，同时捕获时间依赖性。这种360°感知允许机器人与大范围内的物体交互，而无需频繁的重新定位。为了支持策略学习，我们开发了一个全身遥操作系统，用于在全身协调上高效地收集数据。在模拟和真实环境中的大量实验表明，Omni-Manip在大型工作空间和拥挤场景中实现了强大的性能，优于依赖以自我为中心的深度相机的基线方法。

TLDR: The paper introduces Omni-Manip, a LiDAR-driven 3D visuomotor policy for humanoid robots that overcomes the limitations of narrow FOV vision by using 360° perception, allowing for robust manipulation in large workspaces without frequent repositioning.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Omni-Manip，一种基于激光雷达驱动的三维视觉运动策略，用于人形机器人，通过使用360°感知克服了窄视野视觉的局限性，从而能够在大型工作空间中进行稳健的操作，而无需频繁重新定位。

Authors: Pei Qu, Zheng Li, Yufei Jia, Ziyun Liu, Liang Zhu, Haoang Li, Jinni Zhou, Jun Ma

AIM-SLAM: Dense Monocular SLAM via Adaptive and Informative Multi-View Keyframe Prioritization with Foundation Model

Abstract (English): Recent advances in geometric foundation models have emerged as a promising alternative for addressing the challenge of dense reconstruction in monocular visual simultaneous localization and mapping (SLAM). Although geometric foundation models enable SLAM to leverage variable input views, the previous methods remain confined to two-view pairs or fixed-length inputs without sufficient deliberation of geometric context for view selection. To tackle this problem, we propose AIM-SLAM, a dense monocular SLAM framework that exploits an adaptive and informative multi-view keyframe prioritization with dense pointmap predictions from visual geometry grounded transformer (VGGT). Specifically, we introduce the selective information- and geometric-aware multi-view adaptation (SIGMA) module, which employs voxel overlap and information gain to retrieve a candidate set of keyframes and adaptively determine its size. Furthermore, we formulate a joint multi-view Sim(3) optimization that enforces consistent alignment across selected views, substantially improving pose estimation accuracy. The effectiveness of AIM-SLAM is demonstrated on real-world datasets, where it achieves state-of-the-art performance in both pose estimation and dense reconstruction. Our system supports ROS integration, with code is available at https://aimslam.github.io/.

摘要（中文）: 单目视觉同步定位与地图构建(SLAM)中，几何基础模型的最新进展为应对稠密重建的挑战提供了一种有希望的替代方案。尽管几何基础模型使SLAM能够利用可变的输入视图，但先前的方法仍然局限于双视图配对或固定长度的输入，而没有充分考虑视图选择的几何上下文。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了AIM-SLAM，一个稠密单目SLAM框架，它利用自适应和信息丰富的多视图关键帧优先级排序，以及来自基于视觉几何的Transformer (VGGT)的稠密点云地图预测。具体而言，我们引入了选择性的信息与几何感知多视图自适应(SIGMA)模块，该模块采用体素重叠和信息增益来检索候选的关键帧集并自适应地确定其大小。此外，我们构建了一个联合多视图Sim(3)优化，它强制在所选视图之间保持一致的对齐，从而显著提高位姿估计的准确性。AIM-SLAM的有效性在真实世界的数据集上得到了验证，在位姿估计和稠密重建方面都实现了最先进的性能。我们的系统支持ROS集成，代码可在https://aimslam.github.io/上获取。

Authors: Jinwoo Jeon, Dong-Uk Seo, Eungchang Mason Lee, Hyun Myung

CoIn3D: Revisiting Configuration-Invariant Multi-Camera 3D Object Detection

Abstract (English): Multi-camera 3D object detection (MC3D) has attracted increasing attention with the growing deployment of multi-sensor physical agents, such as robots and autonomous vehicles. However, MC3D models still struggle to generalize to unseen platforms with new multi-camera configurations. Current solutions simply employ a meta-camera for unified representation but lack comprehensive consideration. In this paper, we revisit this issue and identify that the devil lies in spatial prior discrepancies across source and target configurations, including different intrinsics, extrinsics, and array layouts. To address this, we propose CoIn3D, a generalizable MC3D framework that enables strong transferability from source configurations to unseen target ones. CoIn3D explicitly incorporates all identified spatial priors into both feature embedding and image observation through spatial-aware feature modulation (SFM) and camera-aware data augmentation (CDA), respectively. SFM enriches feature space by integrating four spatial representations, such as focal length, ground depth, ground gradient, and Plücker coordinate. CDA improves observation diversity under various configurations via a training-free dynamic novel-view image synthesis scheme. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CoIn3D achieves strong cross-configuration performance on landmark datasets such as NuScenes, Waymo, and Lyft, under three dominant MC3D paradigms represented by BEVDepth, BEVFormer, and PETR.

摘要（中文）: 多相机3D目标检测（MC3D）随着机器人和自动驾驶车辆等多传感器物理代理的日益普及而备受关注。然而，MC3D模型仍然难以泛化到具有全新多相机配置的未知平台。目前的解决方案仅采用元相机进行统一表示，但缺乏全面的考虑。在本文中，我们重新审视这个问题，并发现问题在于源配置和目标配置之间的空间先验差异，包括不同的内参、外参和阵列布局。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了CoIn3D，一种可泛化的MC3D框架，能够实现从源配置到未知目标配置的强大迁移能力。CoIn3D通过空间感知特征调制（SFM）和相机感知数据增强（CDA），将所有已识别的空间先验显式地融入到特征嵌入和图像观测中。SFM通过整合焦距、地面深度、地面梯度和普吕克坐标等四种空间表示来丰富特征空间。CDA通过一种免训练的动态新视角图像合成方案，提高了不同配置下的观测多样性。 大量实验表明，在以BEVDepth、BEVFormer和PETR为代表的三种主流MC3D范例下，CoIn3D在NuScenes、Waymo和Lyft等标志性数据集上实现了强大的跨配置性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces CoIn3D, a framework for multi-camera 3D object detection designed to generalize across different camera configurations by explicitly incorporating spatial priors into feature embedding and image observation. It achieves state-of-the-art cross-configuration performance on major datasets.

Authors: Zhaonian Kuang, Rui Ding, Haotian Wang, Xinhu Zheng, Meng Yang, Gang Hua

U-OBCA: Uncertainty-Aware Optimization-Based Collision Avoidance via Wasserstein Distributionally Robust Chance Constraints

Abstract (English): Uncertainties arising from localization error, trajectory prediction errors of the moving obstacles and environmental disturbances pose significant challenges to robot's safe navigation. Existing uncertainty-aware planners often approximate polygon-shaped robots and obstacles using simple geometric primitives such as circles or ellipses. Though computationally convenient, these approximations substantially shrink the feasible space, leading to overly conservative trajectories and even planning failure in narrow environments. In addition, many such methods rely on specific assumptions about noise distributions, which may not hold in practice and thus limit their performance guarantees. To address these limitations, we extend the Optimization-Based Collision Avoidance (OBCA) framework to an uncertainty-aware formulation, termed \emph{U-OBCA}. The proposed method explicitly accounts for the collision risk between polygon-shaped robots and obstacles by formulating OBCA-based chance constraints, and hence avoiding geometric simplifications and reducing unnecessary conservatism. These probabilistic constraints are further tightened into deterministic nonlinear constraints under mild distributional assumptions, which can be solved efficiently by standard numerical optimization solvers. The proposed approach is validated through theoretical analysis, numerical simulations and real-world experiments. The results demonstrate that U-OBCA significantly mitigates the conservatism in trajectory planning and achieves higher navigation efficiency compared to existing baseline methods, particularly in narrow and cluttered environments.

摘要（中文）: 由定位误差、移动障碍物轨迹预测误差和环境干扰引起的不确定性给机器人的安全导航带来了重大挑战。现有的不确定性感知规划器通常使用简单的几何基元（如圆形或椭圆形）来近似多边形机器人和障碍物。虽然在计算上很方便，但这些近似会大大缩小可行空间，导致过度保守的轨迹，甚至在狭窄环境中出现规划失败。此外，许多此类方法依赖于对噪声分布的特定假设，这些假设在实践中可能不成立，从而限制了它们的性能保证。为了解决这些局限性，我们将基于优化的避碰（OBCA）框架扩展到不确定性感知公式，称为\emph{U-OBCA}。所提出的方法通过制定基于OBCA的概率约束，明确考虑多边形机器人和障碍物之间的碰撞风险，从而避免了几何简化并减少了不必要的保守性。在温和的分布假设下，这些概率约束进一步收紧为确定性的非线性约束，这些约束可以通过标准数值优化求解器有效地求解。所提出的方法通过理论分析、数值模拟和实际实验进行了验证。结果表明，与现有的基线方法相比，U-OBCA显著降低了轨迹规划中的保守性，并实现了更高的导航效率，尤其是在狭窄和拥挤的环境中。

TLDR: The paper introduces U-OBCA, an uncertainty-aware optimization-based collision avoidance method that improves robot navigation efficiency by explicitly considering collision risks between polygon-shaped robots and obstacles, avoiding overly conservative trajectories.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了U-OBCA，一种不确定性感知的基于优化的避障方法，通过显式考虑多边形机器人和障碍物之间的碰撞风险，避免过于保守的轨迹，从而提高机器人导航效率。

Beyond the Patch: Exploring Vulnerabilities of Visuomotor Policies via Viewpoint-Consistent 3D Adversarial Object

Abstract (English): Neural network-based visuomotor policies enable robots to perform manipulation tasks but remain susceptible to perceptual attacks. For example, conventional 2D adversarial patches are effective under fixed-camera setups, where appearance is relatively consistent; however, their efficacy often diminishes under dynamic viewpoints from moving cameras, such as wrist-mounted setups, due to perspective distortions. To proactively investigate potential vulnerabilities beyond 2D patches, this work proposes a viewpoint-consistent adversarial texture optimization method for 3D objects through differentiable rendering. As optimization strategies, we employ Expectation over Transformation (EOT) with a Coarse-to-Fine (C2F) curriculum, exploiting distance-dependent frequency characteristics to induce textures effective across varying camera-object distances. We further integrate saliency-guided perturbations to redirect policy attention and design a targeted loss that persistently drives robots toward adversarial objects. Our comprehensive experiments show that the proposed method is effective under various environmental conditions, while confirming its black-box transferability and real-world applicability.

摘要（中文）: 基于神经网络的视觉运动策略使机器人能够执行操作任务，但仍然容易受到感知攻击。例如，传统的2D对抗补丁在固定摄像头设置下是有效的，在这些设置中，外观相对一致；然而，由于透视畸变，它们在来自移动摄像头的动态视角（例如，腕部安装设置）下的效力通常会降低。为了主动研究超越2D补丁的潜在漏洞，本文提出了一种基于可微渲染的3D物体的视角一致性对抗纹理优化方法。作为优化策略，我们采用带有粗到细（C2F）课程的学习预期转换（EOT），利用距离相关的频率特性来诱导在不同相机-物体距离下有效的纹理。我们进一步整合了显著性引导的扰动来重定向策略注意力，并设计了一个目标损失，以持续地将机器人推向对抗性物体。我们全面的实验表明，所提出的方法在各种环境条件下都是有效的，同时证实了其黑盒可迁移性和现实世界的适用性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a method for generating viewpoint-consistent 3D adversarial textures on objects to attack visuomotor policies, demonstrating its effectiveness in both simulated and real-world scenarios with black-box transferability.

Authors: Chanmi Lee, Minsung Yoon, Woojae Kim, Sebin Lee, Sung-eui Yoon

Task-Relevant and Irrelevant Region-Aware Augmentation for Generalizable Vision-Based Imitation Learning in Agricultural Manipulation

Abstract (English): Vision-based imitation learning has shown promise for robotic manipulation; however, its generalization remains limited in practical agricultural tasks. This limitation stems from scarce demonstration data and substantial visual domain gaps caused by i) crop-specific appearance diversity and ii) background variations. To address this limitation, we propose Dual-Region Augmentation for Imitation Learning (DRAIL), a region-aware augmentation framework designed for generalizable vision-based imitation learning in agricultural manipulation. DRAIL explicitly separates visual observations into task-relevant and task-irrelevant regions. The task-relevant region is augmented in a domain-knowledge-driven manner to preserve essential visual characteristics, while the task-irrelevant region is aggressively randomized to suppress spurious background correlations. By jointly handling both sources of visual variation, DRAIL promotes learning policies that rely on task-essential features rather than incidental visual cues. We evaluate DRAIL on diffusion policy-based visuomotor controllers through robot experiments on artificial vegetable harvesting and real lettuce defective leaf picking preparation tasks. The results show consistent improvements in success rates under unseen visual conditions compared to baseline methods. Further attention analysis and representation generalization metrics indicate that the learned policies rely more on task-essential visual features, resulting in enhanced robustness and generalization.

摘要（中文）: 基于视觉的模仿学习在机器人操作领域展现了潜力，但其泛化能力在实际农业任务中仍然有限。这种局限性源于稀缺的示范数据以及由i)作物特定的外观多样性和ii)背景变化造成的显著视觉领域差异。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种用于模仿学习的双区域增强方法（DRAIL），这是一种区域感知增强框架，专为农业操作中可泛化的基于视觉的模仿学习而设计。DRAIL显式地将视觉观察结果分为任务相关区域和任务无关区域。任务相关区域以领域知识驱动的方式进行增强，以保留必要的视觉特征，而任务无关区域则被积极地随机化，以抑制虚假的背景相关性。通过联合处理两种视觉变化来源，DRAIL促进了依赖于任务必要特征而非偶然视觉线索的学习策略。我们通过在人工蔬菜收获和真实生菜残叶采摘准备任务中的机器人实验，在基于扩散策略的视觉运动控制器上评估了DRAIL。结果表明，与基线方法相比，在未见过的视觉条件下，成功率得到了持续提高。进一步的注意力分析和表征泛化指标表明，学习策略更多地依赖于任务必要的视觉特征，从而提高了鲁棒性和泛化能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces DRAIL, a region-aware augmentation framework for vision-based imitation learning in agricultural robotics, improving generalization by augmenting task-relevant and irrelevant regions differently. It shows improved performance on vegetable harvesting and lettuce preparation tasks.

Authors: Shun Hattori, Hikaru Sasaki, Takumi Hachimine, Yusuke Mizutani, Takamitsu Matsubara

Data-Driven Control of a Magnetically Actuated Fish-Like Robot

Abstract (English): Magnetically actuated fish-like robots offer promising solutions for underwater exploration due to their miniaturization and agility; however, precise control remains a significant challenge because of nonlinear fluid dynamics, flexible fin hysteresis, and the variable-duration control steps inherent to the actuation mechanism. This paper proposes a comprehensive data-driven control framework to address these complexities without relying on analytical modeling. Our methodology comprises three core components: 1) developing a forward dynamics model (FDM) using a neural network trained on real-world experimental data to capture state transitions under varying time steps; 2) integrating this FDM into a gradient-based model predictive control (G-MPC) architecture to optimize control inputs for path following; and 3) applying imitation learning to approximate the G-MPC policy, thereby reducing the computational cost for real-time implementation. We validate the approach through simulations utilizing the identified dynamics model. The results demonstrate that the G-MPC framework achieves accurate path convergence with minimal root mean square error (RMSE), and the imitation learning controller (ILC) effectively replicates this performance. This study highlights the potential of data-driven control strategies for the precise navigation of miniature, fish-like soft robots.

摘要（中文）: 磁驱动鱼形机器人因其小型化和敏捷性，为水下探索提供了极具前景的解决方案；然而，由于非线性流体动力学、柔性鳍迟滞以及驱动机制固有的可变时长控制步长，精确控制仍然是一个重大挑战。本文提出了一种全面的数据驱动控制框架，以解决这些复杂性，而无需依赖解析建模。我们的方法包含三个核心组成部分：1）开发一个前向动力学模型 (FDM)，利用在真实世界实验数据上训练的神经网络来捕获不同时间步长下的状态转换；2）将此 FDM 集成到基于梯度的模型预测控制 (G-MPC) 架构中，以优化用于路径跟踪的控制输入；3）应用模仿学习来近似 G-MPC 策略，从而降低实时实现的计算成本。我们通过利用已识别动力学模型的仿真验证了该方法。结果表明，G-MPC 框架实现了精确的路径收敛，具有最小的均方根误差 (RMSE)，并且模仿学习控制器 (ILC) 有效地复制了这种性能。这项研究突出了数据驱动控制策略在微型、鱼形软机器人的精确导航中的潜力。

TLDR: This paper presents a data-driven control framework using neural networks, gradient-based model predictive control (G-MPC), and imitation learning for precise navigation of magnetically actuated fish-like robots in underwater environments, validated through simulations.

Authors: Akiyuki Koyama, Hiroaki Kawashima

Adaptive Policy Switching of Two-Wheeled Differential Robots for Traversing over Diverse Terrains

Abstract (English): Exploring lunar lava tubes requires robots to traverse without human intervention. Because pre-trained policies cannot fully cover all possible terrain conditions, our goal is to enable adaptive policy switching, where the robot selects an appropriate terrain-specialized model based on its current terrain features. This study investigates whether terrain types can be estimated effectively using posture-related observations collected during navigation. We fine-tuned a pre-trained policy using Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO), and then collected the robot's 3D orientation data as it moved across flat and rough terrain in a simulated lava-tube environment. Our analysis revealed that the standard deviation of the robot's pitch data shows a clear difference between these two terrain types. Using Gaussian mixture models (GMM), we evaluated terrain classification across various window sizes. An accuracy of more than 98% was achieved when using a 70-step window. The result suggests that short-term orientation data are sufficient for reliable terrain estimation, providing a foundation for adaptive policy switching.

摘要（中文）: 探索月球熔岩管需要机器人能够在无人干预的情况下进行穿越。由于预训练策略无法完全覆盖所有可能的地形条件，我们的目标是实现自适应策略切换，即机器人根据其当前的地形特征选择合适的地形专业模型。本研究探讨了是否可以利用导航过程中收集的姿态相关观测数据来有效地估计地形类型。我们使用近端策略优化（PPO）对预训练策略进行了微调，然后收集了机器人在模拟熔岩管环境中跨越平坦和粗糙地形时产生的3D姿态数据。我们的分析表明，机器人俯仰角数据的标准差在这两种地形类型之间表现出明显的差异。我们采用高斯混合模型（GMM）评估了不同窗口大小下的地形分类效果。使用70步窗口时，准确率超过98%。结果表明，短期姿态数据足以进行可靠的地形估计，为自适应策略切换奠定了基础。

TLDR: This paper explores using robot pitch data during navigation to classify terrain types in a simulated lunar lava tube environment, achieving high accuracy with Gaussian Mixture Models, which could enable adaptive policy switching for robots.

Authors: Haruki Izawa, Takeshi Takai, Shingo Kitano, Mikita Miyaguchi, Hiroaki Kawashima

Python Bindings for a Large C++ Robotics Library: The Case of OMPL

Abstract (English): Python bindings are a critical bridge between high-performance C++ libraries and the flexibility of Python, enabling rapid prototyping, reproducible experiments, and integration with simulation and learning frameworks in robotics research. Yet, generating bindings for large codebases is a tedious process that creates a heavy burden for a small group of maintainers. In this work, we investigate the use of Large Language Models (LLMs) to assist in generating nanobind wrappers, with human experts kept in the loop. Our workflow mirrors the structure of the C++ codebase, scaffolds empty wrapper files, and employs LLMs to fill in binding definitions. Experts then review and refine the generated code to ensure correctness, compatibility, and performance. Through a case study on a large C++ motion planning library, we document common failure modes, including mismanaging shared pointers, overloads, and trampolines, and show how in-context examples and careful prompt design improve reliability. Experiments demonstrate that the resulting bindings achieve runtime performance comparable to legacy solutions. Beyond this case study, our results provide general lessons for applying LLMs to binding generation in large-scale C++ projects.

摘要（中文）: Python绑定是高性能C++库和Python灵活性之间的关键桥梁，能够在机器人研究中实现快速原型设计、可复现实验，以及与仿真和学习框架的集成。然而，为大型代码库生成绑定是一个繁琐的过程，给一小部分维护人员带来沉重负担。在这项工作中，我们研究了使用大型语言模型（LLMs）来辅助生成nanobind包装器，并保持人类专家参与其中。我们的工作流程模仿C++代码库的结构，搭建空的包装器文件，并利用LLM填充绑定定义。然后，专家审查并完善生成的代码，以确保正确性、兼容性和性能。通过对一个大型C++运动规划库的案例研究，我们记录了常见的失败模式，包括共享指针、重载和跳转表管理不当，并展示了上下文示例和仔细的提示设计如何提高可靠性。实验表明，由此产生的绑定实现了与传统解决方案相当的运行时性能。除了这个案例研究，我们的结果为将LLM应用于大规模C++项目中的绑定生成提供了通用经验。

Authors: Weihang Guo, Theodoros Tyrovouzis, Lydia E. Kavraki

GIANT - Global Path Integration and Attentive Graph Networks for Multi-Agent Trajectory Planning

Abstract (English): This paper presents a novel approach to multi-robot collision avoidance that integrates global path planning with local navigation strategies, utilizing attentive graph neural networks to manage dynamic interactions among agents. We introduce a local navigation model that leverages pre-planned global paths, allowing robots to adhere to optimal routes while dynamically adjusting to environmental changes. The models robustness is enhanced through the introduction of noise during training, resulting in superior performance in complex, dynamic environments. Our approach is evaluated against established baselines, including NH-ORCA, DRL-NAV, and GA3C-CADRL, across various structurally diverse simulated scenarios. The results demonstrate that our model achieves consistently higher success rates, lower collision rates, and more efficient navigation, particularly in challenging scenarios where baseline models struggle. This work offers an advancement in multi-robot navigation, with implications for robust performance in complex, dynamic environments with varying degrees of complexity, such as those encountered in logistics, where adaptability is essential for accommodating unforeseen obstacles and unpredictable changes.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种新颖的多机器人避撞方法，该方法集成了全局路径规划和局部导航策略，并利用注意力图神经网络来管理智能体之间的动态交互。我们引入了一个局部导航模型，该模型利用预先规划的全局路径，使机器人能够在遵守最佳路线的同时动态适应环境变化。通过在训练过程中引入噪声，提高了模型的鲁棒性，从而在复杂的动态环境中获得了卓越的性能。我们通过各种结构多样的模拟场景，将我们的方法与已建立的基线方法进行评估，包括 NH-ORCA、DRL-NAV 和 GA3C-CADRL。结果表明，我们的模型在具有挑战性的场景中，即基线模型表现不佳的情况下，始终能够实现更高的成功率、更低的碰撞率和更高效的导航。这项工作为多机器人导航提供了一项进步，对于在复杂的、动态的、且具有不同复杂程度环境中实现稳健的性能具有重要意义，例如在物流中遇到的情况，其中适应性对于适应无法预见的障碍和不可预测的变化至关重要。

TLDR: The paper introduces GIANT, a novel approach for multi-robot collision avoidance using attentive graph neural networks and global path integration, achieving superior performance compared to baselines in complex environments.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为GIANT的新型多机器人避撞方法，该方法使用注意力图神经网络和全局路径积分，与现有方法相比，在复杂环境中实现了更优越的性能。

Authors: Jonas le Fevre Sejersen, Toyotaro Suzumura, Erdal Kayacan

Autonomous Aerial Non-Destructive Testing: Ultrasound Inspection with a Commercial Quadrotor in an Unstructured Environment

Abstract (English): This work presents an integrated control and software architecture that enables arguably the first fully autonomous, contact-based non-destructive testing (NDT) using a commercial multirotor originally restricted to remotely-piloted operations. To allow autonomous operation with an off-the-shelf platform, we developed a real-time framework that interfaces directly with its onboard sensor suite. The architecture features a multi-rate control scheme: low-level control is executed at 200 Hz, force estimation at 100 Hz, while an admittance filter and trajectory planner operate at 50 Hz, ultimately supplying acceleration and yaw rate commands to the internal flight controller. We validate the system through physical experiments on a Flyability Elios 3 quadrotor equipped with an ultrasound payload. Relying exclusively on onboard sensing, the vehicle successfully performs autonomous NDT measurements within an unstructured, industrial-like environment. This work demonstrates the viability of retrofitting off-the-shelf platforms for autonomous physical interaction, paving the way for safe, contact-based inspection of hazardous and confined infrastructure.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种集成的控制和软件架构，该架构使得首个完全自主的、基于接触式的无损检测(NDT)成为可能，所使用的平台原本是仅限遥控操作的商用多旋翼飞行器。为了实现基于现有平台的自主操作，我们开发了一个实时框架，该框架直接与机载传感器套件交互。该架构的特点是一种多速率控制方案：底层控制以200赫兹的频率执行，力估计以100赫兹的频率执行，而导纳滤波器和轨迹规划器以50赫兹的频率运行，最终为内置飞行控制器提供加速度和偏航率指令。我们通过在配备超声波载荷的Flyability Elios 3四旋翼飞行器上进行的物理实验来验证该系统。仅依赖机载传感，该飞行器便能在非结构化的、类似工业的环境中成功执行自主NDT测量。这项工作证明了对现有平台进行改造以实现自主物理交互的可行性，为危险和受限基础设施的安全、基于接触的检测铺平了道路。

TLDR: This paper presents a system for autonomous non-destructive testing using a commercial quadrotor fitted with an ultrasound payload, demonstrating its capability in unstructured industrial environments.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种使用配备超声波载荷的商用四旋翼飞行器进行自主无损检测的系统，展示了其在非结构化工业环境中的能力。

Authors: Ruben Veenstra, Barbara Bazzana, Sander Smits, Antonio Franchi

Risk-Aware Rulebooks for Multi-Objective Trajectory Evaluation under Uncertainty

Abstract (English): We present a risk-aware formalism for evaluating system trajectories in the presence of uncertain interactions between the system and its environment. The proposed formalism supports reasoning under uncertainty and systematically handles complex relationships among requirements and objectives, including hierarchical priorities and non-comparability. Rather than treating the environment as exogenous noise, we explicitly model how each system trajectory influences the environment and evaluate trajectories under the resulting distribution of environment responses. We prove that the formalism induces a preorder on the set of system trajectories, ensuring consistency and preventing cyclic preferences. Finally, we illustrate the approach with an autonomous driving example that demonstrates how the formalism enhances explainability by clarifying the rationale behind trajectory selection.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出一种风险感知的形式化方法，用于在系统与其环境之间存在不确定性交互的情况下评估系统轨迹。所提出的形式化方法支持不确定性推理，并系统地处理需求和目标之间的复杂关系，包括分层优先级和不可比性。我们并非将环境视为外生噪声，而是显式地建模每个系统轨迹如何影响环境，并在由此产生的环境响应分布下评估轨迹。我们证明该形式化方法在系统轨迹集合上诱导出一个预序关系，从而确保一致性并防止循环偏好。最后，我们通过一个自动驾驶示例来展示该方法，该示例表明该形式化方法通过阐明轨迹选择背后的基本原理来增强可解释性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a risk-aware formalism for trajectory evaluation under uncertainty, particularly within complex environments like autonomous driving, emphasizing explainability and consistent preferences.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种风险感知的形式化方法，用于在不确定性下评估轨迹，特别是在自动驾驶等复杂环境中，强调可解释性和一致的偏好。

Authors: Tichakorn Wongpiromsarn

ELLIPSE: Evidential Learning for Robust Waypoints and Uncertainties

Abstract (English): Robust waypoint prediction is crucial for mobile robots operating in open-world, safety-critical settings. While Imitation Learning (IL) methods have demonstrated great success in practice, they are susceptible to distribution shifts: the policy can become dangerously overconfident in unfamiliar states. In this paper, we present \textit{ELLIPSE}, a method building on multivariate deep evidential regression to output waypoints and multivariate Student-t predictive distributions in a single forward pass. To reduce covariate-shift-induced overconfidence under viewpoint and pose perturbations near expert trajectories, we introduce a lightweight domain augmentation procedure that synthesizes plausible viewpoint/pose variations without collecting additional demonstrations. To improve uncertainty reliability under environment/domain shift (e.g., unseen staircases), we apply a post-hoc isotonic recalibration on probability integral transform (PIT) values so that prediction sets remain plausible during deployment. We ground the discussion and experiments in staircase waypoint prediction, where obtaining robust waypoint and uncertainty is pivotal. Extensive real world evaluations show that \textit{ELLIPSE} improves both task success rate and uncertainty coverage compared to baselines.

摘要（中文）: 在开放世界和安全关键的环境中运行的移动机器人，鲁棒的路点预测至关重要。虽然模仿学习（IL）方法在实践中已表现出巨大的成功，但它们容易受到分布偏移的影响：策略在不熟悉的状态下可能会变得危险地过于自信。在本文中，我们提出了一种名为\textit{ELLIPSE}的方法，该方法基于多元深度证据回归，可以在一次前向传递中输出路点和多元Student-t预测分布。为了减少专家轨迹附近视角和姿态扰动所引起的协变量偏移导致的过度自信，我们引入了一种轻量级的领域增强程序，该程序在不收集额外演示的情况下合成合理的视角/姿态变化。为了提高环境/领域偏移（例如，未见过的楼梯）下的不确定性可靠性，我们对概率积分变换（PIT）值应用事后等张重校准，以保证预测集在部署期间保持合理。我们以楼梯路点预测为基础进行讨论和实验，其中获得鲁棒的路点和不确定性至关重要。大量的真实世界评估表明，与基线方法相比，\textit{ELLIPSE}提高了任务成功率和不确定性覆盖率。

TLDR: The paper introduces ELLIPSE, a method for robust waypoint prediction with calibrated uncertainty estimates using evidential learning, domain augmentation, and isotonic recalibration, demonstrating improved performance in real-world staircase navigation.

简要说明: 本文介绍了ELLIPSE，一种使用证据学习、领域增强和等渗再校准的鲁棒路径点预测方法，该方法具有校准的不确定性估计，并在现实世界的楼梯导航中表现出改进的性能。

Authors: Zihao Dong, Chanyoung Chung, Dong-Ki Kim, Mukhtar Maulimov, Xiangyun Meng, Harmish Khambhaita, Ali-akbar Agha-mohammadi, Amirreza Shaban

Many-RRT*: Robust Joint-Space Trajectory Planning for Serial Manipulators

Abstract (English): The rapid advancement of high degree-of-freedom (DoF) serial manipulators necessitates the use of swift, sampling-based motion planners for high-dimensional spaces. While sampling-based planners like the Rapidly-Exploring Random Tree (RRT) are widely used, planning in the manipulator's joint space presents significant challenges due to non-invertible forward kinematics. A single task-space end-effector pose can correspond to multiple configuration-space states, creating a multi-arm bandit problem for the planner. In complex environments, simply choosing the wrong joint space goal can result in suboptimal trajectories or even failure to find a viable plan. To address this planning problem, we propose Many-RRT*: an extension of RRT*-Connect that plans to multiple goals in parallel. By generating multiple IK solutions and growing independent trees from these goal configurations simultaneously alongside a single start tree, Many-RRT* ensures that computational effort is not wasted on suboptimal IK solutions. This approach maintains robust convergence and asymptotic optimality. Experimental evaluations across robot morphologies and diverse obstacle environments demonstrate that Many-RRT* provides higher quality trajectories (44.5% lower cost in the same runtime) with a significantly higher success rate (100% vs. the next best of 1.6%) than previous RRT iterations without compromising on runtime performance.

摘要（中文）: 高自由度串联机械臂的快速发展，促使人们在高维空间中使用快速的基于采样的运动规划器。虽然像快速探索随机树(RRT)这样的基于采样的规划器被广泛使用，但由于不可逆的正向运动学，在机械臂关节空间中进行规划面临着重大挑战。单个任务空间末端执行器姿态可能对应于多个配置空间状态，从而为规划器创建了一个多臂老虎机问题。在复杂环境中，仅仅选择错误的关节空间目标就可能导致次优轨迹，甚至无法找到可行的规划。为了解决这个规划问题，我们提出了Many-RRT*: 它是RRT*-Connect的扩展，能够并行地规划到多个目标。通过生成多个逆运动学(IK)解，并与单个起始树同时从这些目标配置中增长独立的树，Many-RRT*确保计算资源不会浪费在次优的IK解上。这种方法保持了鲁棒的收敛性和渐近最优性。在不同的机器人形态和各种障碍环境中的实验评估表明，与之前的RRT迭代算法相比，Many-RRT*提供了更高质量的轨迹（在相同的运行时间内成本降低了44.5%），并且具有明显更高的成功率（100% vs. 次优的1.6% ），而且不以牺牲运行时间性能为代价。

TLDR: The paper introduces Many-RRT*, an extension of RRT*-Connect for robotic trajectory planning, which simultaneously explores multiple inverse kinematics solutions to significantly improve trajectory quality and success rate in complex environments without compromising runtime.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 Many-RRT*，这是 RRT*-Connect 的扩展，用于机器人轨迹规划，它同时探索多个逆运动学解决方案，从而在不影响运行时间的情况下显著提高复杂环境中轨迹的质量和成功率。

Authors: Theodore M. Belmont, Benjamin A. Christie, Anton Netchaev

PTLD: Sim-to-real Privileged Tactile Latent Distillation for Dexterous Manipulation

Abstract (English): Tactile dexterous manipulation is essential to automating complex household tasks, yet learning effective control policies remains a challenge. While recent work has relied on imitation learning, obtaining high quality demonstrations for multi-fingered hands via robot teleoperation or kinesthetic teaching is prohibitive. Alternatively, with reinforcement we can learn skills in simulation, but fast and realistic simulation of tactile observations is challenging. To bridge this gap, we introduce PTLD: sim-to-real Privileged Tactile Latent Distillation, a novel approach to learning tactile manipulation skills without requiring tactile simulation. Instead of simulating tactile sensors or relying purely on proprioceptive policies to transfer zero-shot sim-to-real, our key idea is to leverage privileged sensors in the real world to collect real-world tactile policy data. This data is then used to distill a robust state estimator that operates on tactile input. We demonstrate from our experiments that PTLD can be used to improve proprioceptive manipulation policies trained in simulation significantly by incorporating tactile sensing. On the benchmark in-hand rotation task, PTLD achieves a 182% improvement over a proprioception only policy. We also show that PTLD enables learning the challenging task of tactile in-hand reorientation where we see a 57% improvement in the number of goals reached over using proprioception alone. Website: https://akashsharma02.github.io/ptld-website/.

摘要（中文）: 触觉灵巧操作对于自动化复杂的家务任务至关重要，但学习有效的控制策略仍然是一个挑战。虽然最近的工作依赖于模仿学习，但通过机器人遥操作或动觉示教来获得多指手的优质演示是难以实现的。 或者，通过强化学习我们可以在仿真环境中学习技能，但快速且真实的触觉观察仿真具有挑战性。 为了弥合这一差距，我们引入了PTLD：sim-to-real 特权触觉潜在蒸馏，这是一种新颖的方法，可以在不需要触觉仿真的情况下学习触觉操作技能。我们的主要思想不是模拟触觉传感器或仅仅依赖本体感受策略来实现零样本sim-to-real迁移，而是利用现实世界中的特权传感器来收集现实世界的触觉策略数据。 这些数据随后被用于提炼一个在触觉输入上运行的鲁棒的状态估计器。 我们的实验表明，PTLD可以通过整合触觉感应，显著改善在仿真环境中训练的本体感受操作策略。 在基准的掌内旋转任务中，PTLD比仅使用本体感受的策略实现了182%的改进。 我们还表明，PTLD能够学习具有挑战性的触觉掌内重定向任务，在该任务中，我们观察到与单独使用本体感受相比，目标到达数量增加了57%。 项目网站：https://akashsharma02.github.io/ptld-website/。

TLDR: The paper introduces PTLD, a novel sim-to-real approach for tactile dexterous manipulation that uses privileged real-world tactile sensors to distill a robust state estimator, improving proprioceptive manipulation policies trained in simulation without relying on tactile simulation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了PTLD，一种新颖的触觉灵巧操作的模拟到真实的方法，它使用特权的真实世界触觉传感器来提炼一个强大的状态估计器，在不依赖触觉模拟的情况下，显著改善了模拟中训练的本体感受操作策略。

Authors: Rosy Chen, Mustafa Mukadam, Michael Kaess, Tingfan Wu, Francois R Hogan, Jitendra Malik, Akash Sharma

Logi-PAR: Logic-Infused Patient Activity Recognition via Differentiable Rule

Abstract (English): Patient Activity Recognition (PAR) in clinical settings uses activity data to improve safety and quality of care. Although significant progress has been made, current models mainly identify which activity is occurring. They often spatially compose sub-sparse visual cues using global and local attention mechanisms, yet only learn logically implicit patterns due to their neural-pipeline. Advancing clinical safety requires methods that can infer why a set of visual cues implies a risk, and how these can be compositionally reasoned through explicit logic beyond mere classification. To address this, we proposed Logi-PAR, the first Logic-Infused Patient Activity Recognition Framework that integrates contextual fact fusion as a multi-view primitive extractor and injects neural-guided differentiable rules. Our method automatically learns rules from visual cues, optimizing them end-to-end while enabling the implicit emergence patterns to be explicitly labelled during training. To the best of our knowledge, Logi-PAR is the first framework to recognize patient activity by applying learnable logic rules to symbolic mappings. It produces auditable why explanations as rule traces and supports counterfactual interventions (e.g., risk would decrease by 65% if assistance were present). Extensive evaluation on clinical benchmarks (VAST and OmniFall) demonstrates state-of-the-art performance, significantly outperforming Vision-Language Models and transformer baselines. The code is available via: https://github.com/zararkhan985/Logi-PAR.git}

摘要（中文）: 临床环境下的患者活动识别 (PAR) 利用活动数据来提高安全性和护理质量。尽管已经取得了显著进展，但目前的模型主要识别正在发生的活动。它们通常使用全局和局部注意力机制在空间上组合稀疏的视觉线索，但由于其神经管道的特性，只能学习到逻辑上隐式的模式。提升临床安全性需要能够推断出一组视觉线索为何暗示风险，以及如何通过显式逻辑进行组合推理的方法，而不仅仅是单纯的分类。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了 Logi-PAR，这是第一个逻辑注入的患者活动识别框架，它集成了上下文事实融合作为多视图原始特征提取器，并注入了神经引导的可微规则。我们的方法自动地从视觉线索中学习规则，对其进行端到端优化，同时使得在训练期间能够显式地标记隐式涌现的模式。据我们所知，Logi-PAR 是第一个通过应用可学习的逻辑规则到符号映射来识别患者活动的框架。它产生可审计的因果解释作为规则追踪，并支持反事实干预（例如，如果提供协助，风险将降低 65%）。在临床基准数据集（VAST 和 OmniFall）上的广泛评估表明，该方法实现了最先进的性能，显著优于视觉-语言模型和 Transformer 基线。代码可在以下网址获取：https://github.com/zararkhan985/Logi-PAR.git

TLDR: The paper introduces Logi-PAR, a novel framework for patient activity recognition that integrates contextual information and learns differentiable logic rules from visual cues for explainable and improved performance, outperforming existing vision-language models.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 Logi-PAR，一种用于患者活动识别的新型框架，集成了上下文信息并从视觉线索中学习可微分的逻辑规则，以实现可解释和改进的性能，优于现有的视觉-语言模型。

Authors: Muhammad Zarar, MingZheng Zhang, Xiaowang Zhang, Zhiyong Feng, Sofonias Yitagesu, Kawsar Farooq

BioLLMAgent: A Hybrid Framework with Enhanced Structural Interpretability for Simulating Human Decision-Making in Computational Psychiatry

Abstract (English): Computational psychiatry faces a fundamental trade-off: traditional reinforcement learning (RL) models offer interpretability but lack behavioral realism, while large language model (LLM) agents generate realistic behaviors but lack structural interpretability. We introduce BioLLMAgent, a novel hybrid framework that combines validated cognitive models with the generative capabilities of LLMs. The framework comprises three core components: (i) an Internal RL Engine for experience-driven value learning; (ii) an External LLM Shell for high-level cognitive strategies and therapeutic interventions; and (iii) a Decision Fusion Mechanism for integrating components via weighted utility. Comprehensive experiments on the Iowa Gambling Task (IGT) across six clinical and healthy datasets demonstrate that BioLLMAgent accurately reproduces human behavioral patterns while maintaining excellent parameter identifiability (correlations $>0.67$). Furthermore, the framework successfully simulates cognitive behavioral therapy (CBT) principles and reveals, through multi-agent dynamics, that community-wide educational interventions may outperform individual treatments. Validated across reward-punishment learning and temporal discounting tasks, BioLLMAgent provides a structurally interpretable "computational sandbox" for testing mechanistic hypotheses and intervention strategies in psychiatric research.

摘要（中文）: 计算精神病学面临着一个根本性的权衡：传统的强化学习（RL）模型具有可解释性，但缺乏行为的真实性，而大型语言模型（LLM）代理能够生成逼真的行为，但缺乏结构性的可解释性。我们提出了BioLLMAgent，一种新颖的混合框架，它将经过验证的认知模型与LLM的生成能力相结合。该框架包含三个核心组成部分：（i）用于经验驱动价值学习的内部RL引擎；（ii）用于高级认知策略和治疗干预的外部LLM外壳；以及（iii）用于通过加权效用整合各个组成部分的决策融合机制。在六个临床和健康数据集上进行的艾奥瓦赌博任务（IGT）的全面实验表明，BioLLMAgent能够准确地重现人类的行为模式，同时保持出色的参数可识别性（相关性>0.67）。此外，该框架成功地模拟了认知行为疗法（CBT）的原则，并通过多主体动态揭示了社区范围内的教育干预可能优于个体治疗。经过奖励-惩罚学习和时间折扣任务的验证，BioLLMAgent提供了一个结构上可解释的“计算沙盒”，用于在精神病学研究中测试机制性假设和干预策略。

TLDR: The paper introduces BioLLMAgent, a hybrid framework combining reinforcement learning and large language models for simulating human decision-making in computational psychiatry, achieving both behavioral realism and structural interpretability.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了BioLLMAgent，一个结合了强化学习和大型语言模型的混合框架，用于模拟计算精神病学中的人类决策，实现了行为真实性和结构可解释性。

Authors: Zuo Fei, Kezhi Wang, Xiaomin Chen, Yizhou Huang

SCoUT: Scalable Communication via Utility-Guided Temporal Grouping in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Communication can improve coordination in partially observed multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), but learning \emph{when} and \emph{who} to communicate with requires choosing among many possible sender-recipient pairs, and the effect of any single message on future reward is hard to isolate. We introduce \textbf{SCoUT} (\textbf{S}calable \textbf{Co}mmunication via \textbf{U}tility-guided \textbf{T}emporal grouping), which addresses both these challenges via temporal and agent abstraction within traditional MARL. During training, SCoUT resamples \textit{soft} agent groups every \(K\) environment steps (macro-steps) via Gumbel-Softmax; these groups are latent clusters that induce an affinity used as a differentiable prior over recipients. Using the same assignments, a group-aware critic predicts values for each agent group and maps them to per-agent baselines through the same soft assignments, reducing critic complexity and variance. Each agent is trained with a three-headed policy: environment action, send decision, and recipient selection. To obtain precise communication learning signals, we derive counterfactual communication advantages by analytically removing each sender's contribution from the recipient's aggregated messages. This counterfactual computation enables precise credit assignment for both send and recipient-selection decisions. At execution time, all centralized training components are discarded and only the per-agent policy is run, preserving decentralized execution. Project website, videos and code: \hyperlink{https://scout-comm.github.io/}{https://scout-comm.github.io/}

摘要（中文）: 通信能够提升部分可观测多智能体强化学习 (MARL) 中的协作，但学习与 \emph{何时} 以及与 \emph{哪些} 智能体通信，需要在众多可能的发送者-接收者对中进行选择，且任何单条消息对未来奖励的影响都难以隔离。我们提出了 \textbf{SCoUT} (\textbf{S}calable \textbf{Co}mmunication via \textbf{U}tility-guided \textbf{T}emporal grouping，基于效用引导的时间分组的可\textbf{S}伸缩\textbf{Co}mmunication)，其通过传统 MARL 内的时间和智能体抽象来应对上述两个挑战。在训练期间，SCoUT 通过 Gumbel-Softmax 每 \(K\) 个环境步骤（宏步）重新采样 \textit{软} 智能体组；这些组是潜在的聚类，其诱导一种亲和力，用作接收者的可微先验。使用相同的分配，一个组感知的评论家预测每个智能体组的值，并通过相同的软分配将它们映射到各个智能体的基线，从而降低评论家的复杂性和方差。每个智能体都使用一个三头策略进行训练：环境动作、发送决策和接收者选择。为了获得精确的通信学习信号，我们通过从接收者的聚合消息中解析地去除每个发送者的贡献，从而导出反事实通信优势。这种反事实计算能够为发送和接收者选择决策提供精确的信用分配。在执行时，所有中心化训练组件都被丢弃，仅运行每个智能体的策略，从而保留了去中心化的执行。项目网站、视频和代码：\hyperlink{https://scout-comm.github.io/}{https://scout-comm.github.io/}

TLDR: The paper introduces SCoUT, a MARL method that uses utility-guided temporal grouping with counterfactual advantages for scalable and precise communication learning, enabling decentralized execution.

简要说明: 该论文提出了SCoUT，一种MARL方法，它采用效用引导的时间分组和反事实优势来实现可扩展和精确的通信学习，从而实现分散式执行。

Authors: Manav Vora, Gokul Puthumanaillam, Hiroyasu Tsukamoto, Melkior Ornik

HiMAP-Travel: Hierarchical Multi-Agent Planning for Long-Horizon Constrained Travel

Abstract (English): Sequential LLM agents fail on long-horizon planning with hard constraints like budgets and diversity requirements. As planning progresses and context grows, these agents drift from global constraints. We propose HiMAP-Travel, a hierarchical multi-agent framework that splits planning into strategic coordination and parallel day-level execution. A Coordinator allocates resources across days, while Day Executors plan independently in parallel. Three key mechanisms enable this: a transactional monitor enforcing budget and uniqueness constraints across parallel agents, a bargaining protocol allowing agents to reject infeasible sub-goals and trigger re-planning, and a single policy trained with GRPO that powers all agents through role conditioning. On TravelPlanner, HiMAP-Travel with Qwen3-8B achieves 52.78% validation and 52.65% test Final Pass Rate (FPR). In a controlled comparison with identical model, training, and tools, it outperforms the sequential DeepTravel baseline by +8.67~pp. It also surpasses ATLAS by +17.65~pp and MTP by +10.0~pp. On FlexTravelBench multi-turn scenarios, it achieves 44.34% (2-turn) and 37.42% (3-turn) FPR while reducing latency 2.5x through parallelization.

摘要（中文）: 顺序LLM智能体在具有预算和多样性要求等硬约束的长期规划中表现不佳。随着规划的进行和上下文的增长，这些智能体逐渐偏离全局约束。我们提出了HiMAP-Travel，一个分层多智能体框架，将规划分解为战略协调和并行的日级执行。一个协调器在不同日期之间分配资源，而日级执行器并行地独立规划。三个关键机制实现了这一点：一个事务性监视器，用于跨并行智能体强制执行预算和唯一性约束；一个允许智能体拒绝不可行的子目标并触发重新规划的协商协议；以及一个用GRPO训练的单一策略，通过角色条件化为所有智能体提供支持。在 TravelPlanner 上，使用 Qwen3-8B 的 HiMAP-Travel 实现了 52.78% 的验证集和 52.65% 的测试集最终通过率 (FPR)。在与使用相同模型、训练和工具的受控实验中，它比顺序 DeepTravel 基线高出 +8.67 个百分点。它也超过了 ATLAS +17.65 个百分点， MTP +10.0 个百分点。在 FlexTravelBench 多轮场景中，它实现了 44.34%（2 轮）和 37.42%（3 轮）的 FPR，同时通过并行化将延迟降低了 2.5 倍。

TLDR: HiMAP-Travel introduces a hierarchical multi-agent planning framework using a coordinator and parallel day-level executors, achieving state-of-the-art performance on long-horizon travel planning with constraints by using Qwen3-8B and a new training paradigm called GRPO.

简要说明: HiMAP-Travel 提出了一种分层多代理规划框架，使用协调器和并行的天级执行器，通过使用 Qwen3-8B 和一种名为 GRPO 的新训练范式，在具有约束的远程旅行规划中实现了最先进的性能。
