Authors: The Viet Bui, Wenjun Li, Yong Liu

Visioning Human-Agentic AI Teaming: Continuity, Tension, and Future Research

Abstract (English): Artificial intelligence is undergoing a structural transformation marked by the rise of agentic systems capable of open-ended action trajectories, generative representations and outputs, and evolving objectives. These properties introduce structural uncertainty into human-AI teaming (HAT), including uncertainty about behavior trajectories, epistemic grounding, and the stability of governing logics over time. Under such conditions, alignment cannot be secured through agreement on bounded outputs; it must be continuously sustained as plans unfold and priorities shift. We advance Team Situation Awareness (Team SA) theory, grounded in shared perception, comprehension, and projection, as an integrative anchor for this transition. While Team SA remains analytically foundational, its stabilizing logic presumes that shared awareness, once achieved, will support coordinated action through iterative updating. Agentic AI challenges this presumption. Our argument unfolds in two stages: first, we extend Team SA to reconceptualize both human and AI awareness under open-ended agency, including the sensemaking of projection congruence across heterogeneous systems. Second, we interrogate whether the dynamic processes traditionally assumed to stabilize teaming in relational interaction, cognitive learning, and coordination and control continue to function under adaptive autonomy. By distinguishing continuity from tension, we clarify where foundational insights hold and where structural uncertainty introduces strain, and articulate a forward-looking research agenda for HAT. The central challenge of HAT is not whether humans and AI can agree in the moment, but whether they can remain aligned as futures are continuously generated, revised, enacted, and governed over time.

摘要（中文）: 人工智能正在经历一场结构性转型，其标志是涌现出具有开放式行动轨迹、生成式表征与输出以及不断演化目标的主动系统。这些特性给人类-人工智能团队协作（HAT）带来了结构性不确定性，包括行为轨迹、认知基础和控制逻辑随时间推移的稳定性等方面的不确定性。在这种情况下，对齐无法通过对有限输出的共识来确保，而必须在计划展开和优先级转移的过程中持续维持。我们以共享感知、理解和预测为基础，推进团队情境意识（Team SA）理论，将其作为这一转变的整合锚点。虽然团队情境意识在分析上仍然具有基础性，但其稳定逻辑假定，一旦达成共享意识，它将通过迭代更新来支持协调行动。主动型人工智能挑战了这一假设。我们的论证分两个阶段进行：首先，我们扩展团队情境意识，以重新概念化开放式主动性下的人和人工智能的意识，包括对异构系统间预测一致性的理解。其次，我们探讨传统上认为能在关系互动、认知学习以及协调和控制中稳定团队协作的动态过程，在自适应自主性下是否继续发挥作用。通过区分连续性和张力，我们阐明了基础性见解在何处适用，以及结构性不确定性在何处引入压力，并阐述了一个面向未来的HAT研究议程。HAT的核心挑战不是人类和人工智能是否能在当下达成一致，而是它们在未来不断生成、修订、实施和管理的过程中，能否保持对齐。

TLDR: This paper examines the challenges that agentic AI systems (capable of open-ended actions and evolving objectives) pose for human-AI teaming, proposing to adapt Team Situation Awareness theory to handle uncertainty and maintain alignment over time. It identifies areas of continuity and tension in traditional teaming approaches, suggesting a forward-looking research agenda.

简要说明: 本文探讨了具有开放式行动和不断变化目标的智能AI系统对人机协作带来的挑战，并提出调整团队情境意识理论以应对不确定性并维持长期对齐。它确定了传统协作方法中的连续性和紧张性领域，并提出了前瞻性的研究议程。

Authors: Bowen Lou, Tian Lu, T. S. Raghu, Yingjie Zhang

Robustness of Agentic AI Systems via Adversarially-Aligned Jacobian Regularization

Abstract (English): As Large Language Models (LLMs) transition into autonomous multi-agent ecosystems, robust minimax training becomes essential yet remains prone to instability when highly non-linear policies induce extreme local curvature in the inner maximization. Standard remedies that enforce global Jacobian bounds are overly conservative, suppressing sensitivity in all directions and inducing a large Price of Robustness. We introduce Adversarially-Aligned Jacobian Regularization (AAJR), a trajectory-aligned approach that controls sensitivity strictly along adversarial ascent directions. We prove that AAJR yields a strictly larger admissible policy class than global constraints under mild conditions, implying a weakly smaller approximation gap and reduced nominal performance degradation. Furthermore, we derive step-size conditions under which AAJR controls effective smoothness along optimization trajectories and ensures inner-loop stability. These results provide a structural theory for agentic robustness that decouples minimax stability from global expressivity restrictions.

摘要（中文）: 随着大型语言模型（LLM）过渡到自主多智能体生态系统，稳健的极小极大训练变得至关重要，但当高度非线性策略在内部最大化中引起极端的局部曲率时，仍然容易出现不稳定。强制全局雅可比矩阵边界的标准方法过于保守，抑制了所有方向上的敏感性，并导致了巨大的稳健性代价。我们引入了对抗对齐的雅可比矩阵正则化（AAJR），这是一种轨迹对齐的方法，严格控制了沿对抗性上升方向的敏感性。我们证明，在温和条件下，AAJR 相比于全局约束，会产生严格更大的容许策略类，这意味着近似差距的减小和标称性能退化的降低。此外，我们推导出步长条件，在该条件下，AAJR 控制了沿优化轨迹的有效平滑性，并确保了内循环的稳定性。这些结果为智能体稳健性提供了一个结构性理论，将极小极大稳定性与全局表达性限制解耦。

TLDR: The paper introduces Adversarially-Aligned Jacobian Regularization (AAJR) to improve the robustness of agentic AI systems, specifically LLMs in multi-agent settings, by addressing minimax training instability without sacrificing nominal performance through excessive global Jacobian constraints. They provide theoretical guarantees for AAJR's improved policy class and optimization stability.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种对抗对齐雅可比正则化（AAJR）方法，旨在提高智能体AI系统的鲁棒性，特别是多智能体环境中的LLM，并通过解决minimax训练的不稳定性，同时避免牺牲全局雅可比约束带来的标称性能下降。他们为AAJR更好的策略类和优化稳定性提供了理论保证。

Authors: Furkan Mumcu, Yasin Yilmaz

CATNet: Collaborative Alignment and Transformation Network for Cooperative Perception

Abstract (English): Cooperative perception significantly enhances scene understanding by integrating complementary information from diverse agents. However, existing research often overlooks critical challenges inherent in real-world multi-source data integration, specifically high temporal latency and multi-source noise. To address these practical limitations, we propose Collaborative Alignment and Transformation Network (CATNet), an adaptive compensation framework that resolves temporal latency and noise interference in multi-agent systems. Our key innovations can be summarized in three aspects. First, we introduce a Spatio-Temporal Recurrent Synchronization (STSync) that aligns asynchronous feature streams via adjacent-frame differential modeling, establishing a temporal-spatially unified representation space. Second, we design a Dual-Branch Wavelet Enhanced Denoiser (WTDen) that suppresses global noise and reconstructs localized feature distortions within aligned representations. Third, we construct an Adaptive Feature Selector (AdpSel) that dynamically focuses on critical perceptual features for robust fusion. Extensive experiments on multiple datasets demonstrate that CATNet consistently outperforms existing methods under complex traffic conditions, proving its superior robustness and adaptability.

摘要（中文）: 合作感知通过整合来自不同智能体的互补信息，显著增强对场景的理解。然而，现有的研究往往忽略了真实世界多源数据集成中固有的关键挑战，特别是高时间延迟和多源噪声。为了解决这些实际限制，我们提出了一种协作对齐与转换网络（CATNet），一个自适应补偿框架，用于解决多智能体系统中的时间延迟和噪声干扰。我们的主要创新可以概括为三个方面。首先，我们引入了一种时空循环同步（STSync），通过相邻帧差分建模对齐异步特征流，从而建立一个时空统一的表示空间。其次，我们设计了一种双分支小波增强去噪器（WTDen），它抑制全局噪声并重建对齐表示中的局部特征失真。第三，我们构建了一个自适应特征选择器（AdpSel），它动态地关注关键感知特征以实现稳健的融合。在多个数据集上的大量实验表明，在复杂的交通状况下，CATNet始终优于现有方法，证明了其卓越的鲁棒性和适应性。

TLDR: CATNet is a novel cooperative perception framework that handles temporal latency and multi-source noise through spatio-temporal synchronization, wavelet-enhanced denoising, and adaptive feature selection, demonstrating superior performance in complex traffic conditions.

简要说明: CATNet是一个新型的协同感知框架，通过时空同步、小波增强去噪和自适应特征选择来处理时间延迟和多源噪声，并在复杂的交通条件下表现出卓越的性能。

Authors: Gong Chen, Chaokun Zhang, Tao Tang, Pengcheng Lv, Feng Li, Xin Xie

TAPFormer: Robust Arbitrary Point Tracking via Transient Asynchronous Fusion of Frames and Events

Abstract (English): Tracking any point (TAP) is a fundamental yet challenging task in computer vision, requiring high precision and long-term motion reasoning. Recent attempts to combine RGB frames and event streams have shown promise, yet they typically rely on synchronous or non-adaptive fusion, leading to temporal misalignment and severe degradation when one modality fails. We introduce TAPFormer, a transformer-based framework that performs asynchronous temporal-consistent fusion of frames and events for robust and high-frequency arbitrary point tracking. Our key innovation is a Transient Asynchronous Fusion (TAF) mechanism, which explicitly models the temporal evolution between discrete frames through continuous event updates, bridging the gap between low-rate frames and high-rate events. In addition, a Cross-modal Locally Weighted Fusion (CLWF) module adaptively adjusts spatial attention according to modality reliability, yielding stable and discriminative features even under blur or low light. To evaluate our approach under realistic conditions, we construct a novel real-world frame-event TAP dataset under diverse illumination and motion conditions. Our method outperforms existing point trackers, achieving a 28.2% improvement in average pixel error within threshold. Moreover, on standard point tracking benchmarks, our tracker consistently achieves the best performance. Project website: tapformer.github.io

摘要（中文）: 跟踪任意点（TAP）是计算机视觉中一项基础但具有挑战性的任务，它需要高精度和长期的运动推理。最近结合RGB帧和事件流的尝试显示出前景，但它们通常依赖于同步或非自适应融合，当一种模态失效时，会导致时间上的错位和严重的性能下降。我们提出了 TAPFormer，一个基于 Transformer 的框架，用于对帧和事件进行异步的、时间一致性的融合，以实现鲁棒和高频率的任意点跟踪。我们的关键创新是一种瞬态异步融合（TAF）机制，该机制通过连续的事件更新显式地对离散帧之间的时间演化进行建模，从而弥合了低帧率帧和高帧率事件之间的差距。此外，跨模态局部加权融合（CLWF）模块根据模态的可靠性自适应地调整空间注意力，即使在模糊或低光照条件下也能产生稳定且具有区分性的特征。为了在真实条件下评估我们的方法，我们构建了一个新的真实世界帧-事件 TAP 数据集，该数据集涵盖了各种光照和运动条件。我们的方法优于现有的点跟踪器，在阈值范围内平均像素误差提高了 28.2%。此外，在标准点跟踪基准测试中，我们的跟踪器始终取得最佳性能。项目网站：tapformer.github.io

TLDR: The paper introduces TAPFormer, a transformer-based framework for robust point tracking using asynchronous fusion of frames and event streams, achieving state-of-the-art performance on various datasets, including a novel real-world frame-event TAP dataset.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为TAPFormer的基于Transformer的框架，用于通过异步融合帧和事件流来实现鲁棒的点跟踪。该方法在各种数据集上取得了最先进的性能，包括一个新的真实世界的帧-事件TAP数据集。

Authors: Jiaxiong Liu, Zhen Tan, Jinpu Zhang, Yi Zhou, Hui Shen, Xieyuanli Chen, Dewen Hu

SURE: Semi-dense Uncertainty-REfined Feature Matching

Abstract (English): Establishing reliable image correspondences is essential for many robotic vision problems. However, existing methods often struggle in challenging scenarios with large viewpoint changes or textureless regions, where incorrect cor- respondences may still receive high similarity scores. This is mainly because conventional models rely solely on fea- ture similarity, lacking an explicit mechanism to estimate the reliability of predicted matches, leading to overconfident errors. To address this issue, we propose SURE, a Semi- dense Uncertainty-REfined matching framework that jointly predicts correspondences and their confidence by modeling both aleatoric and epistemic uncertainties. Our approach in- troduces a novel evidential head for trustworthy coordinate regression, along with a lightweight spatial fusion module that enhances local feature precision with minimal overhead. We evaluated our method on multiple standard benchmarks, where it consistently outperforms existing state-of-the-art semi-dense matching models in both accuracy and efficiency. our code will be available on https://github.com/LSC-ALAN/SURE.

摘要（中文）: 建立可靠的图像对应关系对于许多机器人视觉问题至关重要。 然而，现有方法在具有大视点变化或无纹理区域的具有挑战性的场景中经常遇到困难，在这些场景中，不正确的对应关系仍然可能获得高相似度评分。 这主要是因为传统模型仅依赖于特征相似性，缺乏显式机制来估计预测匹配的可靠性，从而导致过度自信的错误。 为了解决这个问题，我们提出了SURE，一种半稠密不确定性精炼匹配框架，通过对偶然不确定性和认知不确定性建模，联合预测对应关系及其置信度。 我们的方法引入了一种用于可信坐标回归的新型证据头，以及一个轻量级的空间融合模块，该模块以最小的开销增强了局部特征的精度。 我们在多个标准基准上评估了我们的方法，结果表明，在准确性和效率方面，该方法始终优于现有的最先进的半稠密匹配模型。 我们的代码将在https://github.com/LSC-ALAN/SURE上提供。

TLDR: The paper introduces SURE, a semi-dense feature matching framework that jointly predicts correspondences and their confidence by modeling both aleatoric and epistemic uncertainties to improve robustness in challenging visual scenarios.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了SURE，一种半稠密特征匹配框架，通过对偶然和认知不确定性进行建模，联合预测对应关系及其置信度，从而提高在具有挑战性的视觉场景中的鲁棒性。

Authors: Sicheng Li, Zaiwang Gu, Jie Zhang, Qing Guo, Xudong Jiang, Jun Cheng

Replaying pre-training data improves fine-tuning

Abstract (English): To obtain a language model for a target domain (e.g. math), the current paradigm is to pre-train on a vast amount of generic web text and then fine-tune on the relatively limited amount of target data. Typically, generic data is only mixed in during fine-tuning to prevent catastrophic forgetting of the generic domain. We surprisingly find that replaying the generic data during fine-tuning can actually improve performance on the (less related) target task. Concretely, in a controlled pre-training environment with 4M target tokens, 4B total tokens, and 150M parameter models, generic replay increases target data efficiency by up to $1.87\times$ for fine-tuning and $2.06\times$ for mid-training. We further analyze data schedules that introduce target data during pre-training and find that replay helps more when there is less target data present in pre-training. We demonstrate the success of replay in practice for fine-tuning 8B parameter models, improving agentic web navigation success by $4.5\%$ and Basque question-answering accuracy by $2\%$.

摘要（中文）: 为了获得目标领域（如数学）的语言模型，目前的范式是在大量通用网络文本上进行预训练，然后在相对有限的目标数据上进行微调。通常，仅在微调期间混合通用数据以防止通用领域的灾难性遗忘。我们惊人地发现，在微调期间重放通用数据实际上可以提高在（关联度较低的）目标任务上的性能。具体来说，在一个受控的预训练环境中，拥有 400 万个目标 token，总共 40 亿个 token 和 1.5 亿参数的模型，通用数据重放将微调的目标数据效率提高了高达 1.87 倍，将中间训练的目标数据效率提高了高达 2.06 倍。我们进一步分析了在预训练期间引入目标数据的数据调度策略，发现当预训练中存在的目标数据较少时，重放的帮助更大。我们通过微调 80 亿参数的模型，在实践中展示了重放的成功之处，将智能体网络导航成功率提高了 4.5%，并将巴斯克语问答准确率提高了 2%。

TLDR: This paper surprisingly finds that replaying generic pre-training data during fine-tuning actually improves performance on target tasks, especially when the pre-training data contains limited target data. They demonstrate improvements in web navigation and question-answering.

简要说明: 该论文发现，在微调期间重放通用预训练数据实际上可以提高目标任务的性能，尤其是在预训练数据包含的目标数据有限的情况下。他们展示了在网络导航和问答方面的改进。

Authors: Yiang Wu, Qiong Wu, Pingyi Fan, Kezhi Wang, Wen Chen, Guoqiang Mao, Khaled B. Letaief

Loop Closure via Maximal Cliques in 3D LiDAR-Based SLAM

Abstract (English): Reliable loop closure detection remains a critical challenge in 3D LiDAR-based SLAM, especially under sensor noise, environmental ambiguity, and viewpoint variation conditions. RANSAC is often used in the context of loop closures for geometric model fitting in the presence of outliers. However, this approach may fail, leading to map inconsistency. We introduce a novel deterministic algorithm, CliReg, for loop closure validation that replaces RANSAC verification with a maximal clique search over a compatibility graph of feature correspondences. This formulation avoids random sampling and increases robustness in the presence of noise and outliers. We integrated our approach into a real- time pipeline employing binary 3D descriptors and a Hamming distance embedding binary search tree-based matching. We evaluated it on multiple real-world datasets featuring diverse LiDAR sensors. The results demonstrate that our proposed technique consistently achieves a lower pose error and more reliable loop closures than RANSAC, especially in sparse or ambiguous conditions. Additional experiments on 2D projection-based maps confirm its generality across spatial domains, making our approach a robust and efficient alternative for loop closure detection.

摘要（中文）: 在基于3D激光雷达的SLAM中，可靠的回环检测仍然是一个关键挑战，尤其是在传感器噪声、环境模糊和视点变化条件下。RANSAC常用于回环检测中，用于在存在异常值的情况下进行几何模型拟合。然而，这种方法可能会失败，导致地图不一致。我们引入了一种新的确定性算法CliReg，用于回环验证，它用最大团搜索特征对应关系的兼容性图来代替RANSAC验证。这种公式避免了随机抽样，并提高了在存在噪声和异常值时的鲁棒性。我们将我们的方法集成到一个实时流水线中，该流水线采用二进制3D描述符和一个基于哈明距离嵌入的二叉搜索树匹配。我们对多个具有不同激光雷达传感器的真实世界数据集进行了评估。结果表明，与RANSAC相比，我们提出的技术始终能够实现更低的位姿误差和更可靠的回环，尤其是在稀疏或模糊的条件下。在基于2D投影的地图上进行的额外实验证实了其在空间域的通用性，使我们的方法成为回环检测一个鲁棒且高效的替代方案。

TLDR: This paper introduces CliReg, a novel deterministic loop closure validation algorithm for 3D LiDAR SLAM that replaces RANSAC with maximal clique search, demonstrating improved robustness and accuracy, especially in challenging environments.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为CliReg的新型确定性回环闭合验证算法，用于3D激光雷达SLAM。该算法通过寻找最大团来替代RANSAC，从而在具有挑战性的环境中表现出更高的鲁棒性和准确性。

Authors: Javier Laserna, Saurabh Gupta, Oscar Martinez Mozos, Cyrill Stachniss, Pablo San Segundo

Curve-Induced Dynamical Systems on Riemannian Manifolds and Lie Groups

Abstract (English): Deploying robots in household environments requires safe, adaptable, and interpretable behaviors that respect the geometric structure of tasks. Often represented on Lie groups and Riemannian manifolds, this includes poses on SE(3) or symmetric positive definite matrices encoding stiffness or damping matrices. In this context, dynamical system-based approaches offer a natural framework for generating such behavior, providing stability and convergence while remaining responsive to changes in the environment. We introduce Curve-induced Dynamical systems on Smooth Manifolds (CDSM), a real-time framework for constructing dynamical systems directly on Riemannian manifolds and Lie groups. The proposed approach constructs a nominal curve on the manifold, and generates a dynamical system which combines a tangential component that drives motion along the curve and a normal component that attracts the state toward the curve. We provide a stability analysis of the resulting dynamical system and validate the method quantitatively. On an S2 benchmark, CDSM demonstrates improved trajectory accuracy, reduced path deviation, and faster generation and query times compared to state-of-the-art methods. Finally, we demonstrate the practical applicability of the framework on both a robotic manipulator, where poses on SE(3) and damping matrices on SPD(n) are adapted online, and a mobile manipulator.

摘要（中文）: 在家庭环境中部署机器人需要安全、适应性强且可解释的行为，这些行为要符合任务的几何结构。这些结构通常用李群和黎曼流形表示，包括SE(3)上的姿态，或编码刚度或阻尼矩阵的对称正定矩阵。在这种背景下，基于动力系统的方案为生成这种行为提供了一个自然的框架，在保持对环境变化响应的同时，提供了稳定性和收敛性。我们引入了光滑流形上的曲线诱导动力系统(CDSM)，这是一个用于直接在黎曼流形和李群上构建动力系统的实时框架。所提出的方法在流形上构建一条标称曲线，并生成一个动力系统，该系统结合了一个驱动沿曲线运动的切向分量和一个将状态吸引到曲线的法向分量。我们提供了所得动力系统的稳定性分析，并对该方法进行了定量验证。在S2基准测试中，与最先进的方法相比，CDSM展示了更高的轨迹精度、更小的路径偏差以及更快的生成和查询时间。最后，我们展示了该框架在机器人操纵臂和移动操纵臂上的实际应用，其中SE(3)上的姿态和SPD(n)上的阻尼矩阵都得到了在线调整。

TLDR: The paper introduces Curve-induced Dynamical systems on Smooth Manifolds (CDSM), a real-time framework for generating stable and adaptable robot behaviors on Riemannian manifolds and Lie groups, demonstrating improved performance in trajectory accuracy and reduced path deviation compared to state-of-the-art methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种曲线诱导光滑流形上的动力系统（CDSM），这是一个用于在黎曼流形和李群上生成稳定且适应性强的机器人行为的实时框架，与最先进的方法相比，在轨迹精度和路径偏差方面表现出更高的性能。

Authors: Saray Bakker, Martin Schonger, Tobias Löw, Javier Alonso-Mora, Sylvain Calinon

Gait Generation Balancing Joint Load and Mobility for Legged Modular Robots with Easily Detachable Joints

Abstract (English): While modular robots offer versatility, excessive joint torque during locomotion poses a significant risk of mechanical failure, especially for detachable joints. To address this, we propose an optimization framework using the NSGA-III algorithm. Unlike conventional approaches that prioritize mobility alone, our method derives Pareto optimal solutions to minimize joint load while maintaining necessary locomotion speed and stability. Simulations and physical experiments demonstrate that our approach successfully generates gait motions for diverse environments, such as slopes and steps, ensuring structural integrity without compromising overall mobility.

摘要（中文）: 模块化机器人在提供多功能性的同时，运动过程中过大的关节力矩会对机械故障构成重大风险，尤其是对于可拆卸关节。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一个采用NSGA-III算法的优化框架。与仅关注移动性的传统方法不同，我们的方法推导出帕累托最优解，在保持必要的运动速度和稳定性的同时，最小化关节负载。仿真和物理实验表明，我们的方法成功地为各种环境（例如斜坡和台阶）生成了步态运动，确保了结构完整性，而不会影响整体移动性。

TLDR: This paper introduces an optimization framework using NSGA-III to generate gait motions for modular robots, minimizing joint load while maintaining mobility to prevent mechanical failure, particularly in robots with detachable joints. They validated this with simulations and physical experiments.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种使用NSGA-III的优化框架，为模块化机器人生成步态运动，旨在最小化关节负荷并保持移动性，以防止机械故障，尤其是在具有可拆卸关节的机器人中。并通过仿真和物理实验验证了该方法。

Authors: Kennosuke Chihara, Takuya Kiyokawa, Kensuke Harada

Selecting Spots by Explicitly Predicting Intention from Motion History Improves Performance in Autonomous Parking

Abstract (English): In many applications of social navigation, existing works have shown that predicting and reasoning about human intentions can help robotic agents make safer and more socially acceptable decisions. In this work, we study this problem for autonomous valet parking (AVP), where an autonomous vehicle ego agent must drop off its passengers, explore the parking lot, find a parking spot, negotiate for the spot with other vehicles, and park in the spot without human supervision. Specifically, we propose an AVP pipeline that selects parking spots by explicitly predicting where other agents are going to park from their motion history using learned models and probabilistic belief maps. To test this pipeline, we build a simulation environment with reactive agents and realistic modeling assumptions on the ego agent, such as occlusion-aware observations, and imperfect trajectory prediction. Simulation experiments show that our proposed method outperforms existing works that infer intentions from future predicted motion or embed them implicitly in end-to-end models, yielding better results in prediction accuracy, social acceptance, and task completion. Our key insight is that, in parking, where driving regulations are more lax, explicit intention prediction is crucial for reasoning about diverse and ambiguous long-term goals, which cannot be reliably inferred from short-term motion prediction alone, but can be effectively learned from motion history.

摘要（中文）: 在社交导航的许多应用中，现有研究表明，预测和推理人类意图可以帮助机器人代理做出更安全和更符合社会规范的决策。在这项工作中，我们研究了自动代客泊车（AVP）中的这个问题，其中自动驾驶车辆主体必须放下乘客，探索停车场，找到停车位，与其他车辆协商该停车位，并在没有人为监督的情况下停入该车位。具体来说，我们提出了一种AVP流程，该流程通过显式预测其他代理将要停车的位置（基于它们使用学习模型和概率置信图的运动历史）来选择停车位。为了测试这个流程，我们构建了一个包含反应式代理的仿真环境，并对自动驾驶车辆主体进行了现实建模假设，例如感知遮挡的观测和不完美的轨迹预测。仿真实验表明，我们提出的方法优于从未来预测运动推断意图或将意图隐式嵌入到端到端模型中的现有工作，在预测准确性、社会接受度和任务完成度方面取得了更好的结果。我们的关键见解是，在停车场景中，驾驶规则较为宽松，显式意图预测对于推理多样化和模糊的长期目标至关重要，这些目标无法仅从短期运动预测中可靠推断出来，但可以有效地从运动历史中学习得到。

TLDR: The paper presents an autonomous valet parking (AVP) pipeline that improves performance by explicitly predicting other agents' parking intentions from their motion history, outperforming methods that rely on future motion prediction or end-to-end learning in simulations.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一个自动代客泊车 (AVP) 流程，通过明确预测其他车辆基于其运动历史的停车意图来提高性能，在模拟中优于依赖未来运动预测或端到端学习的方法。

Authors: Long Kiu Chung, David Isele, Faizan M. Tariq, Sangjae Bae, Shreyas Kousik, Jovin D'sa

EVMbench: Evaluating AI Agents on Smart Contract Security

Abstract (English): Smart contracts on public blockchains now manage large amounts of value, and vulnerabilities in these systems can lead to substantial losses. As AI agents become more capable at reading, writing, and running code, it is natural to ask how well they can already navigate this landscape, both in ways that improve security and in ways that might increase risk. We introduce EVMbench, an evaluation that measures the ability of agents to detect, patch, and exploit smart contract vulnerabilities. EVMbench draws on 117 curated vulnerabilities from 40 repositories and, in the most realistic setting, uses programmatic grading based on tests and blockchain state under a local Ethereum execution environment. We evaluate a range of frontier agents and find that they are capable of discovering and exploiting vulnerabilities end-to-end against live blockchain instances. We release code, tasks, and tooling to support continued measurement of these capabilities and future work on security.

摘要（中文）: 公共区块链上的智能合约目前管理着大量的价值，而这些系统中的漏洞可能导致重大损失。随着人工智能代理在读取、编写和运行代码方面的能力增强，很自然会提出一个问题：它们在多大程度上已经能够驾驭这一领域，无论是在提高安全性的方面，还是在可能增加风险的方面。我们介绍了EVMbench，一种评估代理检测、修补和利用智能合约漏洞能力的基准。EVMbench借鉴了来自40个代码仓库的117个精心策划的漏洞，并且在最真实的设置下，使用基于测试和本地以太坊执行环境下的区块链状态的程序化评分。我们评估了一系列前沿代理，发现它们有能力针对实时区块链实例端到端地发现和利用漏洞。我们发布代码、任务和工具，以支持对这些能力的持续测量和未来的安全工作。

TLDR: EVMbench is introduced to evaluate AI agents' ability to detect, patch, and exploit smart contract vulnerabilities, revealing that current frontier agents can successfully find and exploit vulnerabilities in live blockchain instances.

简要说明: EVMbench被提出用于评估AI代理检测、修补和利用智能合约漏洞的能力，结果显示当前的先进代理能够成功地在实时的区块链实例中发现和利用漏洞。

Authors: Justin Wang, Andreas Bigger, Xiaohai Xu, Justin W. Lin, Andy Applebaum, Tejal Patwardhan, Alpin Yukseloglu, Olivia Watkins

DARE: Aligning LLM Agents with the R Statistical Ecosystem via Distribution-Aware Retrieval

Abstract (English): Large Language Model (LLM) agents can automate data-science workflows, but many rigorous statistical methods implemented in R remain underused because LLMs struggle with statistical knowledge and tool retrieval. Existing retrieval-augmented approaches focus on function-level semantics and ignore data distribution, producing suboptimal matches. We propose DARE (Distribution-Aware Retrieval Embedding), a lightweight, plug-and-play retrieval model that incorporates data distribution information into function representations for R package retrieval. Our main contributions are: (i) RPKB, a curated R Package Knowledge Base derived from 8,191 high-quality CRAN packages; (ii) DARE, an embedding model that fuses distributional features with function metadata to improve retrieval relevance; and (iii) RCodingAgent, an R-oriented LLM agent for reliable R code generation and a suite of statistical analysis tasks for systematically evaluating LLM agents in realistic analytical scenarios. Empirically, DARE achieves an NDCG at 10 of 93.47%, outperforming state-of-the-art open-source embedding models by up to 17% on package retrieval while using substantially fewer parameters. Integrating DARE into RCodingAgent yields significant gains on downstream analysis tasks. This work helps narrow the gap between LLM automation and the mature R statistical ecosystem.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型 (LLM) 代理可以自动化数据科学工作流，但许多在 R 中实现的严谨统计方法仍未得到充分利用，因为 LLM 在统计知识和工具检索方面存在困难。 现有的检索增强方法侧重于函数级别的语义，忽略了数据分布，导致次优匹配。 我们提出了 DARE（分布感知检索嵌入），这是一种轻量级的、即插即用的检索模型，它将数据分布信息融入到函数表示中，用于 R 包检索。 我们的主要贡献是：(i) RPKB，一个从 8,191 个高质量 CRAN 包中提取的精选 R 包知识库；(ii) DARE，一个融合了分布特征和函数元数据以提高检索相关性的嵌入模型；以及 (iii) RCodingAgent，一个面向 R 的 LLM 代理，用于可靠的 R 代码生成，以及一套统计分析任务，用于在真实的分析场景中系统地评估 LLM 代理。 经验表明，DARE 在包检索方面实现了 93.47% 的 NDCG@10，优于最先进的开源嵌入模型高达 17%，同时使用的参数明显更少。 将 DARE 集成到 RCodingAgent 中可以显著提高下游分析任务的性能。 这项工作有助于缩小 LLM 自动化和成熟的 R 统计生态系统之间的差距。

TLDR: The paper introduces DARE, a retrieval model for R packages that incorporates data distribution information to improve the performance of LLM agents in data science workflows, demonstrating significant gains in package retrieval and downstream analysis tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了DARE，一种将数据分布信息纳入R软件包检索的检索模型，旨在提升LLM agent在数据科学工作流程中的性能，并在软件包检索和下游分析任务中表现出显著提升。

Authors: Maojun Sun, Yue Wu, Yifei Xie, Ruijian Han, Binyan Jiang, Defeng Sun, Yancheng Yuan, Jian Huang

ZipMap: Linear-Time Stateful 3D Reconstruction with Test-Time Training

Abstract (English): Feed-forward transformer models have driven rapid progress in 3D vision, but state-of-the-art methods such as VGGT and $π^3$ have a computational cost that scales quadratically with the number of input images, making them inefficient when applied to large image collections. Sequential-reconstruction approaches reduce this cost but sacrifice reconstruction quality. We introduce ZipMap, a stateful feed-forward model that achieves linear-time, bidirectional 3D reconstruction while matching or surpassing the accuracy of quadratic-time methods. ZipMap employs test-time training layers to zip an entire image collection into a compact hidden scene state in a single forward pass, enabling reconstruction of over 700 frames in under 10 seconds on a single H100 GPU, more than $20\times$ faster than state-of-the-art methods such as VGGT. Moreover, we demonstrate the benefits of having a stateful representation in real-time scene-state querying and its extension to sequential streaming reconstruction.

摘要（中文）: 前馈Transformer模型极大地推动了3D视觉的快速发展，但诸如VGGT和$π^3$等最先进的方法的计算成本随输入图像数量呈二次方增长，这使得它们在应用于大型图像集时效率低下。顺序重建方法降低了这种成本，但牺牲了重建质量。我们提出了ZipMap，一种有状态的前馈模型，它实现了线性时间、双向3D重建，同时达到或超过了二次时间方法的精度。ZipMap采用测试时训练层，在一次前向传递中将整个图像集压缩成一个紧凑的隐藏场景状态，从而能够在单个H100 GPU上于10秒内重建超过700帧，比诸如VGGT等最先进的方法快20倍以上。此外，我们还展示了有状态表示在实时场景状态查询以及将其扩展到顺序流式重建中的优势。

TLDR: ZipMap introduces a linear-time stateful feed-forward model for 3D reconstruction that achieves comparable accuracy to quadratic-time methods with significantly improved speed and efficiency via test-time training, also enabling real-time scene querying and streaming reconstruction.

简要说明: ZipMap 提出了一种线性时间的状态前馈模型，用于 3D 重建。通过测试时训练，该模型在显著提高速度和效率的同时，实现了与二次时间方法相当的精度，并且支持实时场景查询和流式重建。

Authors: Haian Jin, Rundi Wu, Tianyuan Zhang, Ruiqi Gao, Jonathan T. Barron, Noah Snavely, Aleksander Holynski

Dark3R: Learning Structure from Motion in the Dark

Abstract (English): We introduce Dark3R, a framework for structure from motion in the dark that operates directly on raw images with signal-to-noise ratios (SNRs) below $-4$ dB -- a regime where conventional feature- and learning-based methods break down. Our key insight is to adapt large-scale 3D foundation models to extreme low-light conditions through a teacher--student distillation process, enabling robust feature matching and camera pose estimation in low light. Dark3R requires no 3D supervision; it is trained solely on noisy--clean raw image pairs, which can be either captured directly or synthesized using a simple Poisson--Gaussian noise model applied to well-exposed raw images. To train and evaluate our approach, we introduce a new, exposure-bracketed dataset that includes $\sim$42,000 multi-view raw images with ground-truth 3D annotations, and we demonstrate that Dark3R achieves state-of-the-art structure from motion in the low-SNR regime. Further, we demonstrate state-of-the-art novel view synthesis in the dark using Dark3R's predicted poses and a coarse-to-fine radiance field optimization procedure.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了Dark3R，一个用于黑暗环境下的运动结构恢复框架，它直接作用于信噪比(SNR)低于$-4$分贝的原始图像上——在这个条件下，传统的基于特征和学习的方法会失效。我们的核心思想是通过教师-学生蒸馏过程，将大规模3D基础模型适应于极端的低光照环境，以实现低光照下的鲁棒特征匹配和相机位姿估计。Dark3R不需要3D监督；它仅在噪声-干净的原始图像对上进行训练，这些图像对可以直接捕获，也可以使用应用于良好曝光原始图像的简单泊松-高斯噪声模型合成。为了训练和评估我们的方法，我们引入了一个新的、包含$\sim$42,000张多视点原始图像的曝光包围数据集，该数据集带有真实3D标注，我们证明了Dark3R在低信噪比状态下实现了最先进的运动结构恢复效果。此外，我们还展示了使用Dark3R预测的位姿以及由粗到精的辐射场优化程序，在黑暗环境下实现了最先进的新视角合成效果。

TLDR: Dark3R enables structure from motion in extremely low-light conditions by adapting large-scale 3D foundation models using teacher-student distillation and requiring only noisy-clean raw image pairs for training, achieving state-of-the-art performance.

简要说明: Dark3R通过教师-学生蒸馏调整大型3D基础模型，实现了在极低光照条件下的运动结构重建，仅需噪声-干净原始图像对用于训练，并达到最先进的性能。

Authors: Andrew Y Guo, Anagh Malik, SaiKiran Tedla, Yutong Dai, Yiqian Qin, Zach Salehe, Benjamin Attal, Sotiris Nousias, Kyros Kutulakos, David B. Lindell

Distributional Reinforcement Learning with Information Bottleneck for Uncertainty-Aware DRAM Equalization

Abstract (English): Equalizer parameter optimization is critical for signal integrity in high-speed memory systems operating at multi-gigabit data rates. However, existing methods suffer from computationally expensive eye diagram evaluation, optimization of expected rather than worst-case performance, and absence of uncertainty quantification for deployment decisions. In this paper, we propose a distributional risk-sensitive reinforcement learning framework integrating Information Bottleneck latent representations with Conditional Value-at-Risk optimization. We introduce rate-distortion optimal signal compression achieving 51 times speedup over eye diagrams while quantifying epistemic uncertainty through Monte Carlo dropout. Distributional reinforcement learning with quantile regression enables explicit worst-case optimization, while PAC-Bayesian regularization certifies generalization bounds. Experimental validation on 2.4 million waveforms from eight memory units demonstrated mean improvements of 37.1\% and 41.5\% for 4-tap and 8-tap equalizer configurations with worst-case guarantees of 33.8\% and 38.2\%, representing 80.7\% and 89.1\% improvements over Q-learning baselines. The framework achieved 62.5\% high-reliability classification eliminating manual validation for most configurations. These results suggest the proposed framework provides a practical solution for production-scale equalizer optimization with certified worst-case guarantees.

摘要（中文）: 均衡器参数优化对于以多千兆位数据速率运行的高速存储系统中信号完整性至关重要。然而，现有方法存在计算代价高昂的眼图评估、对期望性能而非最坏情况性能的优化，以及缺乏对部署决策的不确定性量化等问题。在本文中，我们提出了一种分布式的风险敏感强化学习框架，将信息瓶颈潜在表示与条件风险价值(Conditional Value-at-Risk)优化相结合。我们引入了速率失真最优的信号压缩，在量化认知不确定性的同时，实现了相对于眼图51倍的速度提升（通过蒙特卡洛dropout）。使用分位数回归的分布式强化学习能够实现显式的最坏情况优化，而PAC-Bayes正则化则证明了泛化边界。对来自八个存储单元的240万个波形的实验验证表明，对于四阶和八阶均衡器配置，平均改进分别达到37.1%和41.5%，最坏情况保证分别达到33.8%和38.2%，分别代表了相对于Q-learning基线80.7%和89.1%的改进。该框架实现了62.5%的高可靠性分类，消除了大多数配置的手动验证。这些结果表明，所提出的框架为具有认证的最坏情况保证的生产规模均衡器优化提供了一种实用的解决方案。

TLDR: The paper introduces a distributional reinforcement learning framework with an information bottleneck for uncertainty-aware DRAM equalization, achieving significant performance improvements and worst-case guarantees compared to traditional methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种基于信息瓶颈的分布强化学习框架，用于具有不确定性感知的DRAM均衡，与传统方法相比，实现了显著的性能提升和最坏情况保证。

Authors: Muhammad Usama, Dong Eui Chang

A Constrained RL Approach for Cost-Efficient Delivery of Latency-Sensitive Applications

Abstract (English): Next-generation networks aim to provide performance guarantees to real-time interactive services that require timely and cost-efficient packet delivery. In this context, the goal is to reliably deliver packets with strict deadlines imposed by the application while minimizing overall resource allocation cost. A large body of work has leveraged stochastic optimization techniques to design efficient dynamic routing and scheduling solutions under average delay constraints; however, these methods fall short when faced with strict per-packet delay requirements. We formulate the minimum-cost delay-constrained network control problem as a constrained Markov decision process and utilize constrained deep reinforcement learning (CDRL) techniques to effectively minimize total resource allocation cost while maintaining timely throughput above a target reliability level. Results indicate that the proposed CDRL-based solution can ensure timely packet delivery even when existing baselines fall short, and it achieves lower cost compared to other throughput-maximizing methods.

摘要（中文）: 下一代网络旨在为需要及时且经济高效地交付数据包的实时交互服务提供性能保障。在此背景下，目标是在最小化总体资源分配成本的同时，可靠地交付具有应用所施加严格截止期限的数据包。大量研究利用随机优化技术来设计在平均延迟约束下的高效动态路由和调度方案；然而，这些方法在面对严格的逐包延迟要求时表现不足。我们将最小成本延迟约束网络控制问题表述为约束马尔可夫决策过程，并利用约束深度强化学习（CDRL）技术来有效地最小化总资源分配成本，同时保持及时吞吐量高于目标可靠性水平。结果表明，所提出的基于CDRL的解决方案可以确保及时的数据包交付，即使在现有基线表现不佳时也能如此，并且与其它最大化吞吐量的方法相比，它可以实现更低的成本。

TLDR: This paper introduces a constrained deep reinforcement learning (CDRL) approach to minimize resource allocation costs while ensuring timely packet delivery in latency-sensitive networks, outperforming existing methods.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种约束深度强化学习（CDRL）方法，旨在最小化资源分配成本，同时确保延迟敏感网络中及时的数据包交付，并优于现有方法。

ROScopter: A Multirotor Autopilot based on ROSflight 2.0

Abstract (English): ROScopter is a lean multirotor autopilot built for researchers. ROScopter seeks to accelerate simulation and hardware testing of research code with an architecture that is both easy to understand and simple to modify. ROScopter is designed to interface with ROSflight 2.0 and runs entirely on an onboard flight computer, leveraging the features of ROS 2 to improve modularity. This work describes the architecture of ROScopter and how it can be used to test application code in both simulated and hardware environments. Hardware results of the default ROScopter behavior are presented, showing that ROScopter achieves similar performance to another state-of-the-art autopilot for basic waypoint-following maneuvers, but with a significantly reduced and more modular code-base.

摘要（中文）: ROScopter是一个专为研究人员设计的精简型多旋翼飞行器自动驾驶仪。ROScopter旨在通过易于理解和易于修改的架构，加速研究代码的仿真和硬件测试。ROScopter设计为与ROSflight 2.0接口，并完全在板载飞行计算机上运行，利用ROS 2的特性来提高模块化程度。本文介绍了ROScopter的架构，以及如何在仿真和硬件环境中测试应用程序代码。展示了默认ROScopter行为的硬件结果，表明ROScopter在基本的航点跟踪机动中，实现了与另一种最先进的自动驾驶仪类似的性能，但代码库显著减少且更模块化。

TLDR: ROScopter is a modular and lightweight autopilot built on ROSflight 2.0, designed to accelerate research in multirotor control by providing an easily modifiable and understandable codebase. It demonstrates comparable performance to existing autopilots with a simpler architecture.

简要说明: ROScopter是一个基于ROSflight 2.0的模块化且轻量级的自动驾驶仪，旨在通过提供一个易于修改和理解的代码库来加速多旋翼飞行器控制领域的研究。它证明了在更简单的架构下可与现有的自动驾驶仪相媲美的性能。

Authors: Jacob Moore, Ian Reid, Phil Tokumaru, Tim McLain

CT-Enabled Patient-Specific Simulation and Contact-Aware Robotic Planning for Cochlear Implantation

Abstract (English): Robotic cochlear-implant (CI) insertion requires precise prediction and regulation of contact forces to minimize intracochlear trauma and prevent failure modes such as locking and buckling. Aligned with the integration of advanced medical imaging and robotics for autonomous, precision interventions, this paper presents a unified CT-to-simulation pipeline for contact-aware insertion planning and validation. We develop a low-dimensional, differentiable Cosserat-rod model of the electrode array coupled with frictional contact and pseudo-dynamics regularization to ensure continuous stick-slip transitions. Patient-specific cochlear anatomy is reconstructed from CT imaging and encoded via an analytic parametrization of the scala-tympani lumen, enabling efficient and differentiable contact queries through closest-point projection. Based on a differentiated equilibrium-constraint formulation, we derive an online direction-update law under an RCM-like constraint that suppresses lateral insertion forces while maintaining axial advancement. Simulations and benchtop experiments validate deformation and force trends, demonstrating reduced locking/buckling risk and improved insertion depth. The study highlights how CT-based imaging enhances modeling, planning, and safety capabilities in robot-assisted inner-ear procedures.

摘要（中文）: 机器人人工耳蜗植入需要精确预测和调节接触力，以最大程度地减少耳蜗内创伤，并防止诸如锁定和屈曲等失效模式。为了与将先进医学影像和机器人技术结合应用于自主、精准干预相一致，本文提出了一种统一的CT到模拟的流程，用于接触感知的植入规划和验证。我们开发了一个低维、可微的Cosserat杆模型，该模型与电极阵列耦合，并结合了摩擦接触和伪动力学正则化，以确保连续的黏滑过渡。从CT影像中重建患者特异性的耳蜗解剖结构，并通过鼓阶腔的解析参数化进行编码，从而通过最近点投影实现高效且可微的接触查询。基于微分平衡约束公式，我们推导出一个RCM类约束下的在线方向更新律，该约束抑制了横向植入力，同时保持了轴向推进。仿真和台式实验验证了变形和力趋势，表明降低了锁定/屈曲风险并提高了植入深度。该研究强调了基于CT的成像如何增强机器人辅助内耳手术中的建模、规划和安全能力。

TLDR: This paper presents a CT-to-simulation pipeline for contact-aware robotic cochlear implantation, using a differentiable Cosserat-rod model and patient-specific CT data for improved insertion planning and safety.

Authors: Lingxiao Xun, Gang Zheng, Alexandre Kruszewski, Renato Torres

From Code to Road: A Vehicle-in-the-Loop and Digital Twin-Based Framework for Central Car Server Testing in Autonomous Driving

Abstract (English): Simulation is one of the most essential parts in the development stage of automotive software. However, purely virtual simulations often struggle to accurately capture all real-world factors due to limitations in modeling. To address this challenge, this work presents a test framework for automotive software on the centralized E/E architecture, which is a central car server in our case, based on Vehicle-in-the-Loop (ViL) and digital twin technology. The framework couples a physical test vehicle on a dynamometer test bench with its synchronized virtual counterpart in a simulation environment. Our approach provides a safe, reproducible, realistic, and cost-effective platform for validating autonomous driving algorithms with a centralized architecture. This test method eliminates the need to test individual physical ECUs and their communication protocols separately. In contrast to traditional ViL methods, the proposed framework runs the full autonomous driving software directly on the vehicle hardware after the simulation process, eliminating flashing and intermediate layers while enabling seamless virtual-physical integration and accurately reflecting centralized E/E behavior. In addition, incorporating mixed testing in both simulated and physical environments reduces the need for full hardware integration during the early stages of automotive development. Experimental case studies demonstrate the effectiveness of the framework in different test scenarios. These findings highlight the potential to reduce development and integration efforts for testing autonomous driving pipelines in the future.

摘要（中文）: 仿真在汽车软件的开发阶段至关重要。然而，纯虚拟仿真由于建模的局限性，通常难以准确捕捉所有真实世界的因素。为了应对这一挑战，本文提出了一种基于车在环 (ViL) 和数字孪生技术的汽车软件测试框架，该软件运行于集中式电子电气 (E/E) 架构之上，在我们的案例中体现为一个中央车载服务器。该框架将置于测功机试验台上的物理测试车辆与其在仿真环境中同步的虚拟副本耦合。我们的方法为验证采用集中式架构的自动驾驶算法提供了一个安全、可复现、逼真且具有成本效益的平台。该测试方法无需单独测试各个物理 ECU 及其通信协议。与传统的 ViL 方法不同，所提出的框架在仿真过程之后直接在车辆硬件上运行完整的自动驾驶软件，消除了刷写和中间层，同时实现了无缝的虚实融合，并准确地反映了集中式 E/E 的行为。此外，在仿真和物理环境中引入混合测试，降低了在汽车开发早期阶段对完整硬件集成的需求。实验案例研究表明了该框架在不同测试场景中的有效性。这些发现突显了在未来减少自动驾驶流水线测试的开发和集成工作量的潜力。

TLDR: This paper presents a Vehicle-in-the-Loop and Digital Twin-based framework for testing autonomous driving software on a centralized car server, improving simulation realism and reducing development efforts.

Authors: Chengdong Wu, Sven Kirchner, Nils Purschke, Axel Torschmied, Norbert Kroth, Yinglei Song, André Schamschurko, Erik Leo Haß, Kuo-Yi Chao, Yi Zhang, Nenad Petrovic, Alois C. Knoll

Rethinking the Role of Collaborative Robots in Rehabilitation

Abstract (English): Current research on collaborative robots (cobots) in physical rehabilitation largely focuses on repeated motion training for people undergoing physical therapy (PuPT), even though these sessions include phases that could benefit from robotic collaboration and assistance. Meanwhile, access to physical therapy remains limited for people with disabilities and chronic illnesses. Cobots could support both PuPT and therapists, and improve access to therapy, yet their broader potential remains underexplored. We propose extending the scope of cobots by imagining their role in assisting therapists and PuPT before, during, and after a therapy session. We discuss how cobot assistance may lift access barriers by promoting ability-based therapy design and helping therapists manage their time and effort. Finally, we highlight challenges to realizing these roles, including advancing user-state understanding, ensuring safety, and integrating cobots into therapists' workflow. This view opens new research questions and opportunities to draw from the HRI community's advances in assistive robotics.

摘要（中文）: 目前，关于物理康复中协作机器人（cobot）的研究主要集中在针对接受物理治疗者（PuPT）的重复运动训练上，即使这些疗程包含一些可能受益于机器人协作和辅助的阶段。与此同时，残疾人和慢性病患者获得物理治疗的机会仍然有限。协作机器人可以同时支持接受物理治疗者和治疗师，并改善获得治疗的机会，但其更广泛的潜力仍未得到充分探索。我们提出通过设想协作机器人在治疗会话之前、期间和之后辅助治疗师和接受物理治疗者的作用，来扩展协作机器人的应用范围。我们讨论了协作机器人辅助如何通过促进基于能力的治疗设计，以及帮助治疗师管理时间和精力来消除获取障碍。最后，我们强调了实现这些角色所面临的挑战，包括提升用户状态理解、确保安全性，以及将协作机器人集成到治疗师的工作流程中。这种观点开启了新的研究问题和机遇，可以借鉴人机交互（HRI）社区在辅助机器人方面的进展。

TLDR: This paper proposes broadening the role of collaborative robots in physical rehabilitation beyond repetitive motion training to include assisting therapists and patients before, during, and after therapy sessions, with the aim of improving access and efficiency. It identifies key challenges and opportunities for HRI research.

Authors: Vivek Gupte, Shalutha Rajapakshe, Emmanuel Senft

VinePT-Map: Pole-Trunk Semantic Mapping for Resilient Autonomous Robotics in Vineyards

Abstract (English): Reliable long-term deployment of autonomous robots in agricultural environments remains challenging due to perceptual aliasing, seasonal variability, and the dynamic nature of crop canopies. Vineyards, characterized by repetitive row structures and significant visual changes across phenological stages, represent a pivotal field challenge, limiting the robustness of conventional feature-based localization and mapping approaches. This paper introduces VinePT-Map, a semantic mapping framework that leverages vine trunks and support poles as persistent structural landmarks to enable season-agnostic and resilient robot localization. The proposed method formulates the mapping problem as a factor graph, integrating GPS, IMU, and RGB-D observations through robust geometrical constraints that exploit vineyard structure. An efficient perception pipeline based on instance segmentation and tracking, combined with a clustering filter for outlier rejection and pose refinement, enables accurate landmark detection using low-cost sensors and onboard computation. To validate the pipeline, we present a multi-season dataset for trunk and pole segmentation and tracking. Extensive field experiments conducted across diverse seasons demonstrate the robustness and accuracy of the proposed approach, highlighting its suitability for long-term autonomous operation in agricultural environments.

摘要（中文）: 由于感知混淆、季节性变化以及作物树冠的动态特性，自主机器人在农业环境中可靠的长期部署仍然面临挑战。葡萄园以重复的行结构和跨物候期的显著视觉变化为特征，代表着一个关键的领域挑战，限制了传统基于特征的定位和建图方法的鲁棒性。本文提出 VinePT-Map，一种语义建图框架，该框架利用葡萄树干和支撑杆作为持久的结构地标，以实现与季节无关且具有弹性的机器人定位。所提出的方法将建图问题公式化为一个因子图，通过利用葡萄园结构的鲁棒几何约束，整合GPS、IMU和RGB-D观测。一个基于实例分割和跟踪的高效感知流水线，结合用于异常值剔除和姿态优化的聚类滤波器，使用低成本传感器和板载计算实现精确的地标检测。为了验证该流水线，我们提出了一个用于树干和杆分割及跟踪的多季节数据集。在不同季节进行的广泛田间实验证明了所提出方法的鲁棒性和准确性，突出了其在农业环境中长期自主运行的适用性。

TLDR: The paper introduces VinePT-Map, a semantic mapping framework using persistent landmarks (vine trunks and poles) for resilient robot localization in vineyards, demonstrated with a multi-season dataset and field experiments.

Authors: Giorgio Audrito, Mauro Martini, Alessandro Navone, Giorgia Galluzzo, Marcello Chiaberge

Person Detection and Tracking from an Overhead Crane LiDAR

Abstract (English): This paper investigates person detection and tracking in an industrial indoor workspace using a LiDAR mounted on an overhead crane. The overhead viewpoint introduces a strong domain shift from common vehicle-centric LiDAR benchmarks, and limited availability of suitable public training data. Henceforth, we curate a site-specific overhead LiDAR dataset with 3D human bounding-box annotations and adapt selected candidate 3D detectors under a unified training and evaluation protocol. We further integrate lightweight tracking-by-detection using AB3DMOT and SimpleTrack to maintain person identities over time. Detection performance is reported with distance-sliced evaluation to quantify the practical operating envelope of the sensing setup. The best adapted detector configurations achieve average precision (AP) up to 0.84 within a 5.0 m horizontal radius, increasing to 0.97 at 1.0 m, with VoxelNeXt and SECOND emerging as the most reliable backbones across this range. The acquired results contribute in bridging the domain gap between standard driving datasets and overhead sensing for person detection and tracking. We also report latency measurements, highlighting practical real-time feasibility. Finally, we release our dataset and implementations in GitHub to support further research

摘要（中文）: 本文研究了使用安装在桥式起重机上的激光雷达在工业室内工作空间中进行人员检测和跟踪的问题。俯视视角引入了与常见的车辆中心激光雷达基准的强烈领域偏移，并且合适的公开训练数据有限。因此，我们整理了一个特定地点的俯视激光雷达数据集，其中包含3D人体边界框注释，并在统一的训练和评估协议下调整了选定的候选3D检测器。我们进一步集成了使用AB3DMOT和SimpleTrack的轻量级检测跟踪（tracking-by-detection）方法，以保持随时间推移的人员身份。检测性能通过距离分片评估进行报告，以量化传感设置的实际工作范围。最佳调整的检测器配置在 5.0 米水平半径内可达到高达 0.84 的平均精度（AP），并在 1.0 米处提高到 0.97，其中 VoxelNeXt 和 SECOND 成为该范围内最可靠的主干网络。获得的结果有助于弥合标准驾驶数据集与用于人员检测和跟踪的俯视感知之间的领域差距。我们还报告了延迟测量结果，突出了实际的实时可行性。最后，我们在 GitHub 上发布我们的数据集和实现，以支持进一步的研究。

TLDR: This paper presents a new overhead LiDAR dataset for person detection and tracking in industrial environments, evaluates several 3D detectors, and releases the dataset and code, which may help bridge the gap between standard driving datasets and overhead sensing applications.

Authors: Nilusha Jayawickrama, Henrik Toikka, Risto Ojala

Integrated cooperative localization of heterogeneous measurement swarm: A unified data-driven method

Abstract (English): The cooperative localization (CL) problem in heterogeneous robotic systems with different measurement capabilities is investigated in this work. In practice, heterogeneous sensors lead to directed and sparse measurement topologies, whereas most existing CL approaches rely on multilateral localization with restrictive multi-neighbor geometric requirements. To overcome this limitation, we enable pairwise relative localization (RL) between neighboring robots using only mutual measurement and odometry information. A unified data-driven adaptive RL estimator is first developed to handle heterogeneous and unidirectional measurements. Based on the convergent RL estimates, a distributed pose-coupling CL strategy is then designed, which guarantees CL under a weakly connected directed measurement topology, representing the least restrictive condition among existing results. The proposed method is independent of specific control tasks and is validated through a formation control application and real-world experiments.

摘要（中文）: 本文研究了具有不同测量能力的异构机器人系统中的协同定位（CL）问题。 实际上，异构传感器会导致有向且稀疏的测量拓扑，而大多数现有的协同定位方法依赖于具有严格的多邻居几何要求的多边定位。 为了克服这一限制，我们仅使用相互测量和里程计信息来实现相邻机器人之间的成对相对定位（RL）。 首先，开发了一种统一的数据驱动自适应相对定位估计器，以处理异构和单向测量。 然后，基于收敛的相对定位估计，设计了一种分布式位姿耦合协同定位策略，该策略保证在弱连通的有向测量拓扑下进行协同定位，这代表了现有结果中最宽松的条件。 提出的方法与特定的控制任务无关，并通过编队控制应用和实际实验进行了验证。

TLDR: This paper presents a data-driven cooperative localization method for heterogeneous robotic swarms that addresses sparse and directed measurement topologies using pairwise relative localization and a distributed pose-coupling strategy, validated with formation control and real-world experiments.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种针对异构机器人集群的数据驱动协同定位方法。该方法通过成对相对定位和分布式姿态耦合策略来解决稀疏和定向的测量拓扑结构问题，并通过编队控制和实际实验进行了验证。

Authors: Kunrui Ze, Wei Wang, Guibin Sun, Jiaqi Yan, Kexin Liu, Jinhu Lü

Distributed State Estimation for Vision-Based Cooperative Slung Load Transportation in GPS-Denied Environments

Abstract (English): Transporting heavy or oversized slung loads using rotorcraft has traditionally relied on single-aircraft systems, which limits both payload capacity and control authority. Cooperative multilift using teams of rotorcraft offers a scalable and efficient alternative, especially for infrequent but challenging "long-tail" payloads without the need of building larger and larger rotorcraft. Most prior multilift research assumes GPS availability, uses centralized estimation architectures, or relies on controlled laboratory motion-capture setups. As a result, these methods lack robustness to sensor loss and are not viable in GPS-denied or operationally constrained environments. This paper addresses this limitation by presenting a distributed and decentralized payload state estimation framework for vision-based multilift operations. Using onboard monocular cameras, each UAV detects a fiducial marker on the payload and estimates its relative pose. These measurements are fused via a Distributed and Decentralized Extended Information Filter (DDEIF), enabling robust and scalable estimation that is resilient to individual sensor dropouts. This payload state estimate is then used for closed-loop trajectory tracking control. Monte Carlo simulation results in Gazebo show the effectiveness of the proposed approach, including the effect of communication loss during flight.

摘要（中文）: 使用旋翼飞行器运输重型或超大吊挂载荷传统上依赖于单机系统，这限制了有效载荷能力和控制权限。使用旋翼飞行器团队进行协同多举升提供了一个可扩展且高效的替代方案，特别是对于不常见但具有挑战性的“长尾”有效载荷，而无需建造越来越大的旋翼飞行器。大多数先前的多举升研究假设GPS可用，使用中心化估计架构，或依赖于受控的实验室运动捕捉设置。因此，这些方法缺乏对传感器丢失的鲁棒性，并且在GPS拒止或操作受限环境中不可行。本文通过提出一种用于基于视觉的多举升操作的分布式和去中心化载荷状态估计框架来解决这一局限性。利用机载单目相机，每个无人机检测载荷上的标志板并估计其相对姿态。这些测量通过分布式和去中心化扩展信息滤波器（DDEIF）进行融合，实现鲁棒且可扩展的估计，能够应对单个传感器掉线的情况。然后，该载荷状态估计用于闭环轨迹跟踪控制。在Gazebo中的蒙特卡洛仿真结果表明了所提出方法的有效性，包括飞行期间通信丢失的影响。

TLDR: This paper presents a distributed state estimation framework for vision-based cooperative slung load transportation using multiple UAVs in GPS-denied environments, employing onboard monocular cameras and a Distributed and Decentralized Extended Information Filter (DDEIF). The method demonstrates robustness to sensor and communication loss through Gazebo simulations.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于视觉的多无人机协同吊运的分布式状态估计框架，用于GPS受限环境。该框架利用机载单目相机和分布式去中心化扩展信息滤波器（DDEIF）进行估计，并通过Gazebo仿真展示了对传感器和通信丢失的鲁棒性。

Authors: Jack R. Pence, Jackson Fezell, Jack W. Langelaan, Junyi Geng

The Spatial and Temporal Resolution of Motor Intention in Multi-Target Prediction

Abstract (English): Reaching for grasping, and manipulating objects are essential motor functions in everyday life. Decoding human motor intentions is a central challenge for rehabilitation and assistive technologies. This study focuses on predicting intentions by inferring movement direction and target location from multichannel electromyography (EMG) signals, and investigating how spatially and temporally accurate such information can be detected relative to movement onset. We present a computational pipeline that combines data-driven temporal segmentation with classical and deep learning classifiers in order to analyse EMG data recorded during the planning, early execution, and target contact phases of a delayed reaching task. Early intention prediction enables devices to anticipate user actions, improving responsiveness and supporting active motor recovery in adaptive rehabilitation systems. Random Forest achieves $80\%$ accuracy and Convolutional Neural Network $75\%$ accuracy across $25$ spatial targets, each separated by $14^\circ$ azimuth/altitude. Furthermore, a systematic evaluation of EMG channels, feature sets, and temporal windows demonstrates that motor intention can be efficiently decoded even with drastically reduced data. This work sheds light on the temporal and spatial evolution of motor intention, paving the way for anticipatory control in adaptive rehabilitation systems and driving advancements in computational approaches to motor neuroscience.

摘要（中文）: 抓握、操控物体是日常生活中至关重要的运动功能。解码人类运动意图是康复和辅助技术面临的核心挑战。本研究着重于通过多通道肌电图(EMG)信号推断运动方向和目标位置来预测意图，并探究此类信息相对于运动起始点的时空精度如何被检测。我们提出了一个计算流程，它结合了数据驱动的时序分割与经典和深度学习分类器，从而分析在延迟抓取任务的计划、早期执行和目标接触阶段记录的EMG数据。 早期意图预测使设备能够预期用户行为，提高响应速度，并支持自适应康复系统中积极的运动恢复。随机森林在25个空间目标（每个目标相隔14°方位角/仰角）上实现了80%的准确率，卷积神经网络实现了75%的准确率。此外，对EMG通道、特征集和时间窗口的系统评估表明，即使在大幅减少数据的情况下，也能有效地解码运动意图。 这项工作阐明了运动意图的时空演变，为自适应康复系统中的预测性控制铺平了道路，并推动了运动神经科学计算方法的进步。

TLDR: This paper investigates the accuracy and timing of motor intention decoding from EMG signals during a reaching task, achieving reasonable accuracy in predicting target location using machine learning models. Authors: Marie Dominique Schmidt, Ioannis Iossifidis

Visual-Informed Speech Enhancement Using Attention-Based Beamforming

Abstract (English): Recent studies have demonstrated that incorporating auxiliary information, such as speaker voiceprint or visual cues, can substantially improve Speech Enhancement (SE) performance. However, single-channel methods often yield suboptimal results in low signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) conditions, when there is high reverberation, or in complex scenarios involving dynamic speakers, overlapping speech, or non-stationary noise. To address these issues, we propose a novel Visual-Informed Neural Beamforming Network (VI-NBFNet), which integrates microphone array signal processing and deep neural networks (DNNs) using multimodal input features. The proposed network leverages a pretrained visual speech recognition model to extract lip movements as input features, which serve for voice activity detection (VAD) and target speaker identification. The system is intended to handle both static and moving speakers by introducing a supervised end-to-end beamforming framework equipped with an attention mechanism. The experimental results demonstrated that the proposed audiovisual system has achieved better SE performance and robustness for both stationary and dynamic speaker scenarios, compared to several baseline methods.

摘要（中文）: 近期研究表明，整合辅助信息，例如说话人声纹或视觉线索，能够显著提升语音增强(SE)性能。然而，单通道方法在低信噪比(SNR)条件、高混响环境或涉及动态说话人、重叠语音或非平稳噪声的复杂场景中，通常产生次优结果。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了一种新颖的视觉信息神经波束成形网络(VI-NBFNet)，该网络利用多模态输入特征，整合了麦克风阵列信号处理和深度神经网络(DNN)。所提出的网络利用预训练的视觉语音识别模型来提取唇动作为输入特征，用于语音活动检测(VAD)和目标说话人识别。该系统旨在通过引入配备注意力机制的监督端到端波束成形框架来处理静态和移动的说话人。实验结果表明，与几种基线方法相比，所提出的视听系统在静态和动态说话人场景中均实现了更好的语音增强性能和鲁棒性。

TLDR: The paper introduces a Visual-Informed Neural Beamforming Network (VI-NBFNet) for speech enhancement that uses lip movements to improve performance in challenging acoustic environments, especially with dynamic speakers.

Authors: Chihyun Liu, Jiaxuan Fan, Mingtung Sun, Michael Anthony, Mingsian R. Bai, Yu Tsao

Not All Trust is the Same: Effects of Decision Workflow and Explanations in Human-AI Decision Making

Abstract (English): A central challenge in AI-assisted decision making is achieving warranted, well-calibrated trust. Both overtrust (accepting incorrect AI recommendations) and undertrust (rejecting correct advice) should be prevented. Prior studies differ in the design of the decision workflow - whether users see the AI suggestion immediately (1-step setup) or have to submit a first decision beforehand (2-step setup) -, and in how trust is measured - through self-reports or as behavioral trust, that is, reliance. We examined the effects and interactions of (a) the type of decision workflow, (b) the presence of explanations, and (c) users' domain knowledge and prior AI experience. We compared reported trust, reliance (agreement rate and switch rate), and overreliance. Results showed no evidence that a 2-step setup reduces overreliance. The decision workflow also did not directly affect self-reported trust, but there was a crossover interaction effect with domain knowledge and explanations, suggesting that the effects of explanations alone may not generalize across workflow setups. Finally, our findings confirm that reported trust and reliance behavior are distinct constructs that should be evaluated separately in AI-assisted decision making.

摘要（中文）: 人工智能辅助决策的核心挑战是实现有保证的、良好校准的信任。应当避免过度信任（接受不正确的AI建议）和不信任（拒绝正确的建议）。以往的研究在决策流程的设计上有所不同——即用户是立即看到AI建议（一步设置）还是需要事先提交一个初步决策（两步设置）——以及信任的衡量方式上有所不同——通过自我报告或作为行为信任，即依赖度。我们研究了（a）决策流程类型、（b）解释的存在、（c）用户的领域知识和先前的AI经验的影响和交互作用。我们比较了报告的信任度、依赖度（一致率和转换率）以及过度依赖。结果表明，没有证据表明两步设置能减少过度依赖。决策流程也没有直接影响自我报告的信任度，但与领域知识和解释之间存在交叉交互效应，表明解释的单独作用可能无法推广到不同的流程设置中。最后，我们的研究结果证实，在人工智能辅助决策中，报告的信任度和依赖行为是不同的结构，应该分别进行评估。

TLDR: This paper investigates how different decision workflows and explanations affect trust and reliance in human-AI decision-making, highlighting the distinct nature of reported trust versus reliance behavior.

简要说明: 本文研究了不同决策流程和解释如何影响人机决策中的信任和依赖，强调了报告的信任与依赖行为的本质区别。

Authors: Laura Spillner, Rachel Ringe, Robert Porzel, Rainer Malaka

A 360-degree Multi-camera System for Blue Emergency Light Detection Using Color Attention RT-DETR and the ABLDataset

Abstract (English): This study presents an advanced system for detecting blue lights on emergency vehicles, developed using ABLDataset, a curated dataset that includes images of European emergency vehicles under various climatic and geographic conditions. The system employs a configuration of four fisheye cameras, each with a 180-degree horizontal field of view, mounted on the sides of the vehicle. A calibration process enables the azimuthal localization of the detections. Additionally, a comparative analysis of major deep neural network algorithms was conducted, including YOLO (v5, v8, and v10), RetinaNet, Faster R-CNN, and RT-DETR. RT-DETR was selected as the base model and enhanced through the incorporation of a color attention block, achieving an accuracy of 94.7 percent and a recall of 94.1 percent on the test set, with field test detections reaching up to 70 meters. Furthermore, the system estimates the approach angle of the emergency vehicle relative to the center of the car using geometric transformations. Designed for integration into a multimodal system that combines visual and acoustic data, this system has demonstrated high efficiency, offering a promising approach to enhancing Advanced Driver Assistance Systems (ADAS) and road safety.

摘要（中文）: 本研究提出了一种先进的紧急车辆蓝色警示灯检测系统，该系统基于 ABLDataset 开发，这是一个经过精心整理的数据集，包含欧洲紧急车辆在各种气候和地理条件下的图像。该系统采用了由四个鱼眼摄像头组成的配置，每个摄像头具有 180 度的水平视场角，安装在车辆侧面。通过标定过程，实现了对检测结果的方位角定位。此外，还对主要的深度神经网络算法进行了比较分析，包括 YOLO (v5、v8 和 v10)、RetinaNet、Faster R-CNN 和 RT-DETR。选择 RT-DETR 作为基础模型，并通过整合颜色注意力模块进行了增强，在测试集上实现了 94.7% 的准确率和 94.1% 的召回率，现场测试检测距离可达 70 米。此外，该系统利用几何变换估计了紧急车辆相对于车辆中心的接近角。该系统的设计旨在集成到结合视觉和声学数据的多模态系统中，已展示出高效性，为增强高级驾驶辅助系统 (ADAS) 和道路安全提供了一种很有前景的方法。

TLDR: The paper presents a multi-camera system using a color-attention enhanced RT-DETR model for detecting blue emergency lights, achieving high accuracy and recall on a curated dataset and field tests. It aims to improve ADAS and road safety by integrating visual and acoustic data.

Authors: Francisco Vacalebri-Lloret, Lucas Banchero, Jose J. Lopez, Jose M. Mossi

S5-SHB Agent: Society 5.0 enabled Multi-model Agentic Blockchain Framework for Smart Home

Abstract (English): The smart home is a key application domain within the Society 5.0 vision for a human-centered society. As smart home ecosystems expand with heterogeneous IoT protocols, diverse devices, and evolving threats, autonomous systems must manage comfort, security, energy, and safety for residents. Such autonomous decision-making requires a trust anchor, making blockchain a preferred foundation for transparent and accountable smart home governance. However, realizing this vision requires blockchain-governed smart homes to simultaneously address adaptive consensus, intelligent multi-agent coordination, and resident-controlled governance aligned with the principles of Society 5.0. Existing frameworks rely solely on rigid smart contracts with fixed consensus protocols, employ at most a single AI model without multi-agent coordination, and offer no governance mechanism for residents to control automation behaviour. To address these limitations, this paper presents the Society 5.0-driven human-centered governance-enabled smart home blockchain agent (S5-SHB-Agent). The framework orchestrates ten specialized agents using interchangeable large language models to make decisions across the safety, security, comfort, energy, privacy, and health domains. An adaptive PoW blockchain adjusts mining difficulty based on transaction volume and emergency conditions, with digital signatures and Merkle tree anchoring to ensure tamper evident auditability. A four-tier governance model enables residents to control automation through tiered preferences from routine adjustments to immutable safety thresholds. Evaluation confirms that resident governance correctly separates adjustable comfort priorities from immutable safety thresholds across all tested configurations, while adaptive consensus commits emergency blocks.

摘要（中文）: 智能家居是人类社会5.0愿景中以人为本社会的一个关键应用领域。随着智能家居生态系统通过异构的物联网协议、多样化的设备以及不断演化的威胁扩展，自治系统必须管理居民的舒适度、安全性、能源和安全。这种自治决策需要一个信任根，使得区块链成为透明且可问责的智能家居治理的首选基础。然而，实现这一愿景需要区块链治理的智能家居同时解决自适应共识、智能多代理协同以及与人类社会5.0原则对齐的居民控制的治理。现有的框架仅依赖于具有固定共识协议的僵化智能合约，最多采用单个AI模型，而没有多代理协同，并且不提供居民控制自动化行为的治理机制。为了解决这些局限性，本文提出了一种由人类社会5.0驱动、以人为本的、支持治理的智能家居区块链代理（S5-SHB-Agent）。该框架编排了十个利用可互换的大型语言模型的专业代理，以便在安全、安保、舒适、能源、隐私和健康领域做出决策。一种自适应的工作量证明（PoW）区块链根据交易量和紧急情况调整挖矿难度，并采用数字签名和Merkle树锚定，以确保防篡改的可审计性。一个四层治理模型使居民能够通过从常规调整到不可变的安全性阈值等分层偏好来控制自动化。评估证实，在所有测试配置中，居民治理能够正确区分可调节的舒适度优先级和不可变的安全性阈值，而自适应共识能够提交紧急区块。

TLDR: The paper introduces S5-SHB-Agent, a blockchain-based multi-agent framework for smart homes that incorporates adaptive consensus, AI-driven agent coordination, and resident-controlled governance aligned with Society 5.0 principles.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了S5-SHB-Agent，一个基于区块链的智能家居多智能体框架，它结合了自适应共识、AI驱动的智能体协调和符合Society 5.0原则的居民控制治理。

Authors: Janani Rangila, Akila Siriweera, Incheon Paik, Keitaro Naruse, Isuru Jayanada, Vishmika Devindi

MOOSEnger -- a Domain-Specific AI Agent for the MOOSE Ecosystem

Abstract (English): MOOSEnger is a tool-enabled AI agent tailored to the Multiphysics Object-Oriented Simulation Environment (MOOSE). MOOSE cases are specified in HIT ".i" input files; the large object catalog and strict syntax make initial setup and debugging slow. MOOSEnger offers a conversational workflow that turns natural-language intent into runnable inputs by combining retrieval-augmented generation over curated docs/examples with deterministic, MOOSE-aware parsing, validation, and execution tools. A core-plus-domain architecture separates reusable agent infrastructure (configuration, registries, tool dispatch, retrieval services, persistence, and evaluation) from a MOOSE plugin that adds HIT-based parsing, syntax-preserving ingestion of input files, and domain-specific utilities for input repair and checking. An input precheck pipeline removes hidden formatting artifacts, fixes malformed HIT structure with a bounded grammar-constrained loop, and resolves invalid object types via similarity search over an application syntax registry. Inputs are then validated and optionally smoke-tested with the MOOSE runtime in the loop via an MCP-backed execution backend (with local fallback), translating solver diagnostics into iterative verify-and-correct updates. Built-in evaluation reports RAG metrics (faithfulness, relevancy, context precision/recall) and end-to-end success by actual execution. On a 125-prompt benchmark spanning diffusion, transient heat conduction, solid mechanics, porous flow, and incompressible Navier--Stokes, MOOSEnger achieves a 0.93 execution pass rate versus 0.08 for an LLM-only baseline.

摘要（中文）: MOOSEnger是一个工具使能的人工智能代理，专为多物理场面向对象模拟环境（MOOSE）量身定制。MOOSE案例在HIT ".i" 输入文件中指定；庞大的对象目录和严格的语法使得初始设置和调试过程缓慢。MOOSEnger提供了一种对话式工作流程，通过结合对精选文档/示例的检索增强生成以及确定性的、MOOSE感知的解析、验证和执行工具，将自然语言意图转化为可运行的输入。核心加领域架构将可重用的代理基础架构（配置、注册表、工具调度、检索服务、持久性和评估）与MOOSE插件分离，该插件增加了基于HIT的解析、输入文件的语法保留摄取以及用于输入修复和检查的特定于领域的实用程序。输入预检查管道消除隐藏的格式伪影，通过有界语法约束循环修复格式错误的HIT结构，并通过应用程序语法注册表上的相似性搜索来解决无效的对象类型。然后，通过MCP支持的执行后端（具有本地回退），在MOOSE运行时循环中验证输入并选择性地进行冒烟测试，将求解器诊断信息转换为迭代的验证和纠正更新。内置评估报告RAG指标（忠实性、相关性、上下文精确率/召回率）以及通过实际执行实现的端到端成功率。在一个涵盖扩散、瞬态热传导、固体力学、多孔介质流动和不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程的125个提示基准测试中，MOOSEnger达到了0.93的执行通过率，而仅使用LLM基线的执行通过率为0.08。

TLDR: MOOSEnger is an AI agent that uses retrieval-augmented generation, domain-specific parsing, and validation tools to convert natural language into executable MOOSE input files, significantly improving the success rate compared to LLMs alone.

Authors: Mengnan Li, Jason Miller, Zachary Prince, Alexander Lindsay, Cody Permann

From Offline to Periodic Adaptation for Pose-Based Shoplifting Detection in Real-world Retail Security

Abstract (English): Shoplifting is a growing operational and economic challenge for retailers, with incidents rising and losses increasing despite extensive video surveillance. Continuous human monitoring is infeasible, motivating automated, privacy-preserving, and resource-aware detection solutions. In this paper, we cast shoplifting detection as a pose-based, unsupervised video anomaly detection problem and introduce a periodic adaptation framework designed for on-site Internet of Things (IoT) deployment. Our approach enables edge devices in smart retail environments to adapt from streaming, unlabeled data, supporting scalable and low-latency anomaly detection across distributed camera networks. To support reproducibility, we introduce RetailS, a new large-scale real-world shoplifting dataset collected from a retail store under multi-day, multi-camera conditions, capturing unbiased shoplifting behavior in realistic IoT settings. For deployable operation, thresholds are selected using both F1 and H_PRS scores, the harmonic mean of precision, recall, and specificity, during data filtering and training. In periodic adaptation experiments, our framework consistently outperformed offline baselines on AUC-ROC and AUC-PR in 91.6% of evaluations, with each training update completing in under 30 minutes on edge-grade hardware, demonstrating the feasibility and reliability of our solution for IoT-enabled smart retail deployment.

摘要（中文）: 扒窃是零售商面临的一个日益严重的运营和经济挑战，尽管广泛应用了视频监控，但扒窃事件和损失仍在增加。持续的人工监控是不可行的，这促使人们寻求自动化、保护隐私且感知资源的检测解决方案。在本文中，我们将扒窃检测定义为一个基于姿态的、无监督的视频异常检测问题，并引入了一个为现场物联网（IoT）部署设计的周期性自适应框架。我们的方法支持智能零售环境中的边缘设备从流式、未标记数据中进行自适应学习，从而支持在分布式摄像头网络中实现可扩展且低延迟的异常检测。为了支持可复现性，我们引入了RetailS，这是一个新的大规模真实世界扒窃数据集，该数据集是在零售店内，在多天、多摄像头条件下收集的，记录了真实的物联网环境中无偏差的扒窃行为。为了可部署运行，在数据过滤和训练过程中，使用F1得分和H_PRS得分（精度、召回率和特异性的调和平均值）选择阈值。在周期性自适应实验中，我们的框架在91.6%的评估中，在AUC-ROC和AUC-PR指标上始终优于离线基线，且每次训练更新在边缘级硬件上均在30分钟内完成，证明了我们的解决方案对于物联网赋能的智能零售部署的可行性和可靠性。

Authors: Shanle Yao, Narges Rashvand, Armin Danesh Pazho, Hamed Tabkhi

A Dual-Helix Governance Approach Towards Reliable Agentic AI for WebGIS Development

Abstract (English): WebGIS development requires rigor, yet agentic AI frequently fails due to five large language model (LLM) limitations: context constraints, cross-session forgetting, stochasticity, instruction failure, and adaptation rigidity. We propose a dual-helix governance framework reframing these challenges as structural governance problems that model capacity alone cannot resolve. We implement the framework as a 3-track architecture (Knowledge, Behavior, Skills) that uses a knowledge graph substrate to stabilize execution by externalizing domain facts and enforcing executable protocols, complemented by a self-learning cycle for autonomous knowledge growth. Applying this to the FutureShorelines WebGIS tool, a governed agent refactored a 2,265-line monolithic codebase into modular ES6 components. Results demonstrated a 51\% reduction in cyclomatic complexity and a 7-point increase in maintainability index. A comparative experiment against a zero-shot LLM confirms that externalized governance, not just model capability, drives operational reliability in geospatial engineering. This approach is implemented in the open-source AgentLoom governance toolkit.

摘要（中文）: WebGIS开发需要严谨性，但自主AI（agentic AI）经常失败，原因在于五个大型语言模型(LLM)的局限性：上下文约束、跨会话遗忘、随机性、指令失败和适应刚性。我们提出了一种双螺旋治理框架，将这些挑战重新定义为结构性治理问题，而仅仅是模型能力无法解决这些问题。我们将该框架实现为一个三轨架构（知识、行为、技能），该架构使用知识图谱基底通过外化领域事实和强制执行可执行协议来稳定执行，并辅以自主知识增长的自学习循环。将其应用于FutureShorelines WebGIS工具，一个受治理的智能体将一个2265行代码的单体代码库重构为模块化的ES6组件。结果表明，循环复杂度降低了51％，可维护性指数提高了7点。与零样本LLM进行的一项对比实验证实，外化的治理而非仅仅是模型能力，驱动了地理空间工程中的运营可靠性。该方法已在开源的AgentLoom治理工具包中实现。

TLDR: The paper presents a dual-helix governance framework (AgentLoom) using knowledge graphs and self-learning to improve the reliability of agentic AI for WebGIS development, demonstrating improved code maintainability through refactoring a monolithic codebase.

Authors: Boyuan, Guan, Wencong Cui, Levente Juhasz

Fusion4CA: Boosting 3D Object Detection via Comprehensive Image Exploitation

Abstract (English): Nowadays, an increasing number of works fuse LiDAR and RGB data in the bird's-eye view (BEV) space for 3D object detection in autonomous driving systems. However, existing methods suffer from over-reliance on the LiDAR branch, with insufficient exploration of RGB information. To tackle this issue, we propose Fusion4CA, which is built upon the classic BEVFusion framework and dedicated to fully exploiting visual input with plug-and-play components. Specifically, a contrastive alignment module is designed to calibrate image features with 3D geometry, and a camera auxiliary branch is introduced to mine RGB information sufficiently during training. For further performance enhancement, we leverage an off-the-shelf cognitive adapter to make the most of pretrained image weights, and integrate a standard coordinate attention module into the fusion stage as a supplementary boost. Experiments on the nuScenes dataset demonstrate that our method achieves 69.7% mAP with only 6 training epochs and a mere 3.48% increase in inference parameters, yielding a 1.2% improvement over the baseline which is fully trained for 20 epochs. Extensive experiments in a simulated lunar environment further validate the effectiveness and generalization of our method. Our code will be released through Fusion4CA.

摘要（中文）: 如今，越来越多的工作将激光雷达和RGB数据融合在鸟瞰图 (BEV) 空间中，用于自动驾驶系统中的3D目标检测。然而，现有方法过度依赖激光雷达分支，对RGB信息的探索不足。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了Fusion4CA，它构建在经典的BEVFusion框架之上，并致力于通过即插即用组件充分利用视觉输入。具体来说，设计了一个对比对齐模块来校准图像特征与3D几何，并引入一个相机辅助分支，以在训练期间充分挖掘RGB信息。为了进一步提升性能，我们利用现成的认知适配器来充分利用预训练的图像权重，并将标准的坐标注意力模块集成到融合阶段，作为补充增强。在nuScenes数据集上的实验表明，我们的方法仅用6个训练周期和仅3.48%的推理参数增量就实现了69.7%的mAP，相比完整训练20个周期的基线提高了1.2%。在模拟月球环境中的大量实验进一步验证了我们方法的有效性和泛化性。我们的代码将通过Fusion4CA发布。

TLDR: The paper proposes Fusion4CA, a method to improve 3D object detection by better utilizing RGB information in LiDAR-RGB fusion, achieving improved mAP on the nuScenes dataset with minimal increase in parameters and training epochs.

Authors: Kang Luo, Xin Chen, Yangyi Xiao, Hesheng Wang

MoRe: Motion-aware Feed-forward 4D Reconstruction Transformer

Abstract (English): Reconstructing dynamic 4D scenes remains challenging due to the presence of moving objects that corrupt camera pose estimation. Existing optimization methods alleviate this issue with additional supervision, but they are mostly computationally expensive and impractical in real-time applications. To address these limitations, we propose MoRe, a feedforward 4D reconstruction network that efficiently recovers dynamic 3D scenes from monocular videos. Built upon a strong static reconstruction backbone, MoRe employs an attention-forcing strategy to disentangle dynamic motion from static structure. To further enhance robustness, we fine-tune the model on large-scale, diverse datasets encompassing both dynamic and static scenes. Moreover, our grouped causal attention captures temporal dependencies and adapts to varying token lengths across frames, ensuring temporally coherent geometry reconstruction. Extensive experiments on multiple benchmarks demonstrate that MoRe achieves high-quality dynamic reconstructions with exceptional efficiency.

摘要（中文）: 由于运动物体的存在会干扰相机位姿估计，重建动态4D场景仍然具有挑战性。现有的优化方法通过额外的监督来缓解这个问题，但它们大多计算成本高昂，在实时应用中不切实际。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出MoRe，一种前馈4D重建网络，可以有效地从单目视频中恢复动态3D场景。MoRe建立在强大的静态重建骨干网络之上，采用了一种注意力强制策略，将动态运动从静态结构中解耦。为了进一步增强鲁棒性，我们在包含动态和静态场景的大规模多样化数据集上对模型进行微调。此外，我们采用的分组因果注意力可以捕获时间依赖性，并适应跨帧变化的不同token长度，从而确保时间上连贯的几何重建。在多个基准测试上的大量实验表明，MoRe以卓越的效率实现了高质量的动态重建。

TLDR: The paper introduces MoRe, a feed-forward transformer network for efficient dynamic 4D scene reconstruction from monocular video, utilizing attention mechanisms to disentangle motion and structure.

Authors: Juntong Fang, Zequn Chen, Weiqi Zhang, Donglin Di, Xuancheng Zhang, Chengmin Yang, Yu-Shen Liu

MI-DETR: A Strong Baseline for Moving Infrared Small Target Detection with Bio-Inspired Motion Integration

Abstract (English): Infrared small target detection (ISTD) is challenging because tiny, low-contrast targets are easily obscured by complex and dynamic backgrounds. Conventional multi-frame approaches typically learn motion implicitly through deep neural networks, often requiring additional motion supervision or explicit alignment modules. We propose Motion Integration DETR (MI-DETR), a bio-inspired dual-pathway detector that processes one infrared frame per time step while explicitly modeling motion. First, a retina-inspired cellular automaton (RCA) converts raw frame sequences into a motion map defined on the same pixel grid as the appearance image, enabling parvocellular-like appearance and magnocellular-like motion pathways to be supervised by a single set of bounding boxes without extra motion labels or alignment operations. Second, a Parvocellular-Magnocellular Interconnection (PMI) Block facilitates bidirectional feature interaction between the two pathways, providing a biologically motivated intermediate interconnection mechanism. Finally, a RT-DETR decoder operates on features from the two pathways to produce detection results. Surprisingly, our proposed simple yet effective approach yields strong performance on three commonly used ISTD benchmarks. MI-DETR achieves 70.3% mAP@50 and 72.7% F1 on IRDST-H (+26.35 mAP@50 over the best multi-frame baseline), 98.0% mAP@50 on DAUB-R, and 88.3% mAP@50 on ITSDT-15K, demonstrating the effectiveness of biologically inspired motion-appearance integration. Code is available at https://github.com/nliu-25/MI-DETR.

摘要（中文）: 红外小目标检测（ISTD）极具挑战性，因为微小、低对比度的目标很容易被复杂且动态的背景所掩盖。传统的基于多帧的方法通常通过深度神经网络隐式地学习运动，这通常需要额外的运动监督或显式的对齐模块。我们提出了一种运动集成DETR（MI-DETR），这是一种受生物启发的双通路检测器，它处理每个时间步的一帧红外图像，同时显式地建模运动。首先，一个受视网膜启发的细胞自动机（RCA）将原始帧序列转换为一个运动图，该运动图定义在与外观图像相同的像素网格上，使得类似于小细胞的（parvocellular-like）外观通路和类似于大细胞的（magnocellular-like）运动通路可以在没有额外运动标签或对齐操作的情况下，被同一组边界框监督。其次，一个小细胞-大细胞互连（PMI）块促进了这两个通路之间双向的特征交互，提供了一种受生物学启发的中间互连机制。最后，一个RT-DETR解码器对来自这两个通路的特征进行操作，从而产生检测结果。令人惊讶的是，我们提出的简单而有效的方法在三个常用的ISTD基准测试中产生了强大的性能。MI-DETR在IRDST-H上实现了70.3%的mAP@50和72.7%的F1（比最好的多帧基线高出+26.35 mAP@50），在DAUB-R上实现了98.0%的mAP@50，在ITSDT-15K上实现了88.3%的mAP@50，证明了受生物启发的外观-运动集成的有效性。代码可在https://github.com/nliu-25/MI-DETR获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces MI-DETR, a bio-inspired dual-pathway detector for infrared small target detection that explicitly models motion using a retina-inspired cellular automaton and demonstrates strong performance on standard benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了MI-DETR，一种受生物学启发的双通路红外小目标检测器，它使用视网膜启发的细胞自动机显式建模运动，并在标准基准测试中表现出强大的性能。

Authors: Nian Liu, Jin Gao, Shubo Lin, Yutong Kou, Sikui Zhang, Fudong Ge, Zhiqiang Pu, Liang Li, Gang Wang, Yizheng Wang, Weiming Hu

MultiGO++: Monocular 3D Clothed Human Reconstruction via Geometry-Texture Collaboration

Abstract (English): Monocular 3D clothed human reconstruction aims to generate a complete and realistic textured 3D avatar from a single image. Existing methods are commonly trained under multi-view supervision with annotated geometric priors, and during inference, these priors are estimated by the pre-trained network from the monocular input. These methods are constrained by three key limitations: texturally by unavailability of training data, geometrically by inaccurate external priors, and systematically by biased single-modality supervision, all leading to suboptimal reconstruction. To address these issues, we propose a novel reconstruction framework, named MultiGO++, which achieves effective systematic geometry-texture collaboration. It consists of three core parts: (1) A multi-source texture synthesis strategy that constructs 15,000+ 3D textured human scans to improve the performance on texture quality estimation in challenge scenarios; (2) A region-aware shape extraction module that extracts and interacts features of each body region to obtain geometry information and a Fourier geometry encoder that mitigates the modality gap to achieve effective geometry learning; (3) A dual reconstruction U-Net that leverages geometry-texture collaborative features to refine and generate high-fidelity textured 3D human meshes. Extensive experiments on two benchmarks and many in-the-wild cases show the superiority of our method over state-of-the-art approaches.

摘要（中文）: 单目3D服装人体重建旨在从单张图像生成完整且逼真的纹理化3D化身。现有方法通常在带有标注几何先验的多视角监督下进行训练，并且在推理过程中，这些先验由预训练网络从单目输入中估计。这些方法受到三个关键因素的限制：在纹理上受限于训练数据的不可用性，在几何上受限于不准确的外部先验，以及在系统上受限于有偏差的单模态监督，所有这些都导致次优的重建效果。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了一种新颖的重建框架，名为MultiGO++，它实现了有效的系统性几何-纹理协作。它由三个核心部分组成：（1）一种多源纹理合成策略，构建了15000+个3D纹理化人体扫描，以提高在挑战场景中纹理质量估计的性能；（2）一个区域感知形状提取模块，提取并交互每个身体区域的特征以获得几何信息，以及一个傅里叶几何编码器，用于缓解模态差距以实现有效的几何学习；（3）一个双重重建U-Net，利用几何-纹理协作特征来细化和生成高保真度的纹理化3D人体网格。在两个基准数据集和许多真实场景下的广泛实验表明，我们的方法优于最先进的方法。

TLDR: The paper presents MultiGO++, a novel framework for monocular 3D clothed human reconstruction that addresses limitations in texture quality, geometric accuracy, and single-modality supervision through geometry-texture collaboration.

简要说明: 该论文提出了MultiGO++，一种用于单目3D服装人体重建的新框架，通过几何-纹理协作解决纹理质量、几何精度和单模态监督方面的局限性。
